O vos, tres chiers filz, je vos ai acomplit cest livre qui est li derriens de la science de medicine ensamble l’emplissement de lui, et ai fait la fin per ses expositions et par ses declarations.	O you, dear children, I have completed this book which is the last of the medical science volume, and have made it whole through its explanations and declarations.
Et m’est venu en vision que je le vos acomplisse avec cest traitier, qui est partie de l’uevre de mains, c’est a savoir «cyrurgie».	And to me has come in vision that I shall complete it with this treatise, which is part of the work of hands - namely, "Surgery."
Et por ceu que l’uevre de mains est fortraite en nostre region et est etraingie dou tout en tout, si est perie li science et decopee, et n’est riens demorez de li fuers que les petites descriptions en livres des anciens que les mains ont muees.	And because the work of hands is taught in our region and practiced entirely, it has been overshadowed by science and knowledge, with only minor details remaining from ancient texts that describe actions performed on limbs.
Et de ceu est venue li error et li vanitez, et sont closes les ententions et est aloignie li science.	And thus comes about the error and folly, closing off understanding and separating knowledge.
Or me semble que je la vuel vivifier ensamble l’ordination de cest traitier selonc la voie d’exposition et de declaration et de l’abreviation;	 Or it seems to me that I will revive them together with the direction of this treatise according to the way of exposure and explanation and abbreviation.
et venrai ensamble les formes des ferremens de cautere, et des autres estrumens de l’uevre avec l’ajostement de la declaration et de preparation de li, sicom il est mestier.	 And I will come together with the forms of cauldrons and other tools of surgery, along with the arrangement for explanation and preparation as needed.
Et por la raison de ceu que nuls boins maistres de mains n’est trovez en nostre tens, est li ars de medicine eslongié.	And because no good masters of hands are to be found in our time, the art of medicine has been abandoned.
Et covient celui qui s’en entremet sormonter en la science d’anathomie, si com Galiens dit, tant qu’il saiche la juement des menbres, et les formes et les conjunctions et les separations d’aus, et aient connissance des osses et des nerf et des brais et le nombre d’ous, et le demenement et des voines movans et des reposans, et dou leu de lor issue.	to tc;s s ...
Et por ceu dist Ypocras que li nons avec le non est mout, et avec l’uevre est poc;	 And so Hippocrates says that without it there is not much, and with surgery there is little;
et meismement en l’art de main.	 Also particularly in the art of hands.
Nos vos disons en l’introite de cest livre que qui n’est conissans des choses devant dites, si se gart qu’il ne chiece en error et qu’il n’ocie les homes;	 We tell you at the beginning of this book that those who are not acquainted with the aforementioned things must be careful so as to not err and kill people.
ensi que j’ai veut maintes fois plusors de ces qui s’entremettent de ceste science et si s’abandonent sen science et sens experiment.	 So I have seen many times how some who engage in this science abandon themselves to theory and lack experience.
Car je vis un fol mire qui copa I apostume de scrophules ou col d’une femme, et copa les arteres dou col;	 For I have seen a crazy barber who cut an abscess of hard swellings or neck of a woman, and severed the arteries at the neck.
por coi tant de sanc issit hors que li femme cheit morte entre ses mains.	 Because so much blood came out that the woman died in his hands.
Et vis I autre mire qui traït une piere d’un home d’eaige, et li piere estoit grans;	 And I saw another barber who treated a stone of a man's eye, and the stone was large;
si emporta avec li une piece de la vessie, et fut mors li hons dedens III jors.	 thus it took away with him a piece of the bladder, and within three days the man died.
Et je i avoie ja esteit apelez por lou traire, et vis la disposition dou malaide et la grandor de la piere, et soi bien s’on lou tailloit il en morroit.	And I have already been called to treat him, and I saw the patient's condition and the severity of the wound, and if it were not for treating it, he would surely die.
Et vis I autre mire qui prist en cure I duc de nostre terre qui avoit la jambe brisie, et avec la briseure ot plaie;	 And I saw another barber who took in care our duke who had a broken leg, and with the fracture there was an injury.
et li mires plains d’ignorance estraint la brisure sus la plaie as esteles par fort lieure, et ne lassa a la plaie point de xalain, et le lassa ensi I termine;	 and the ignorant barber pulled out the fracture near to the wound with great force, did not allow any bandage on the wound, and left it like this for so long.
et li comanda qu’il ne la desliast mie;	 And he commands that it not be dislocated again;
et demora ensi que li jambe fut toute enflee et li piez et vint a perdition.	 and remains so, causing the leg to become completely swollen and the foot leading to destruction.
Je fuis apelez por venir a lui, et me hastai por venir deslier la jambe;	 I am summoned to come to him, and have been hurriedly dislocated from his leg;
et quant je l’oi desloie si fut em pais et ne sentit point de dolor.	 and when it is dislocated again, he feels no pain at all.
Mais toute voie li corruptions estoit ja confermee ou membre, et ne la poi saner;	 But in any case, the contamination had already set in or limb, and could not be cured;
et ne cessa li corrution d’aler par le membre tant que li membres fut dou tout perdus.	 and the corruption did not stop spreading through the member until the whole limb was completely lost.
Et vis .i. autre mire qui effondra .i. apostume enchancreit, et puis enflama per le malice de sa signorie.	And there was another physician who collapsed an abscess and it became infected, then inflamed due to the spite of its lordship.
Car chancre, quant il est purs d’umor melancolique, ne covient mie qu’on i(l) touche de fer s’il n’est en teil leu c’on puisse toute oster ce que est corrumpus.	and: the first.
Et por ceu, treschier filz, vos est besoig que vos sachiez que oevre de mains est devisee en II divisions:	 And therefore, dear sons, you must know that the work of hands is divided into two parts:
c’est asavoir, huevre ou il a peril en plusors dispositions;	 That is to say, where there is danger in various disorders;
et je mostrerai en chescun leu de cest livre ou il a paour et peril.	 And I will show in each part of this book where there is fear and danger.
Por coi il est besoig que vos vos en gardez, si que li fol mire ne puissent mal parler de vos.	 Therefore, you must be vigilant so that the foolish may not speak ill of you.
Si prenez vos armes en cusenson, et entreprenez vos malaides legierement et fermement, et usez de la millor voie si que per la graice de Deu vos venez a salut et soiez loez;	 If you take up your weapons in consideration and undertake your maladies lightly yet firmly, and follow the best course with God's grace to attain salvation and be praised.
et lassiez les maladies espoantables de grief saniteit;	 and let go of hopeful diseases causing great suffering in health.
et ostez vos armes de ceu que vos fait douter, et aiez foit en vos si que vos puissiez venir de cestui monde a l’autre de gloire.	 And arm yourselves with this so that you may not doubt, and be ready in such a way that you can come from this world to the other of glory.
Galiens dist en aucuns de ses amonestemens:	 Galien states in some of his admonitions:
«Ne prenez mie en cure male maladie, que vos ne soiez apelez fol mire.	 "Do not take careless illnesses into treatment, lest you be called mad master.
» J’ai deviseit cest traitier selonc III chapitres.	 "I have devised this treaty according to three chapters.
Li premiers chapitres est des cauteres de feu et dé cauteres de medicine ague, et est li chapitres ordenez de lou chief jusques as piez;	 The first chapters are of fire cautery and medicinal cupping, and the chapters are ordered from the head to the feet.
et des formes des estrumens, et des ferremens de cautere, et de tout ceu qui est necessaire en l’ueuvre.	 And of exudations, and iron cauteries, and all that is necessary in work.
Li secons chapitres si est de taillier et de percier, et des ventouses et des plaies, et des estractions des saiettes, et des semblans choses;	 The second chapter is of cutting and piercing, and cupping and wounds, and arrow extractions, and such like things.
et est li chapitres ordenez et les formes des estrumens.	 And it is about ordered chapters and forms of inflammations.
Li tiers chapitres est de restorer les dislocations et des torcions, et des semblans choses;	 The third chapter is about correcting dislocations and sprains, and similar things;
et est ordeneiz des lou chief jusc’as piez, et des formes des estrumens.	 And it is organized up to the head, and forms of inflammations.
Ainsois que nos nos remembriens de l’uevre, il covient que je die la qualiteit de l’aide et dou nuisement de chescune complexion.	So we remember this work, it is necessary for me to describe the quality of aid and harm from each temperament.
Je dis que li qualiteis de l’aide, et dou nuisement, est li plus longe parole et subtilz science et li secrez reponus;	 I say that the quality of help, and harm done, is a longer speech and subtle art and secret remedies.
et de ceu parlerent li plusors des saiges, et s’acorderent a ceu;	 and about this spoke many wise men, and agreed on it.
et me soffisent poc lor paroles, car je redous la longesce.	 and I am not satisfied with their words because I repeat the lengthiness.
Je dis que cautere aide universement a toute complexion ou il a matiere, fuer que II complexions:	 I say that cautery helps everywhere for any constitution or matter it has, whether there are conditions:
c’est a savoir complexion chaude sens matere, et complexion seche sens matere.	 That is to say, hot temperament with moist matter, and dry temperament with dry matter.
En complexion chaude et seche ensamble matiere, deviserent aucun et dirent que cautere i est grans aide;	 In hot and dry constitutions combined with certain matters, some advise that fire cautery is greatly helpful.
et li autre dirent le contraire:	 And others said the opposite:
que cautere ne vaut a maladie que vient de chalor et de sechour.	 That fire cautery does not help diseases that come from heat and dryness.
Car li nature dou feu si est chaude, et ne doit mie estre cureiz de chaude maladie par chalor, ne per sechour;	 Because the nature of fire is hot, and it should not be used to treat hot diseases caused by heat or dryness.
et dist cil qui dist lou contraire que cautere fait grant aide a maladie chaude et seche que vient en cors des homes.	 And those who say the opposite believe that fire cautery provides great help for hot and dry diseases that occur in the bodies of men.
Car quant tu comperes le cors de l’ome et sa moistor a la complexion dou feu, tu trueves le cors froit.	When you examine the body of the person and their moisture to its constitution with heat, you find the body cold.
Et je m’acorde a ceste parole.	And I agree upon this statement.
Car je l’ai troveit aucune fois per experiment.	ouest douce la cuire the luist les plaies. Et quant tu ne soigné, et les tires in its froid gues-le chaude of heat it est curet is à chaud déguises de a le croix coupeur temps let: Car tu; and l’ai ou la partis d’est douce or li cuise au teste.
Et toute voie, ne s’en entremette mie fuers que cil qui l’a esproveit, et qui conoit par lonc usaige le chapistre des cauteres, et la diversiteit des complexions des homes, et les dispositions et les causes de lor maladies, et les sorvenues et l’espaice dou tens;	 And so, let no one meddle in it who has not tried and understood the art of cautery over a long period, and knows the different temperaments of people, their dispositions and causes of diseases, outcomes, and duration.
des autres complexions n’avons nos mie paour, meismement em maladies froides et moistes.	 We do not have fear of other conditions, particularly cold and damp diseases.
Et tuit li mire s’asemblerent et s’acorderent au cautere.	And all the physicians gathered and agreed on the use of cautery.
Et sachiez, filz, que cautere ensamble feu si est des secrez des cures, et de plus grant bonteit que cautere de medicine ardant.	And know this, my children, that fire-cautery is a secret of healing and more generous than caustic medicinal cautery.
Car li feus est simples, et ne vient mie fuers que au membre qui est cuis, et ne nuit a autre membre se poc nom.	The fire is simple, and does not come from force except to the limb that is cooked, and harms no other limb unless it has a name.
Les medicines ardans vienent de membre a autre en aloignant, et font venir au membre maladies de grief sanation;	 Ardent medications come from one member joining another, causing the affected limb to develop serious healing diseases;
et par aventure ocit lou malaide.	 And sometimes it kills the patient.
Li feus por sa hautece et por la bonteit de sa substance ne fait mie ceu, s’il n’i a superfluiteit.	 The heat due to its intensity and for the kindness of its nature does not occur without excess if there is no surplus.
Et ceu vos ai je troveit par experiment et par la longesce dou servise et de l’estude que j’ai mis en l’art, et esteit sus la verteit des choses;	 And this I have found through experiments and the long service and study that I have put into the art, and it is based on the truth of things;
et por ceu je m’escuse de la longesce de la parole, car il ne me plait mie que je vos oste le secreit qui est reponus ou feu, et la qualiteit de l’uevre, coment il deboute les maladies des cors, si com li philosophe le dit en demostrant;	 And because of the length of my words, I excuse myself so that I may reveal to you the secret hidden in fire and the quality of its workmanship on how it counteracts diseases of the body as the philosopher explains by demonstrating.
or le recevez en vos pensees.	 Or receive them in your thoughts.
Et sachiez, fil, que il s’acorderent en quel tens doient estre faites les cauteres, et eslirent prientens.	And know, son, that they are agreed upon when to be made the fire cauteries, and choosing prayers.
Et je dis que cautere est covenable en tous tens, por ceu que li nuisemens sorvenans est desoz mis par l’aide dou cautere;	 And I say that cauldration is appropriate at all times because the harm that occurs can be prevented by the aid of cauldration.
et meismement se li cauteres est por dolors necessaires fors et hastans que ne puent atendre le tens que plus grans malice ne veigne au membre.	 and especially when cauldrations are needed urgently and quickly, so that they cannot wait until a greater harm comes to the limb.
Et n’i pensez onques, chier fil, si com font li fol mire;	 And never think as fools do.
car a la maladie qui est sanee par cautere n’a point de revenue;	 because the disease that is treated by cauldration has no return.
et il le dient ensi;	 and it speaks thusly.
mais il n’est mie si com il cuident, por ce que cauteres nen est que medicine qui mue la complexion, et seche les humors que sont cause de la dolor, et vaut mues que medicine por le hastement de sa valor, et por la vertut de son oevre et de sa signorie.	 but it is not as they claim because cauldration is a medicine that changes the temperament and dries up the humors causing pain; its value lies in moving quickly and in the virtue of its work and dominion.
Et possans chose est que li maladie viegne aucune fois selonc la complexion dou malaide et lou leu de la maladie et sa vertut;	 And it is possible that illness comes at any time according to the constitution of the individual and the nature and virtue of the disease.
et sont assemblees en lui les superfluitez par l’aquisition des viandes et des semblans choses, se ce n’est cauteres administrez em leu ou il ait poc de superfluitez et de moistor, si com cauteres de dens por la dolor, et les semblans choses, et teil dolor ne revient mie;	 And they are accumulated in him due to the consumption of meats and such things, unless there have been caustics administered on site where there is little excess and moisture, as with cauterizations for pain, and similar matters, so that no great pain returns.
mais ce avient poc.	 But this happens rarely.
Et mout de gens n’entendent mie por coi cauteres est apelez li derriens de medecine, et c’est voir;	 And many people do not understand why caustics are called the last of medicine, and that is true.
mais il ne croient mie que cauteres vaille aprés medicine, mais lor ententions est fause, et est cauteres li derriens de medicine por ceu que quant nos aministrons manieres de cures en aucune maladie et elles ne valent, adonc administrons nos le cautere, et il vaut.	 But they do not believe that caustics are worth more than medicine, but their understanding is false; caustics are the last of medicine because when we administer treatments for any illness and they are ineffective, then we apply our caustics, which work.
Adonques apert bien que cauteres est li derriens de medicine, ne mie selonc l’entention des folz mires.	Then indeed, fire cautery is the last of medicines, not according to the misguided beliefs of fools.
Li ancien dirent que cauteres d’estrument d’or est muedres que de fer, et ne dirent ceu fuers que por la qualiteit de l’or et por la hautece de sa substance;	 The ancients said that cauterization with a tool of gold is more effective than iron, and they did not consider copper because of the quality of gold and the high value of its substance.
et dirent que li leus de cautere ne fait mie porriture, mais ceu n’est mie voir car je l’ai esprovei, et ai troveit que c’est voir en aucuns homes;	 And they said that the application of cauterization does not cause itching, but this is not true as I have tested and found that it happens in some individuals.
et cauteres d’or vaut mues que de fer, si com il lou dirent.	 and gold tools are more valuable than iron ones, just as they claimed.
Et toutevoie quant tu chaufes estrument d’or, tu ne seis mie quant il est chaus par la color de l’or, et s’est tantost refroidiez;	 And nevertheless, when you heat the instrument made of gold, it is not because of the color of the gold, and cools down quickly.
et s’on le chaufe trop;	 and if heated too much;
si font au feu;	 If done with fire;
et ensi i a assez d’empechement.	 And thus there is sufficient hindrance.
Et por ce usons nos de cautere de feir que nos l’avons mues apparilliet a nostre oevre.	And so we employ fire cautery, which we have prepared for our work.
Or vos ai ordeneit cest chapitre des lou chief jusc’a piez, por ceu que li voie soit plus legiere a trover.	And I have ordered this chapter from the main points up until now so that the journey may be easier to find.
dou cautere olivaire	Olive oil is often used in medieval medical treatments for its supposed healing properties, though it should be noted that many of these beliefs were not based on our modern understanding of medicine and science. It was sometimes applied externally as a salve or ointment to wounds or afflictions such as skin conditions, believed to have soothing effects due to the oil's moisturizing properties.
Cist cauteres vaut a moistor et a froidor sus lou cerveil, et en i a dous c’on fait par la cause d’une maladie qui est apelee «soda», et par la cause de maintes humors qui dessendent dou chief as eulz, et as oreilles, et por multitude de songes et dolor de dens et dolor de gorge, et meismement a toutes maladies qui vienent de froidor si com paralisie et sode et apoplexie et semblans maladies.	These fire cauteries are effective for moisture and cold on the brain, and among them there is a sweet way to treat an illness called 'soda,' as well as due to various humors descending into the ears, and causing numerous dreams and toothache pain, throat pain, and primarily for all diseases caused by cold such as paralysis, apoplexy, and similar afflictions.
Li forme de cest cautere si est que li malaides soit espurgiez par medicine solutive mondifiant le chief III nuis ou IIII, selonc ceu que li vertus et li eaige et li acostumance dou malaide le puet soffrir;	 The form of this cautery is that the patient should be purged by a solutive medicine altering the chief III or IV, depending on what its virtues and effects and the condition of the ill person can tolerate.
et puis fai rere lou chief dou malaide.	 And then raise the head of the sick person.
Et puis le fai seoir croisiet entre tes mains, et mettre ses mains sor som peis;	 Then make them sit with their crossed hands and place their hands under some small stones.
aprés met la racine de ta palme sus la racine de son neis entre ses II eulz;	 After that, put the root of your palm over the root of his nose between his two eyes;
et lai ou venra tes dois moiens, si saigne d’enche puis eschaufe le cautere qui est apelé «olivare», de coi ci est li forme:	 and there you will take your two means, so bleed him afterward and then apply the caustic called "olivari" of which this is the form:
Et le met sor le leu signiet d’encre, et fai en dessendant et en estraignant ta main poc et poc en trestornant;	 And you place it on a piece of parchment with ink, and make it by drawing and slowly stretching your hand bit by bit while turning.
puis lieve ta main isnelement, et rewarde le leu se tu vois l’os I sol petit;	 Then lift your hand slightly, and return the joint as soon as you see the bone has moved a little;
et se tu ne lou vois, si rencomence le cautere tant que tu voies l’os si com je lou t’ai dit;	 And if you do not see it, resume the fire treatment until you observe the bone as I have told you.
aprés pren I poc de seil, et met en awe et molle coton dedens, et met sor le leu, et li laisse III jors;	 Then take a bit of wool, and place soft, moist cotton inside, and put it on the joint, and leave for three days.
aprés met sus cotun moilliet en burre;	 After placing soft butter-covered cloth over it;
et laisse sus tant que li eschaudure soit ostee;	 And leave until the burn is healed.
aprés cure la plaie de l’oignement qui est apelez «tetrafarmaçon», tant qu’il soit sanez.	 After caring for the wound with anointment called 'tetrapharmakon' until it is sound.
Et se dirent li ancien, que quant plus demoure overte li plaie, plus s’espurge;	 And when they are said by the ancients, that the longer an open wound remains, the more it purifies.
et por ce si aide mues.	 and so he may move again.
Et dirent aucun de ces que on doit tant lassier le cautere que partie de l’os soit arse, et puis rese on ceu qui est ars de l’os, et soit curez.	And some say that one should not overuse the cautery if part of the bone is burnt; and then remove what has been burned from the bone, and treat it.
Et dient li autre c’on doit le cautere tant lassier sus, et bouter si fort c’on abaite de l’os ausi large comme I vertoil que les femmes mettent en lor fusez por ceu que les humors issent mues hors;	 And they say that the caustery should be placed lengthwise, and pushed so hard that it widens like a wreath women put in their hair to expel the fluids.
et doit on lassier la plaie longement overte;	 and one must keep the wound openly exposed for an extended period.
aprés le doit on curer et sodeir.	 Afterward, cleanse and dry it.
Et ces II manieres de cauteres ne me semblent mie estre bones dou tout en tout, fuers qu’en aucuns homes ou il ait voie de paor;	 And these two methods of caustery do not seem to me entirely good for everyone, except in some men who have cause for fear.
et mues me semble que je lou doie laissier;	 and it seems to me that I should leave them.
car li chiés li est afoiblis par les solutions continuees de nature, si com nos le tesmoignons ens autres membres;	 because the head becomes weakened by continuous natural draugnces, as we testify in other limbs.
et meisme quant li chiés dou malaide est foibles par nature, et li premiere semblance de cautere est plus salve et muedre por moi, et de celi use je oevre en donques emsamble salut.	 and similarly when the head of an ill person is weak by nature, and the first sign of caustery seems more healing and restorative to me, and thus I do this work for health in kind.
de l’anciainne dolor dou chief	Regarding the pain from an open wound
Quant en tout le chief vient dolor croniques, et dure longement, si doit user li malaides yeris et pilules qui sont apelees «cochie», et d’espurgement de chief et d’oiles et d’emplastres;	 When there is chronic pain throughout the body that persists for a long time, one must use herbs and pills called "cachet," along with enemas of wine and oil ointments.
et s’on li fait le cautere que nos avons devant dit, et il ne vaut.	 And if the fire cautery is performed as we have mentioned before, it does not work.
Pren warde se li chiés dou malade est de fort nature, et qu’il ne soit trop froit;	 Be aware that the patient's shoulder is of a strong nature, and should not be too cold.
adonques le cauterize desoz celui cautere un poc que nos avons dit desus.	 Then one must perform the fire cautery slightly as we have mentioned above.
Aprés fai cautere sus chescune corne dou chief jusc’a l’os, si com devant avons dit, et fai I cautere ou leu qui est apelez «vasselz»;	 After performing the fire cautery on each horn of the shoulder up to the bone, as we have said before, and perform the fire cautery at that spot which is called "vaseline.";
et est I leus en coi on met ventouses;	 And it is where one applies cups;
et alige ta main si que tu ne voises mie jusc’a l’os:	 and lift your hand so that you do not see to the bone.
li malaides sent trop plus grant dolor en cest cautere que as autres, et je em parlerai aillors;	 the patient feels much more pain in this cauterization than others, and I will speak elsewhere;
et covient que li cauteres des cornes soient plus subtis que cil dont on cautere la moieneteit dou chief, et c’est li forme:	 it is necessary that the cauters of horns be more delicate than those used to cauterize the middle of the head, and this is how they are made.
dou cautere dou chief	For both fire cauterization of the head
Quant en une partie dou chief vient dolor sodaine, et est estendue li maladie jusc’a l’oil, et li chiés est espurgiez par medicines mondifians, et on a fait les autres cures que j’ai dit en la division des maladies, et tout ceu ne profite mie:	 When sudden pain occurs in a part of the head and extends to the joints, and the head is purged by dissolving medicines, and other treatments I have mentioned in the classification of diseases are done, none of it helps.
adonques li fai cauteres selonc II manieres, c’est a savoir de medicine ague et de feir.	 Then you must make cauterizations according to two methods: one with ague medicine and the other with pitch.
Li cauteres de medicine ague si est que tu preignes une doce d’alz, et oste l’escorce et le recope I poc as II chiés, et puis fent la temple ou li dolor tient en teil maniere que tu puisses reponre la doce d’alz desoz le cuir;	 The medical cautery for ague requires you to pluck a hair of straw and remove the bark and paste as little as possible from around the head, then treat the temple in such a way that you can replace the straw on the leather.
et quant elle sera reponuee si le lie et l’estraint bien et le laisse ensi XII houres;	 And when it is replaced, if bound and strapped tightly, let it remain so for twelve hours;
et puis le deslie et trait fuers la doce d’ail, et laisse la plaie ensi II jors ou III;	 Then remove the binding and treat the wound in this manner for two or three days;
puis met sus cotun plongiet en burre tant que porreture en isse.	 Then place a piece of cloth soaked in butter until it becomes thoroughly permeated;
Aprés le cure d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez;	 After the ointment treatment, when it is sufficiently healed;
et se tu vues si fai ceu d’aucunes medicines comburans que j’ai escrites ou dozime traitier des medicines comburans.	 And if you wish to use any burning remedies that I have written or mentioned, treat with combustible medicines;
Li cautere de fer si est selonc ceste meniere.	 The iron cautery is made in such a manner.
Chaufe le cautere de coi ci est li forme:	 Heat the shape of which here is the cauldron:

et le met sor le leu dolorous, et tien ta main et trestorne le feir un poc legierement, tant que li moitiez de l’espés dou keur soit arse;	 And it must be placed back in its rightful position, and hold your hand and gently twist the fire a little, until the joints are as white as cream.
et lieve ta main que li artere n’arde, que est defuers, et decorre habundance de sanc.	 And release your hand so that the vein does not burn further backward and flows abundant blood.

puis i met coton moilliet em burre, et puis cure le leu d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez;	 Then you apply softened lard to the area, and then treat the head with ointment until it is healthy.

de emigraine	Migraine

de l’epilempsie	On epilepsy

de la cure de fistule par cautere	On the treatment of a fistula by cautery
Quant tu cures fistule si com nos avons dit en divisions des maladies, et tes cures ne profitent mie, adonques covient il que tu li fais cautere selonc ceste maniere.	When treating a fistula as we have described in the divisions of diseases, and if your treatments do not yield results, then it is necessary for you to perform cautery according to this method.
Comande au malaide qu’il mette son chief en ton sain;	 Command the patient to put his head in your hand.
et teigne li menistres son chief entre tes mains en teil maniere qu’il ne se mueve, ne ne demoinne son chief;	 and instruct the assistant to place the master's head between their hands in such a way that it does not move or turn.
aprés met coton moilliet en abin d’uef ou en jus de persillion sus l’oil;	 after, place soft cotton swabs in an eggcup or glass of lemon juice on the eye.
aprés chaufe le cautere qui est teilz:	 then heat the caustic which is ready:
et est chevez au chief si com li forme d’une penne de vouteul, ensamble la queil soit li cautere;	 And it is near the head as if of a bell-clapper shape, with the quill being the fire cautery.
se tu vues, si soit apointé des l’un chief dusc’a l’autre, et se tu vues, si soit ausi com une tente;	 If you observe it, if it is pointed from one head to the other, and if you see it, so it is as a tent.
mais toutevoie, cist qui est chevez vaut mues por ton ovraige.	 However, this which is near the top must be moved for your operation.
Aprés presse la fistule s’ele est overte, et en trai la porriture, et la seche;	 After pressing the abscess if it is open, and treating any swelling, and drying out.
et s’ele est close, si la oevre, et trai fuers la bowe;	 And if it is closed, treat the wound, and apply heat to scars.
aprés met sus le cautere chaut forment, et tien ta main au cautere a la partie dou neif ensus de l’oil, que ta mains ne faice folie;	 After applying hot caustic properly, and hold your hand to the caustic on the part without hair above the oil, so that your hands do not become foolish.
et met le cautere en la graisse de l’oil, et la corromp.	 And place the caustic in the fat of the oil, and let it fester.
Se tu viens au comencement dou cautere jusc’a l’os, si serait bien.	 If you come to the beginning of the cautery up to the bone, that would be best.
Se ceu non, si rencomence le cautere encor une fois, et autre se tu en as mestier, et le laisse III jors;	 If not, repeat the caustic treatment once more, and if necessary, leave for three days;
aprés i met sus coton moilliet en burre, et lou cure de l’oignement desiccatif tant qu’il soit sanez, et se XL jors passent qu’il ne soit sanez, si met sus medicine ague corrosive tant que li os soit descovers;	 After that, apply moist cotton in butter, and heal the dry ointment until it is healthy again, and if 40 days have passed without improvement, then apply corrosive medication until the bone is exposed.
et lou reis selonc ceu que il venrait en son chapistre.	 And follow accordingly as described in this chapter.
Et i a une maniere de cautere de fistule que aucun des anciens dirent.	 And there is a method of fire cautery for treating fistulas that none of the ancients mentioned.
Entens a fistule, et fens le leu;	 On touches the abscess, and feels its depth.
aprés met en la fendure I camahan subtil de coi ci est li forme:	 Afterward insert the slender instrument with which is formed its shape:
et i font a la quantiteit d’une .З. de plonc;	 and they make it to the quantity of one ounce of lead;
et tien ta main ou camahan fermement, et ne se mueve li malaides nes point, que li plons fondus ne corre a son oil;	 and hold your hand or instrument firmly, ensuring that the patient does not move so that the molten lead can flow into its cavity.
et covient c’on mette sus l’oil a malaide coton moilliet en abin d’uefz ou en awe:	 and it is necessary to place over the oil on the sickbed, cotton wool in an eggshell or bowl:
li plonc si art lou leu de fistule, et lou saine per mervillouse saniteit.	 The lead fills up the hole of the abscess and heals it with marvelous healthiness.
Et se li fistule est sanee per le cautere que nos avons dit, c’est boin.	 And if the fistula has been healed by fire cautery as we have described, it is good.
Se ce non, si covient aministrer pertus au neif, et ramener la fistule au cors dou neif selonc ceu qu’il covient en som propre leu.	 If not, if it needs to be administered by the needle and drawn back into place on the skin where properly located in its right place.
des crevaices en levres	From cracks in the lips
Mout de fois avienent crevaices en levres que sont apelees «poil», et meismement en levres des enfans.	Often there occur lip cracks called "hairs," particularly in children's lips.
Quant tu cures ces crevaices de ceu que nos avons dit en divisions, et li cure ne profite, adonques eschaufe .i. petit cautere cultellaire selonc ceste forme:	When you treat these cracks as we have said in sections, and the treatment does not help, then apply a small pointed cautery according to this method:
Et le met hastanment en celles crevaices tant qu’il viegne jusc’a font;	 And quickly put it in those cavities as long as it flows out:
aprés cure le leu de cerote tant qu’il soit sanez.	 Afterward, cleanse the hole of pus until it is healed.
de l’aposteme de la goule	From the incision of a boil on the throat
Quant apostume vient en la racine de la goule ou en l’uve, ou ou palais, ou as racines des dens, aprés fait porriture et ront et est enveillis et devient fistule;	 When an abscess comes to the root of the throat or in the ear, or on the roots of the teeth, after causing decay and pus and is aged and becomes a fistula.
et tu le cures si com nos avons dit en divisions, et il ne profite mie:	 And you treat it as we have said in sections, but it does not heal.
adonques covient il que tu aies I cautere selonc la quantiteit de la fistule;	 Then it is necessary for you to apply the fire cautery according to the quantity of the fistula.
aprés le bote ou pertus de la fistule, et tien ta main tant que li fer chaus viegne au font de li, et ou derrien leu;	 After opening or piercing the fistula, and hold your hand until the heat subsides at its source, and thereafter.
et fai ensi une fois ou II, aprés le cure de ce que nos avons dit en cures, tant qu’il soit sanez;	 And do so twice as we have said in treatments, until it is healed.
et s’il est curez ensi, c’est boin;	 And if treated thusly, it is good.
et se ceu non, si covient descovrir le leu et oster l’os corrumput, selonc ceu que vos le troverez en son chapistre.	 And if not, it is necessary to discover its place and remove the decayed bone, according to what you will find in this chapter of the treatise.
dou movement des dens	The two movements of the teeth (or "dou mouvement des dens") likely refers to dental issues such as shifting or misalignment within Old French medical texts. It could also pertain to treatments involving teeth, like adjusting their position for proper occlusion or addressing dental abscesses that might require procedures akin to modern endodontics or extractions.
Quant les gencives sont mollifies par moistor et les dens muevent, et tu le cures per medicines et ceu ne vaut, adonc met le chief dou malaide en ton sain;	 When the gums are softened by moisture and the teeth move, and you treat it with medicine but nothing works, then place the head of the ailing in their bed.
aprés eschaufe le cautere dont li forme venra ci aprés en teil maniere que tu mettes une cainne sor le dent;	 After healing the fire cautery, its shape will come again later, place a wick on the tooth in such a way.
et met dedens le cautere chaut hastanment, et tien tant ta main que li malaides sente la chalor venant a la racine dou dent;	 And insert the hot fire caustery into the gaps of the tooth, and hold your hand so that the patient feels the heat coming from the root of the tooth.
aprés lieve ta main et rencomence le cautere selonc ta volenteit;	 After releasing your hand, resume the caustery as you wish.
aprés emplisse li malaides sa bouche d’awe salee, et la teigne une houre et raiche fuers.	 After filling the patient's mouth with saltwater pus, and letting it sit for an hour and a half.
Et en teil maniere li dens qui estoit movans si est confermez, et li gencive mollifie restrainte, et li moistors corrumpue sechie.	And in such a manner that the tooth which was moving is firmly put back; and the softened gums are kept from further movement, and the moisture corrupted is dried.
de la dolor des dens	Of the pain of the teeth
Quant dolor de dens vient por froidor, ou il i a froidor ou veir, et les cures de medicine ne valent, adonc i ait mestier de cautere selonc II manieres:	 When toothache comes from cold or heat, and medicinal treatments are ineffective, then there is need for cauterization according to two methods:
et cautere de burre et cautere de feu.	 And cauterization with butter and cauterization with fire.
Cautere de burre si est telz que tu preignes burre de vaiche, et le bout en une cuillier de fer ou d’arain;	 The cauterization of butter is as follows: you take butter from a cow, and the end in a spoon made of iron or silver.
aprés pren coton et envolope sus la pointe d’une tente, et la moille en burre bulit, et met sus le dent dolant hastanment et tien tant qu’il soit refroidiez;	 After taking cotton and wrapping it around the tip of a tent, and applying grease to the wool, then place it on the aching tooth quickly and hold until cooled.
et ensi fai sovent tant que sa vertus viegne a la racine de la dent, et se tu vues si moille laine et coton en burre froit, et met sus le dent doillant, et met sus I fer chaut tant que li feus viegne au chevement dou dent.	 Often do this until its virtue reaches the root of the tooth; and if you see that it is very soft wool and cotton in cold butter, place it on the aching tooth, and place a hot iron upon it until the heat comes to the union with the tooth.
Li cauteres ensamble feu si est telz que tu preignes uns cainne de fer ou d’arain, et soit grosse si que li feus ne viegne a la bouche dou malaide;	 The fire cauterization consists of such devices that you grasp with an iron or copper rod, and it is thick enough so that the heat does not reach to the mouth of the patient.
aprés chaufe le cautere, de coi li forme venra ci aprés, et le met sus le dent et tien ta main tant que li cauteres soit refroidiez;	 After heating the cauterization, so that its form will come afterward, and place it on the tooth and hold your hand until the cauterization has cooled.
fai ceu sovent, car li dolor sera ostee celui jor meisme ou l’endemain.	 Do this often, because the pain will be reduced that same day or the next.
Et covient que li malaides emplisse sa bouche de boin burre en l’empressement de cel cautere, et puis le raiche fuer;	 It is necessary for the patient to fill his mouth with good butter during the urgency of that fire cautery, and then let it flow.
et c’est li forme dou cautere:	 And this is the form of the fire cautery:
Et fai cautere dou queil chief que tu voudras, et selonc ceu que tu as pooir;	 And perform a cautery on the eyelid that you wish to do, and according to your ability.
et c’est li forme de la caine:	 And this is the form of the lancet:
des scrophules	the f h. Manze de lapeccest c's.
Quant les scrophules sont de fleume et de moistors froides, et ne sont obeissans a digestion par medicines, adonques eschaufe le cautere cheveit de coi ci aprés vient li forme, et ait II aovertures por les fumees a issir au cautere de l’autre partie;	 When the scrofula is of phlegm and cold humors, and does not obey digestion by medicines, then apply the fire cautery as follows so that it comes in afterward, with two openings for the fumes to escape from the other part of the cautery.
et met le cautere chaut sus l’apostume une fois, ou II se mestier est, tant qu’il viegne au font de l’apostume;	 and place the hot cautery over the abscess once or as often as necessary until it reaches the source of the abscess.
et se li apostume est petis si met cautere selonc la quantiteit de l’apostume, et le laisse ensi III jors;	 If the abscess is small, apply a cautery according to its size, and leave it as such for three days.

Li forme de la cainne:	 The shape of the caulbone:
Quant les moistors vainquent sus les chenals dou pormon, et meismement quant ce vient de froide complexion, adonc covient que li malaides soit voidiez premiers par medicines solutives;	 When stones obstruct the ducts due to heat or particularly cold conditions, then it is necessary for the patient to first be purged with soluble medicines;
aprés li fai cautere a la racine de la gorge, et te garde que tu ne venir mie jusc’a la gorge, et n’ardre dou keur mais c’un poc.	 After performing the fire cautery at the root of the throat, ensure that you do not come near to the throat itself and let it burn only slightly;

et cure le leu si com nos avons devant dit tant qu’il soit sanez.	 And treat the joint as we have previously said until it is well positioned.
de la toust	To treat inflammation of the throat, also known as tonsillitis or pharyngitis.
Quant tous et maladie de pormon sont de moistors froides, et li malaides nen ait fievre ne sechor, et est li maladie anciaine, se li fai .II cauteres sus la forcele en leus vuis;	 When all diseases of the pharynx are due to cold dampness, and the patient has no fever or thirst, and it is an early illness, then apply two fire cauteries on the lymph nodes behind your tongue.
et I autre cautere emmi le pis entre II mameles;	 and another one at the point between the nipples.

et soient li poins jusc’a XXX, ou enqui entor.	 and let the points be up to thirty or near it.

de la dislocation de l’ajutoire	Regarding shoulder joint dislocation.
Quant li chiés de l’ajutoire est desaloiez par cause de moistor, et on le remet a leu, et il n’i puet demorer ains revient adés et desalue par petit movement qui avient, si com nos avons esproveit, adonques covient il que tu ramoinnes la dislocation premierement.	When the head of the shoulder is dislocated due to moisture, and it is reset but cannot stay in place, repeatedly dislocating with slight movement as we have tested, then you must first reset the dislocation.
Aprés soit sovinez li malaides sus son dos et sus son costeit;	 Afterward, place the sickly on their backs and along their ribs.
aprés lieve le keur qui est dedens le titillite as dois de ta main senestre;	 Afterwards, remove the key that is within the tight joint of your left hand;
et se li jointure est desaluee dedens, si eschaufe le cautere qui a II ners douqueil ci est li forme:	 and if the joint is dislocated internally, then heat the cautery that has two ends for shaping.
et cauterize lou keur tant qu’il le perce jusc’a costeit, et venrait li fugure dou cautere ensamble IIII cauteres;	 and cauterize the key until it reaches your ribs, then bring the shape of the cautery together with four cauteries.
et por ceu est faite cautere avec le cautere qui a III ners, por coi li figure de cauterization sunt sis cauteres;	 and because it is made from the cautery that has three ends, thus the shapes of cauterization are these three cauteries.
et sont li nerf selonc la subtiliteit d’une tente et c’est li forme dou cautere qui a III ners:	 and they are the nerves according to the subtlety of a tent, which is the shape of the caturery that has three ends.
Et aucune fois est ajostez sus ce .i. nerf por coi il i a .viij. cauteres.	On any occasion it is touched upon this particular nerve, where there are seven cauterizations.
Aprés met sus le cautere porrelz broiez avec seil;	 After applying the fire cautery, rub with salt mixed with fat;
aprés fai reposer le malaide, et ne soit meus li membres par lonc tens tant qu’il soit bien confortez.	 After allowing the patient to rest, and not moving their limbs for a long time until they are well supported.
Et s’il est desaloiez desus, liquelz chose avient poc, adonques fait cautere sus l’epaisse dou cautere clavile, ou mout de cauteres en poignant.	 And if it becomes dislocated above, little happens at first; then make a cautery on the thick part of the cauliflower bone or many dots close together.
Car li jointure est refermee, et est ostee li moistor et est sanez li malaides.	 For the joint is repositioned, and there is moisture in the bone and health returns to the patient.
Quant en l’estomac vienent froidures et mout de moistors tant qu’il l’estraient a sa complexion, et sont multipliet li catharre a lui, et es manieres de cures acostumees et il ne profite mie, adonc covient que li malaides soit sovinez sus son dos, et estende ses jambes et ses mains.	 When the stomach has many coldness and moisture so that it's removed from its nature, and there are multiple catharsis for him, along with usual treatment methods which do not help; then it should be made to lie supine on his back, stretching out his legs and hands.
De ceu en aprés li fai III cauteres I desoz la cuillier dou pis per la quantiteit d’un doi, a tout le cautere clavile, et II cauteres defuers les II costez tant que li figure des cauteres soit a III angles, et ait teil espaice entre l’une et l’autre qu’elles ne soient jointes ensamble quant elles giteront porriture;	 After this, then do three cauldrons on the left side of the hip for an amount equal to one double measure at each cautery point, and two cauldrons behind the two ribs until the marks from the cauteries are in a triangular shape, and have adequate spacing between them so that they do not merge when spreading.
et soient li cautere si parfont qu’il porpreignent les II pars dou keur, et soit li figure des cauteres selonc ceste forme sens ajostement:	 and the cauldrons should be placed front to back so they prick both sides of the chest, and the marks from the caturers are according to this pattern without crowding.
Et se tu vues cauterize d’un grant cautere enmi l’estomac selonc ceste forme;	 And if you see a large fire cautery within the stomach according to this method;
et celui qui avra paour de cest cautere, cauterize en poignant et seigne sus l’estomac i. point selonc la quantiteit que tu vues d’enche;	 And if one has fear of this fire cautery, perform it by poking and sign above the stomach at a specific spot according to the quantity you see thereof;
puis le cauterize a tot le cautere qui est apelez «poins».	 Then cauterize with all the caustic substance called "points".
Aprés le cure de la cure que nos avons eut devant, tant qu’il soit sanez.	 After the treatment of the fracture we have had before, until it is healed.
Quant au foie vient dolor de froit et de moistor et de grosse ventositeit, tant qu’il est fuer mis de sa complexion natureil per les superfluitez;	 When the liver comes to pain from cold and moisture and distention, until it is removed from its natural state by excesses;
et li malaides est curez de ceu que nos avons dit en divisions, et il ne li profite mie, si covient que li malaides soit sovinez sus son haitereil;	 and the patient is treated as we have described in sections, but it does not benefit them, so it must be ensured that they are supine on their side.
et signe d’enche III cauteres selonc ceste forme et ceste figure et ceste quantiteit sus lou foie, defuer les ypocondres, lai ou li coutes de l’ome vient;	 and apply fire cauldrons in quantities of three according to this method, shape, and figure on the liver, avoiding the epigastric region where the edges of the lobes meet;
et ait d’espaice entre chaicun cautere la groissece d’un doi;	 And there is space between each cautery, the growth of a thumb.
et soient li cautere dou lonc dou cors, et ne presser mie mout ta main a tot le cautere;	 and let the cautery be long and wide across the body, and do not squeeze too much at all the cautery site.
et soit arse tant soulement li moitiez dou keur, et soit li malaides drois sus ses piez;	 and let it burn only halfway down so that the patient's head may be upright, and make them lie on their side.
et s’il ne peut, si soit gisans, et estende ses jambes, et lieve ses brais;	 and if they cannot do so, let them be lying down, extend their legs, and lift their arms.
et c’est li forme:	 And this is the form:
Et se ta volentez est, si cauterize ces cauteres dou cutellaire, se tu es subtilz et saiges en l’art, et te warde que tu n’ardes mie tout le keur, car tu feroies sechier tout le cors;	 And if you wish to do so, if you are subtle and wise in the art, cauterize these cutaneous cauders, but be sure not to burn all of the head, for this would dry up the entire body.
et qu’il ne viegne jusc’a boueil, car li keurs est mout subtilz lai endroit, et lou saiches por voir.	 And it does not reach to boiling point, for the veins are very delicate in that place, and they swell as though to see.
Quant il a apostume au foie, et tu vues savoir s’il est en la char dou foie ou en la toile:	 When it is an abscess on the liver, and you must determine if it is in the fleshy part of the liver or in the tissue.
s’il est en la char, se sent li malaides dolor ne mie trop fort;	 If it is in the flesh, the patient feels pain but not too severe;
et s’il est en la toile, si sent dolor forsenee.	 And if it is in the tissue, he feels unbearable pain.
Et lors quant ceste cure desoit les mires, si covient que li malaides soit sovinez sus sa teste;	 And when this treatment requires bandaging, then one must lay the patient supine with their head raised;
et puis seigne d’enche le leu ou li apostumes est, et puis chaufe le cautere qui est semblans au rais, de coi ci est li forme:	 And next, examine where the wound or abscess is located, and then heat the caustic which resembles iron filings, in this way:
Et cauterize I cautere tant que li keurs soit ars, et viegne jusc’a syphac, tant que li porreture soit toute fuers;	 And with fire cautery up to when the core is scorched, and until the sphincter comes, so that the protrusion is fully retracted.
aprés la cure selonc la cure des essues tant qu’il soit sanez;	 Afterward, according to the procedure of closing wounds until it is healthy again;
et ne covient mie que de cest cautere use nuls fuers que cil qui ait estudieit longement en l’art de medicine, et par cui mains cestes maladies ont corrut aucune fois.	 And only this type of cautery should be used by those who have studied extensively in the art of medicine, and through whose hands these diseases have spread at times.
Adonques puet il hardiement ovrer, et toutevoies il me semble que mues vaut li laissier.	 Then he may hardly work, and in any case, it seems to me that one should let it move freely.
dou cautere de pleuresin	byrto:
Li ancien dirent que on doit faire a pleuresin cauteres de racines d’aristologe, et en teil maniere:	 The ancients said that one must make root cauteries with rhizome as follows:
pren une racine d’aristologe longe, la plus grant que tu poras troveir, et soit seche, et soit ausi grosse et ausi longe comme tes dois;	 Take a rhizome root of Aristology long, the largest that you can find, and let it be dried, and also as thick and as long as your finger.
et la moille en oile, et l’emprens au feu, et cauterize I cautere entre la forcele et lou col, et II petis cauteres un poc en dessendant en la partie qui est desoz la barbe;	 And the flesh in oil, and grasp at the fire, and perform a cautery between the forelock and the neck, and small cauldrations slightly descending on the part that is below the beard.
et II cauteres entre la quinte coste et la sisime, en declinant derrier un poc;	 And two cauteries between the fifth rib and the sixth, slightly inclined backward a bit.

et ne presser mie ta main, ains fai apertement ausi com en odorant.	 And do not tighten your hand too much, but make it open as in smelling.
Et dirent aucun ancien que aucun home usent de cautere de feir semblant a I raseur, et l’eschaufent et le mettent entre les costes, tant qu’il vient a cel aposteme;	 And the ancient ones say that no man should use fire cauldrations resembling a barber's, and they warm it up and place it between the ribs until it reaches the abscess.
et saut fuers li dolor, si com nos avons dit en l’aposteme dou foie.	 And it jumps up the pain, as we have said in the abscess of the liver.
Mais en cestui ovraige est paour ou li malaides muert maintenant, ou fistule i vient qui ne puet estre sanee.	 But in this treatment there is fear or the patient dies immediately, or a fistula arises which cannot be healed.
de la mice	The ancient ones said that no man should use a cautery resembling shaving, heat it and place it between the ribs until an abscess reaches; then there is relief from pain as we have described in liver abscess. But in this kind of treatment often fear or illness cause death immediately, or fistula appears that cannot be healed.
Quant tu cures la maladie de la mice de ceu que nos avons dit as divisions des cures, et il ne profite mie, adonques i afierent .iij. manieres de cautere que tuit sont boin.	When treating the illness of epilepsy as we have said in the previous sections on treatments, and it proves effective, then there are three methods of cautery that all work well.
Desquelz li une maniere si est que tu faices III cauteres, ou IIII, en lignant selonc la longor de la mice, selonc la figure dou cautere dou foie que nos avons dit devant;	 There is a way in which you make three or four cauterizations, arranging according to the length of the wound, following the liver cautery method we have mentioned before.
et n’apresser mie ta main a tout le cautere, et soit li malaides sovins sor son dos;	 and do not press down with your hand on all the cauterization, and let the patient lie on their back.
et une autre maniere de cautere si est que tu eschaufe le cautere qui a II ners, si com nos l’avons mostreit en la dislocation de l’espaule;	 And another method of cauterization is to boil the one with two nicks, as we have shown in shoulder dislocation.
et lieve le keur qui est endroit la mice, ou li coutes dou malaide vient devers senestre, et soit li elevations dont tu lieves le keur selonc la keur, selonc la longesce dou cors, et li cautere soient selonc la largesce dou cors.	 and lift the head which is where the wound edges come from the left side, and make the elevations of which you raise the head according to its size, following the body's length and width for the cauterization.
Aprés i boute les II ners enflamez tant que li keurs soit perciez de l’autre part, et puis trai fuers le cautere, et ensi en i avra IIII.	 After placing two inflamed nerves until the core is pierced from the other side, and then apply the fire cautery, so there will be four in total.
Et se tu vues, si cauterize a tot le cautere a III ners.	 And if you see it, cauterize all with the cautery at three nerves.
Aprés le cure quant il a geteit porriture par lonc tens, et ce vaut mues que li autre des cures devant dites.	 After the healing process has been ongoing for long periods, and this results in movements like those of previously mentioned treatments.
de ydropisie	Of dropsy.
Cautere ne vaut a ydropique, fors c’a la maniere qui est apelee «asclytes».	 Caution does not pertain to hydrophobia, but rather to the manner called "esclitics".
Quant tu la cures selonc les manieres que nos avons dit en divisions, et ta cure ne profite mie, adonques covient il que tu li faices IIII cauteres entor la boude, et I sus l’estomac, et un sus le foie, et I sus la mice, et II derrier le dos sus l’espinee, et I endroit le pis;	 When you treat as we have described in divisions and the cure does not work, then it is necessary to make four cauterizations around the buttocks, one on top of the stomach, one above the liver, one above the kidneys, two behind the back at the spine, and one spot on the genitals;
et soit li cauteres bien pres de l’espés dou keur.	 And each cautery should be close to the region of pain in the core.
Aprés laisse le cautere aovert por giter porriture lonc tens, et ne lassier mie la cure dou malaide aprés le cautere;	 After leaving the open cautery for prolonged use, do not leave the patient's pain untreated afterward.
et sanation se hasterait, et seront ensamble les II ententions avec l’aide de Deu.	 And healing would hasten, and they shall together have two intentions with the help of God.
Li forme dou cautere por le ventre soit li clavile que nos avons devant mostreit;	 The form of the fire cautery for the belly is shown by us before.
et cil por le dos soit olivaire, selonc ceu qu’il est ci devant mis.	 and that one for the back be olive-shaped, as it was previously set here.
de l’enfleure des piez	Of inflammation in the joints
Quant li piez sont enflez a celui qui est ydropique, et sont plain d’awe citrine, il covient que tu cauterizes sus le dos dou piet entre l’auriculaire et l’anulaire;	 When the feet are swollen in one who is dropsical, and filled with pale yellow bile, it is necessary to cauterize on the back between the little finger and the ring finger.
et lieve ta main avec le cautere sens torner.	 and lift your hand with a turning of the cautery.
Et n’entrer mie trop em parfont, ensi sarrait fuers li awe citrine, et soit li cauteres selonc cest forme:	 And do not go too far in, so it would shrink the clear yellow fluid, and let the cautery be according to this method.
Aprés fai sus II jambes II cauteres en chescune jambe a la pointe dou cutellaire;	 Afterward, perform two cauteries on each leg at the point of the calf muscle;
et soit li cauteres dou lonc, l’un desoz le genoil devant et l’autre defuers, enmi la jambe;	 and let one cautery be long, one behind the thigh beforehand and another further down, in between the leg.
et laisse les cauteres aovers longement sens curer, que li awe en isse;	 And leave the burns to heal for a long time until they break open;
aprés le cure des autres cures que nos avons dit.	 After treating other wounds as we have mentioned.
de la menoison	of melancholy
Quant solution de ventre vient de froidor et de moistor, tant que li vertus retentive et digestive qui est ou stomac et en l’intestine est afleboie, et ne puet estre curez par manieres de cures;	 When the solution of a swollen belly comes from coldness and moisture, as long as the retentive and digestive virtues that are in the stomach and intestines have burst forth, and cannot be treated by usual methods.
et tu vois le malaide bien soffrant et de fort vertut, si fai I grant cautere sus l’estomac selonc ceu qu’il en a parleit ci devant ou cautere de l’estomac, au cautere circule;	 and you see the patient suffering greatly and with great virtue, then do a large fire cautery on the stomach as described here before or the cautery of the stomach, where the cautery circulates.
et IIII cauteres entor la boude subtilz a tout I cautere clavile subtil, et II cauteres sus les hainches.	 and four subtle cauteries around the belly with all sharp cauteries, and two on the groins.
Et se tu vois les moistors habundans et le malaide soffrant, se li fai cautere sus le poignil, et .i. cautere sus chaicun yle, et .ij. petis cauteres sus l’estomac delez le grant, car li cure est profitans quant il i a bone aide.	And if you see abundant moistors and the patient suffering, make a cautery on the palm, and one cautery on each finger, and two small cauteries near the large stomach, for the treatment is beneficial when there is good aid.
de la cure des emorroydes	On the treatment of hemorrhoids
Quant les emorroydes sont ou fondement, ou une ou plusors, et sont ancienes et sont de grosses humors froides et moistes corrumpues, et sont curees si com nos avons dit en divisions, et il ne profite mie, si fai cauteres:	 When bunions are at their foundation, or one or more, and they are ancient and filled with large cold and damp corrupted humors, and treated as we have said in sections, then it does not help if you do not apply fire cautery.
III sus l’espine dou dos, celi qui est tout defuers desoz almecdate poc et poc en triangulant, et I cautere desoz la boude II dois;	 For the spine of the back, which is a little forward and forward in triangle, apply fire cautery below the vertebrae two.
et se tu penses que ses estomac soit refroidiez, et li viande ne cuise, et on voit enfler la faice, adonques li faice on I grant cautere sus le stomac, si com il est devant dit, et I autre sus le foie, et I autre sus la mice a tout le cautere clavile;	 And if you think that the stomach is cooled, and the flesh does not cook, and one sees swelling of the face, then apply a large fire cautery to the stomach as before mentioned, and another on the liver, and another with a piercing cautery over all.
et laisse le cautere overt lonc tens.	 And leave the fire cautery on for long periods of time.
Aprés cure le leu tant qu’il soit sanez.	 After curing the joint until it is sound.
de la charnositeit qui est nommee «thelul»	From the flesh which is called "thelel".
Quant tu copes althelul, si eschaufe le cautere qui semble I raseur, et puis le met tout embraseit sus cel althelul copeit;	 When you come to the eyebrow, if the hair is short and sparse, then ignite the fire over it, and set it all aflame where the eyebrows are placed.
et i laisse tant ta main que li cauteres viegne a la naissance de la voine, de coi li sans cort;	 and leave your hand as well as the caustic to touch the opening of the vein, so that the blood does not clot.
fai ceu une fois ou II, et s’il i a mout d’althelul, si cauterize chaicun si com nos avons dit;	 do this once or twice, and if there are many eyebrows, cauterize each as we have said.
aprés les cure d’oignemens profitans tant qu’il soient sanez;	 after applying healing ointments until they become healthy.
et se tu cauterizes d’un cautere grant sus alchatim, si avra plus grant aide.	 and if you use a large caustic on the eyelid, it will have more benefit.
de plaie mal curee	Of poorly treated wound
Quant li malaides ne puet soffrir tailleure ne overture, que nos raconterons en son leu, si vient teil maladie que ne puet estre sanee fuer que par cautere.	When the patient cannot bear cutting or opening, we will tell you in its place about a disease that cannot be healed but by cautery.
Quant a aucun vient fistule, et est enveillie et giete porriture et moistors corrumpues, si la doies prover a tot une tente subtil, et garde que tu saiches a tot la tente combien elle a de parfont.	 When there is an abscess and it becomes old and rotten with decay and corrupted moisture, you should thoroughly explore the entire area, and be aware of all aspects within that area.
Aprés eschaufe le cautere qui semble I raseur, et le boute en la fistule selonc la quantiteit que li tente i est entrée, et rencomence lou cautere tant que cil cors porris et corrumpus soient ars, une fois, ou II ou III, selonc la quantiteit de som besoing;	 After igniting the caustic that appears sparse, and pour it into the fistula according to the quantity that has entered inside it, and continue with the caustic until the corrupted or decayed body is healed, once, or twice, or three times, depending on how much is needed.
et te warde d’ardre lé nerf qui sunt enqui, et des grans voinnes.	 And watch for inflaming of the nerves present therein, and large veins.
se li fistule vait au cors de la vesie et a l’intestine, si te warde de ces leus, et ne faire ceu fuers que en leu charnut, et pense qu’ele n’est mie persans;	 If the abscess leads to the bladder and intestines, watch for these slits, and do not perform this further when fully developed, but think that it is not true perforations.
aprés cure le leu tant qu’il soit sanez, et se li leus est saielez, et les matieres sont ostees lonc tens, adonc saiches que li leus est sanez entierement;	 After treating the wound until it is cleaned out, and if the slits are filled with pus, and the materials have been long gone, then declare that the slit has healed completely.
et se les matieres ne sont ostees, saiche que li leus est troez, et corrumpus li os au font;	 And if the materials have not been removed, determine that the wound is overfilled, and corruption occurs in the bone at its base.
et ensi com un de ces que nos dirons en son leu.	 And thus as one of these which we mention within it.
de la maladie des reins	On kidney disease
Quant dolor de froit vient as rains, et de grosse ventositeit, et ne prent talant de femme, adonc covient il que tu li fais cautere sus les rains d’une part et d’autre au cautere clavile que nos avons devant dit;	 When the pain of cold comes as rain and heavy windiness, and does not take interest in women, then one must make a cautery on both sides with the pointed caustic iron that we have previously mentioned.
et se nos le cauterizons em mileu, si avra III cauteres en ligne, et se feront plus grant aide.	 And if we cauterize it completely, there will be three cauteries in a line, and this will provide greater help.
de la vessie	of the bladder
Quant li vessie est mole et foible de froit et de moistor, si que li malaides retient l’urine, adonc li fai cautere en la partie defuers sus la vessie, la ou encomencent li poil dou poignil, et I a destre et I a senestre, et soit chescuns cauteres si lons com li nous d’un poce;	 When the bladder is swollen and weak from cold and moisture, and the patient holds in urine, then you must make a cautery on the part behind it near the bladamoignon where hairs begin to grow, one to the right, one to the left, and each as long as our pace.
et li fais I cautere defuers le dos, ou II se tu en as besoing;	 and you shall make I cautery along the back, or two if needed in that area.
et soit li cauteres clavile selon la forme devant dite.	 And perform the clavicular cauldrons according to the previously mentioned form.
de la marris	of the testicles
Quant li marrix est froide et moiste, et ne laisse mie por ceu a concevoir, et les flors sont corrumpues et lor termines tarde;	 When the phlegm is cold and damp, it does not allow for conception, and the seeds are corrupted and their ends delay.
et quant elles vienent, si sent grant dolor:	 and when they come, there is great pain:
adonques covient il c’on li faice III cauteres entor la boude, si com nos avons dit ou cautere de la vessie, et II cauteres defuers le dos;	 then it must be done as we have said with three cauldrons around the bladder and two cauldrons forward of the back.
et soit li cauteres clavile, si com nos avons dit.	 And perform the clavicular cauldron as we have mentioned.
de la hainche	Causes of thigh pain:
Quant les moistors viscouses dessendent a la boiste de la hainche, et por ceste cause si se muet de son leu, et li signes est que li cuisse est plus longe que li autre quant on le mesure ensamble;	 When the viscid drops descend to the hip bone sac, and because of this it moves from its place, and the sign is that the thigh is longer than the other when measured together;
et est trovez li leus dou departement vuis, si covient que tu cauterizes le malaide sus la boiste de la hainche a I cautere semblant au cercle, et seigne devant le leu entor la boiste si com elle torne, si que li boiste soit dedens le cercle;	 And the hinges of departure are found, it is necessary that you causticate the patient on the hip socket with a cautery resembling a circle, and place it so that the socket turns as if in a circle, ensuring the socket is within the circle.
et si soit li cauteres telz com cil dont on a cauterizeit le stomac.	 And the caustication should be such as those used to cauterize the stomach.
Et se cist cauteres ne t’est presens, se li fai III cauteres de l’olivaire grans, et soit li cauteres ausi parfont com tous li keurs;	 And if these caustications are not present, use three olive-sized caustics and make the caustic as broad as any of them.
et le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	 And apply until it is properly healed.
de la dolor de la hainche	From the pain of the hip
Quant dolor vient en la boiste de la hainche, et c’est de froidor et de moistor, et li malaides est curez de ceu que nos avons dit en la division et li cure ne vaut, et li maladie est anciene:	 When pain comes in the hip socket, and it is from coldness and moisture, the patient has been treated as we have said in the section, and the treatment does not work, and the illness is old.
adonc covient il que tu purges le malaide des grosses humors de pilules fetides, ou autres pilules bones semblans.	 Then it is necessary for you to purge the patient of excess humors with foul pills or other good-smelling pills.
Aprés li fai cautere;	 After performing the fire cautery;
et li maniere dou cautere si est selonc II manieres:	 and there are two ways to do this cautery as follows:
c’est a savoir ensamble medicines ardans, et cautere de feu.	 That is to say, together with burning medications, and fire cautery.
Cautere de feu si est selonc mout de manieres, desquelz li uns est telz:	 Fire cautery comes in many ways, among which one kind is such:
que tu cauterize sus la boiste de la hainche III cauteres triangulalz selonc ceste forme, et i fai bone profunditeit et grant, et ait entre chaicun cautere d’espaice la groissece d’un doi, et soit li cauteres olivaire;	 that you perform three triangular cautions according to this shape on the thigh bag, with good depth and size, and leave enough space between each caution as big as a bean;
aucune fois fait on cautere en mileu sus lou chief de la hainche, por coi il en i a IIII selonc ceste forme:	 never make the caution in the middle of the thigh, because there are four according to this shape:
Et se tu vues, si le cauterize au cautere dou cercle que nos avons devant dit en la dislocation de la hainche;	 And if you see it, use the fire cautery at the circle we have previously mentioned in the shoulder dislocation.
mais fai en teil maniere que li cercles conteigne toute la hainche, et tous li espés dou keur soit ars.	 But do so that the circle contains the entire shoulder, and all sides are smoothed out.
Et c’est li maniere c’on fait en sciatique, quant li dolor tient en la hainche, et ne parvient mie jusc’a la cuisse ne jusc’a la jambe.	 And this is the method used for sciatica when the pain is in the thigh and does not reach the thigh or the leg.
Et s’ele vient jusc’a la cuisse et la jambe, se li fai II cauteres lai ou li malaides dit que li dolor li tient, et I cautere desus la cheville IIII dois, a la partie senestre un poc;	 And if it extends to the thigh and leg, make the fire cautery at the place where the patient says the pain is, and apply four small cauteries above the ankle on the left side.
et soit li cauteres cutellaire, et soit arse li espesseté dou keur;	 and it should be a surgical fire cautery, and trim down the thickness of the edges.
et se li malaides sent que li dolor s’estende jusc’a dois dou piet ou pres d’enqui, se le cauterize la ou il sent la dolor III poins ou IIII au cautere qui est apelez «poins».	 and if the patient feels that the pain extends to two fingers' width from the sole of the foot or near it, then make the fire cautery at where they feel the pain three times or four times on what is called "points" cauterization.
Et se mestiers est, se li en fai plus;	 And if surgery is needed, if there are more problems;
et se il seit que li dolor soit desoz le genoil vers la cuisse, se li fais cautere au cautere cutellaire ou circulaire, et te done bien garde en tous tes cauteres que tu n’i lassier mie tant le cautere que tu brules les ners et les grans arteres, et que tu ne faices au malaide plus grant nuisance et contraction.	 And if it is known that the pain extends from the groin to the thigh, then you shall perform a caustery or circular cauterization with a heated iron and take good care in all your cauteries not to harm either the nerves or large arteries, ensuring no further distress or contraction for the patient.
Et je meisme ai veus plusors qui ont fait cautere sus la cheville dou piet, et li lasserent tant que li jambe fut toute enflee, et li piez ausi, et fut perciez et corrumpus toz li piez.	 And I have seen some who made cauterizations above the ankle on the foot, and they rested until the entire leg was consumed by it, with the feet in a similar condition, which were pierced and all the flesh corrupted.
Aprés une solution de ventre dont il ot la mort.	 After a treatment of belly where there was death.
Et se li dolors est en II parties ensamble, fai cautere en l’une et en l’autre, selonc ceste maniere.	 And if the pain is in two parts together, make a fire treatment on one and the other according to this manner.
Et li saige dirent en la cautere de la hainche, de coi ci est li maniere, fai I tel fer et soit au chief ausi gros com uns nauvillon de dacte, ou un poc moins, et soit par entrechetres et soit des l’un entrechetres jusc’a l’autre d’espaice la quantiteit d’un nou de poce;	 And the sage advises in the cautery of the haunch: make an iron rod as large as a small nail or slightly smaller, and it should be spaced apart so that the quantity between each is equivalent to the length of a pea.
et soient li entrechetres aovers de II pars, et soient aussi comme noez, et i ait I mainche de fer bien fait;	 And let there be hooked pivots over two parts, and they are also like nails, with one iron handle well made.
et c’est li forme:	 and it is the form:
Et soit eschaufez tant qu’il soit toz rouges et giete senteles, et puis le mette on sus la boiste de la hainche malaide, et soit tornez sus lou sain costeit;	 And let it be cooled until all is red and blistered without moisture, then place it under the box of the bad elbow joint, and turn it towards the strong side.
et lou cauterize une fois I cautere reont et lou laisse III jors;	 and apply the cautery once with a fire-cautery and leave for three days;
et puis fai emplaustre de burre, et laisse la plaie aoverte lonc tens;	 then make an ointment of butter, and leave the open wound exposed for long periods.
aprés la cure d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez.	 after the treatment with salve until it is healed.
Albucasim dit que nos usons poc de cest cautere por la paor de son regart, et se voions poc qui en usent;	 Albuquerque says that we seldom use this type of cautery due to fear of its appearance, and few practice it.
et toutevoie ceu est des boins cauteres, qui le puet soffrir, et lai ou il s’afiert.	 And indeed this is of good cauteries, which can suffer it, and where it presses into.
Li cauteres de medicine ardant si est que tu faices I estrument a entrechetres en coi dessende li marge de la porte, et soit d’arain ou de fer a une paroit longe, et en la hautece ait II nous, et ait entre chaicun la quantiteit de la groissece d’un doi;	 The cauterization of medicine by fire is such that you make an instrument with pincers to descend the edge of the wound, and it should be made of iron or brass of one width, and in height have II (2) notches, and between each have the amount of the thickness of a thumb.
et soient overt defuer et desus, et se joignent ensamble selonc ceste forme:	 And they are to be above-cut and below, and joined together according to this shape:
Aprés met sus la boiste de la hainche au malaide gisant sor suin costeit sain, et apresse ta main mout sus la boiste de la hainche;	 After placing the bag of the thigh above the patient lying on his good side, and press your hand much upon the bag of the thigh.
aprés giete entre les II cercles de l’awe chaude qui soit chaufee au feu I poc, et li laisse une houre dou tens, et soffre li malaides la chalor et l’arsure de li.	 After pouring between the II circles of the hot iron which is heated in the fire a bit, and let it remain for an hour at a time, and cause the patient to suffer the heat and burning from them.
Car il i trueve mordication ausi com de feu;	 In its place, there is a burning pain like from fire;
et quant li mordications iert passee, se lieve ta main avec l’estrument et leve la hainche d’awe douce, et laisse ensi III jors, et met sus burre tant que ceu qui est noir de l’eschaudure soit osteit;	 And when the mordication is completed, gently lift the limb with the instrument and raise it softly, leave so for three days, and apply butter until what appears black from bruising turns white.
et lou laisse III jors que porriture en istrait;	 And let it remain strained for three days to heal properly;
et ceu serait li derriene aide aprés le cure d’oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez.	 This is the final aid after applying ointments until it becomes healthy.
Et se li dolor s’est estendue jusc’a la cuisse ou jusc’a la jambe, se li fai I estrument que teigne awe selonc ceu que tu as fait en la hainche igaument;	 And if the pain extends to the thigh or leg, make an instrument similar to what you did for the limb evenly;
et c’est li maniere de l’awe chaude, et je l’ai escripte ou traitier de la rectification de medicine.	 This is how one makes a warm poultice, which I have written or treated in the treatise of medical correction.
Pren alcali et chaulz vive, autant de l’une com de l’autre, et les broie ensamble, et les met en I nuef pot.	 Take soda and quicklime, an equal amount of each, grind them together, and put into a new jar.
ou il ait I petit pertuis defuer se que li pointe d’un raisor i puisse entreir;	 When there is a small opening not fitting, so that the point of an arrow may enter.
et met desor celui pot I autre pot bien plombeit, et met sus alcali et chalz et awe douce sus, tant qu’il en i ait I doi desus les poudres cant tu l’avras bien preingte a ta main;	 And put on him who can be well bandaged, and apply honey, salt, and soft warmth upon it, so that after two days you have thoroughly prepared the powders.
et le laisse ensi tant qu’il en dessende awe ague et chiece ou pot plombeit, puis pren toute cele awe, et la giete sus chalz et sus alcali si com devant.	 And leave it thus until it exudes pus and can be well bandaged, then take all the warmth, and pour it upon salt and alkali as before.
Et lors si sera mout ague et est aministree en mou d’ovraiges de medicine et en cauteres d’autres membres.	 And when this is very pus-filled, it will be treated with the bread of medicinal ointments and other members' fire cauterizations.
Car elle fait auteil oevre com feus, et si a autres medicines dont on cauterize bien la hainche ensi com tesisie et miel anacardi et chalz avec savon, toutes ces choses mellees ensamble.
