Because it does other work as fuses, and with other medicines that one well-cauterizes the joints as in syrup and honey of cashew nuts and salt with soap, all these things mixed together.
Et Galiens nos raconte une cure dont uns hons fut curez de la dolor de la hainche et de la voine sciatique, et lou loe mout, et dit que on n’i fist autre cure, et qu’il en fut sanez a une soule fois quant on ot fait ceste cure, et il se fut baigniez si com il l’enseigne ci aprés.	 And Galien tells of a case where a gentleman was healed from ankle pain and sciatic nerve, which greatly troubled him; and said that no other treatment was given to it but with this cure, and the patient recovered once for all when this cure was done as instructed hereafter.
Et dist en teil maniere que tu preignes dou litargire vert fres et sec, et le broie mout avec I poc de graisse, et met sus la hainche et sus la cuisse et sus la jambe ou la dolor tient, et la lie;	 And he said in that manner you pluck the fresh and dry lettuce leaves, and crush them well with a little fat, and apply to the hip and thigh and leg where the pain is, and wrap.
et li laisse III houres et par la quantiteit que li malaides ne sente plus l’arsure.	 And let it remain for three hours or until the amount that the sick person no longer feels the burning sensation.
Et puis le fai entrer ou bain tant que li cors li soit un poc arousez, et lou fai entrer ou lit, et li dolor s’en ira toute et sera sanez.	 And then he makes him take a bath until the body is somewhat revived, and he makes him enter bed, and the pain will go away entirely and be soothed.
Et saiches que nuls ne doit user de cautere de telz medicines, se ceu n’est aprés l’evacuation de cors.	 And know that no one should use fire cautery with such remedeby unless after the evacuation of bodily fluids.
Et Dyascorides dist que quant li voine sciatique est cauterizee de fiens de chievre, si i aide mout;	 And Dioscorides said that when the sciatic nerve is cauterized with goat fat candles, it greatly helps.
et doit estre fais li cauteres en teil maniere.	 and it must be done as follows:
Prenez lainne et la beurez d’oile vielz, et metez sus la fossete qui est entre le pouce dou piez et l’autre qui est apelez foscile.	 Take the bandage and moisten it with old oil, and place it over the hollow that is between the thumb and forefinger, which are called foscile.
Aprés pren fiens de chievre sec, et l’empren a feu tant qu’il soit charbons, et lou met sus la laine, et le laisse tant qu’il soit estains;	 After taking goat fat seco, and holding it in fire until it becomes ashes, and then applying to the wool, and leaving it until it is completely burnt out.
et refai encor ensi, et ne cesser de faire ensi tant que tu penses par sens qu’il viegne jusc’a la hainche, et que li dolor soit cessee;	 and do this again in the same way, and continue doing so until you think by touch that it reaches to the hip, and the pain is gone.
et cist manieres de cautere est apelez «cautere de chievre».	 And these methods of cautery are called "cauterization by goat.
de la dolor dou dos	Of the pain in the back
Quant dolor vient au dos, ou par cheoir ou de percussion ou par trop grant evacuation, ou par semblans de matiere espandue froide, a nule de ces semblances ne vaut cauteres, fuer que a celi qui vient de infusion de froide matiere.	When pain comes to the back, whether from falling or percussion or from excessive blood loss, or from similar matters of cold substance spreading, none of these cases call for fire cauterization; rather it is for those who have an influx of cold matter.
Il covient c’aprés ceu que li malaides est voidiez de pilules fetides ou d’autres semblans, que on li faice sus lou dos, lai ou li dolor tient, trois lignes signies d’enche, et en chescune ligne V cauteres ou plus selonc la vertut et la quantiteit que li malaides puet soffrir;	 After the patient has been relieved of foul pills or similar things, make three lines marked with crosses on their back where they feel pain, and in each line, make V cauteries or more according to the virtue and quantity that the patient can endure.
et soit fait li cauteres selonc le cautere qui est apelez «poins»;	 And the cauterizations should be done as per "points" type of cauterization;
et se tu vues, fai III cauteres ou IIII au cautere clavile moien selonc ceste forme:	 And if you see it, make III cauteries or IIII at the midpoint of the clavicle in this manner:
Maintes fois vient ceste maladie as petis enfans, et li signes de l’encomencement si est qu’il ont estroite alainne quant il se lievent, et paor;	 Often this disease comes to young children, and the signs at the beginning are that they have a narrow waist when they sit up, and fear.
et tu trueves en la derriene espinee dou dos et en nous l’apparance qui vient sus les autres espinees.	 And you find it at the last spine of the back, with its appearance that comes above the other spines.
Quant tu vois ceu et tu le vues curer, si le cauterize au cautere de celcle selonc ceste forme.	When you see this wound and observe it healing, then cauterize with a caustic cautery according to the following method.
Si que li cautere porpreigne chescune partie de l’espinee egaument.	 If the cautery can be used for each part of the spine equally.
Et se tu vues, si cauterize entor l’espinee au cautere poignant II lignes ou III, et soient li poins pres l’uns de l’autre.	 And if you see, using a fire caustic around the spine with a needle pricking two or three lines, and be the points near each other.
Aprés cure le leu tant qu’il soit sanez selonc ceu que nos avons dit, et warde que tu n’amenistrer cautere en gilbositeit qui soit en spame de nerf.	 After healing the limb so that it is smooth according to what we have said, and beware not to perform caustic in a spot where there are nerves.
de la dolor des jointes	For pain of the joints
Quant dolor de jointes sunt de moistors que sont espandues a chaicun membre dou cors, et quant dolor vient em piez, que li mire apelent «podagre» proprement, et quant elle est de froide cause et cures de medicines ne la puent curer, si est curez par cauteres en teil maniere:	 When joint pains are from moistness that has spread to every part of the body, and when pain comes on in the feet, which they call "gout" properly, and when it is caused by cold and remedies cannot heal it, then it is treated with cauldrons as follows:
fai li mout de cauteres entor la jointure dou piet, et soit li cauteres olivaire selonc ceste forme:	 Make the mouth of the cauldron around the joint of the foot, and let the cauldron be olive-shaped as follows:
Et s’il i a besoigne que tu poignes sus la faice dou piet, se li fai cautere a tot le cautere c’on claime «point».	 And if it is necessary to grasp above the face of the foot, make the caustic across all the area you claim "no point.
Et se les dolors viegnent jusc’a genous et as autres jointures, et ceu avient maintes fois, se li fai cautere sus chaicun genoil III cauteres ou IIII de chescunne partie, a tout le cautere olivaire;	 And if the pains come up to the knee and other joints, which happens often, then make cauldrons on each third (III) or fourth (IV) of every part, with all the olive-shaped cauldron.
et se tu as mestier de plus, si en fai plus, mais n’i tenir mie ta main fuers que tant que li espés dou keur soit ars.	 And if you need more, do so, but do not hold your furred hand until the point is bent.
Et se les dolors dessendent jusc’a genoil et au dos, se li aministre le cautere que nos avons dit en son chapistre.	 And if the pains extend to the knees and back, administer the fire cautery as we have mentioned in its chapter.
Et se les dolors sunt as mains, si fai poins entor le foscile II lignes;	 And if pain is in the hands, make points around the small lines twice.
et s’il remaint point de dolor as dois, si fai poins sus chescune jointe et sus lou poil de la main;	 and if there is no more pain in the fingers, make points above each joint and on the hand's hair;
et se les dolors vienent jusc’as coutes ou jusc’as espaules, si cauterize chescune partie, et fai boin governement au malaide et penre medicines.	 and if pain comes near the edges or shoulders, cauterize each part, provide good care to the patient and give them appropriate remedies.
Car se tu li fais boin governement et tu purges fleume, si sera saneis a l’aide de Deu.	 For if you provide good care and purge phlegm, he will be healthy with God's help.
de la routure dou syfac	Of sore festering
Quant routure vient en angres, et li bouelz dessendent as coions et c’est novelement, si covient que quant tu lou vues curer, qu’il ne menjuce mie celui jor;	 When inflammation comes between the fingers and they swell down to the knuckles anew, it is necessary that when you see them healed, you do not use the affected hand for a day.
et qu’il use choses qui laichent lou ventre, si que li fiens dessende de son ventre;	 And use things that stimulate the belly, so that the fetus descends from its abdomen.
aprés le fai seoir sus son dos entre tes mains, et li comande qu’il teigne son alaine tant que li boueil soient repairiet, et les ramoinne a tes dois, et seigne d’enche desoz la routure sus l’os dou poignil, et a tout un signe que soit semblans a la moitiet d’un cercle a desus dou cors;	 After the child has sat on its back between your hands, and command it to warm its ankle until the vein is repaired, and bend the joints at your wrists, and insert fingers into the ear canal, as if making half of a circle above the body.
puis eschaufe le cautere de coi ci est li forme:	 Then prepare the fire cauldrone whose shape is this:
tant qu’il soit blans et qu’il giete senteles.	 until it is white and secretes serum.
Puis ramoine les bouels a lor leu;	 Then reset the veins to their place;
et li ministres teigne sa main sus qu’il ne retornent arrier;	 And let the minister warm his hand so that it does not return backward;
et oevre bien les cuisses au malaide, et met desoz lui I cussin et I serjant sus les cuisses, et I autre sus lou pis qui li teigne les mains;	 Work well on the patient's thighs and place a pillow and bandage under them, and another over the buttocks where he warms his hands.
puis met le cautere sus lou signe a tout ta main, et lou tien droit et lou tien tant que tu ateignes l’os, et se tu ne l’ateins la premiere fois, si le rencomence encor une autre tant que tu viegnes jusc’a l’os;	 Then place the cautery over the sign with all your hand, and hold it straight and firm until you reach the bone, and if you don't reach on the first attempt, try again another time until you get to the bone.
et te warde subtilment que li boueil ne saille quant tu fais lou cautere;	 and be careful that the boil does not burst when making the cautery.
que tu ne le brulasses;	 so you do not burn it.
et que par ceu li malaides ne muere, ou autre malz.	 and by this, the patient does not die or suffer other ills.
Et saiches que quant tu ne viens jusc’a l’os au cautere, tes ovraiges ne vaut rien.	 And know that when you do not reach the bone with the fire cautery, your work is of no value.
Et covient que li cauteres des enfans soit subtilz selonc la mesure d’ous, et des grans gens aussi grans selonc lor mesure;	 And it is necessary that the cautery for children be subtle according to their size, and for large people also appropriate to their size.
aprés III jors cure lou leu dou cautere de burre tant que li eschaudure soit ostee;	 After three days heal the wound from the cautery with butter until the burn is healed.
aprés le cure d’autres oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez, et gise li malaides XL jors sus son dos tant que li plaie soit bien soudee;	 After treating with other salves until it is healed, and apply 40 drops of oil to the patient's back as long as the wound is properly closed.
et covient que ses norrissemens soit lassatis longement, si que li boueil ne saillent quant il se preigdra d’aler en chambres.	 And it is necessary for his extremities to be well-stretched, so that the veins do not protrude when he attempts to stand and walk into a room.
Et aprés XL jors, quant il se voudra lever, se li amenistre une faixe bien faite, et la porse XL autres jors;	 And after ninety days, when he wishes to get up, prepare him with well-made bandages and keep them on for another ninety days.
et ait boin repos, qu’il se travaille poc et se warde de trop grant repletion de boivre et de mengier, et de trop haut braire;	 And he should have good rest, work little, and avoid excessive drinking and eating, as well as too loud shouting.
et quant il fait cest enseignement si est sanez entierement.	 And when this teaching is completed, it will be entirely healed.
Et je dirai ci aprés la cure de taillier en son chapistre.	 And I will now describe the treatment of tailor in this chapter.
de la routure dou ventre	Regarding the routine care of the abdomen
Quant routures vienent en autres ventres et sont connisans, et tu vues qu’elles ne croissent plus, se li fai I cautere dou cautere reont selonc sa quantiteit, et soit ars li tiers dou keur;	 When ulcers come in other bodies and are known to him, and you see that they no longer grow, he makes a fire cautery according to the amount needed, and it should be one-third of their size.
aprés le cure selonc ceu que nos avons dit;	 Afterward, as we have said;
et aucun des anciens ont dit c’on le doit cauterizer au cautere a III angles selonc ceste forme:	 and none of the old ones have said that it should be cauterized with fire caustics at three angles according to this form:
mais signe premier le leu d’enche et fai une ligne per la largesce desus la routure, et une autre defuers, et main ta main emmi a tout le cautere clavile.	 But mark the first incision and draw a line for width above the tumor, and another below it, and keep your hand steady during the entire procedure of the scalpel blade.
Mais li premiers cauteres est plus legiers et muedres.	 However, the first incision is lighter and easier to make.
de dolor anciene en aucun membre	from old pain in any limb
Quant dolor vient en aucun membre, ou de cheoir ou de ferir, et cele dolor tient lonc tens, et li cure de medicine n’i vaut, adonc covient qu’il soit cauterizeis au cautere qui est apelez «poins», et soit li cauteres selonc la longesce dou membre et la petitece et sa foibleteit et sa vertut et sa location de torcions et de sa dolor.	 When pain comes to any limb, whether from falling or being struck, and this pain lasts a long time, and the cure of medicine is not effective; then it must be treated with cautery called 'poins', which should be applied according to the length, size, weakness, virtue, location of torsions, and its pain.
s’il est sanez dou premier cautere, c’est bien;	 if it is safe after the first cautery, it is well;
se ceu nom, recomence I autre cautere sus celui, car teilz costume est qu’il se doit muer au membre que li est prochiens, por coi il covient que tu faices les cauteres tant que li malaides soit saneis.	 if not, start another cautery on that one, because it is customary for the affected member to heal where it is close, so it must be done with caustics until the patient recovers safely.
de meselerie	Of healing art
Li meseil sont aidiet aucune fois par cautere par grant aide, et meismement li maladie que vient de la putrefaction de fleume et de melancolie.	 The measures have been eased at times by caustics greatly; especially the diseases that come from the putrefaction of humors and melancholy.
Cant tu la vues cauterizer, pren warde se li maladie est au comencement, et s’ele est curee selonc ceu que nos avons dit en la division, et ne dessent ne ne demoure, et tu doutes que li corruption ne porpreigne tout le malaide, adonques li fai V cauteres sus lou chief:	 If you can see it being cauterized, take care if the disease is at the beginning and has been treated according to what we have said in division, and neither descends nor ascends, and you doubt that corruption will infect the whole body, then make five caustics on its head:
I emmi le chief a nouf, et l’autre vers lou front a la fin des chevous;	 I insert the knife at the nape of the neck, and the other towards the forehead near the ends of the hairs.
et II sus les II cornes, et I derrierre sus le haiterel;	 And it goes behind the two horns, and then in front of the occipital bone.
et i laise tant ta main que li cauteres viegne jusc’a l’os, et tant que les escorces en issent fors si que les vapors des grosses humors s’en puissent issir;	 And let the hand rest so that the cautery reaches just to the bone, and as long as scabs form on it, such that the vapors of thick humors can escape.
et le cauterize sus la mice selonc ce qu’il est devant.	 And then cauterize around the wound according to what is in front.
Et se li meselerie est partout esparse;	 And if the infestation is scattered everywhere;
et elle pert manifestement, si covient que tu lou cauterizes de ces cauteres que nos avons dit ou chief, et I cautere en som lou neis, et II cauteres sus l’espinee dou col, et VI cauteres sus l’espinee dou dos, et I grant sus la crupie et I autre delez, et II sus les II espaules;	 And it is clearly evident, therefore you must cauterize with these cauteries that we have mentioned above: and the first of them at the collarbone, and another two on the spine down the neck, and six along the spine of the back, one large one on the loins and another near it, and two on each shoulder.
et II sus les coutes, et II sus les tendrons dou pis, et I sus chascune jointe des mains et des piez, et sus les fosses des mains;	 and two on the elb cuisses, and two on the tendons of the feet, one over each joint in hands and fingers, and above the palm pits.
et te warde des ners que sunt sus lou derrien calcant, que tu ne les bruler;	 and beware of the veins that lie behind them, do not burn them.
et aucune fois fait om cautere sus l’os dou poignil, et I autre sus l’os de l’estomac, et I autre sus lou foie.	 and never perform a cautery on the bone of the wrist, nor one on the bone of the stomach, nor another on the liver.
Et saiches que quant plus i fais de cautere, plus li fais d’aide, et mues li profite;	 And know that the more you perform cautery on it, the more you help it heal, and the better it benefits.
et saiches que li malaides ne sent point de dolor au cautere si com li sain le sentent, por ce que li cors est ja toz corrumpus.	 And know that the patient does not feel pain from the cautery as healthy ones do, because their body is already completely corrupted.
Et covient ke li cautere soient grant et petit selonc les membres et les jointures, selonc ceu que vos lou troverez en manieres des fers.	 And it must be that cautery be large and small according to the limbs and joints, as you will find in handling iron tools.
Aprés cure lou leu de farine de veces avec miel et autres cures tant qu’il soit saneis.	 After curing him of his illness with wheat flour mixed with honey and other remedies until he is healthy again.
Quant enfleure vient en aucun membre et est curee par medicines et oiles et emplastres, et il n’est mie sanez, adonques li fai cauteres sus le membre selonc la grandour et la petitece dou membre;	 When swelling comes to any limb and is treated with medicines, oils, and poultices, but it is not healthy, then you perform cautery on the limb according to its size and magnitude.
et soit li cauteres un poc entrans en l’espés dou keur;	 and make the cautery a little incision near where the swelling is.
puis le cure d’oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez.	 then treat it with ointments until it becomes healthy.
Et aucune fois fait on cautere et a la main et au piet et au dos, a l’issue dou nerf que muet le membre, et ensi si est ostee li enfleure;	 And never perform cautery and on the hand or foot or back, at the site where the nerve moves the limb, and thus is swelling present.
et toutevoie ne s’en entremette nuls s’il n’est conoissans des membres et des issues des ners movans lou cors.	 And in any case, it does not interfere with anyone unless one is familiar with the members and the pathways of moving nerves within the body.
de albaras	The practice known as 'albaras' involves applying a heated iron or substance to the skin, creating cauterization that closes wounds, removes growths, or stops bleeding by sealing blood vessels through heat coagulation.
Quant li maladie qui est apelee «albaras» est enveillie, et li engien de medicine n’i valent rien, adonques le cauterize d’un cautere un poc parfont, selonc la quantiteit de l’espés dou keur, tant que li blenchour soit ostee, et soit muee sa color;	 When the disease known as "albaras" is old and medical remedies are of no avail, then cauterize with a hot iron somewhat superficially, according to the amount of heat desired such that the blister is raised, and its color changes.
puis le cure de farine de veces et de lentilles avec oile roset et foilles de plantain, et sanc de colon et sanc d’alondre, de chescun une partie;	 Then apply a poultice of flour and lentils with rose oil and plantain leaves, along with the blood of conies and that of swans, each in equal parts.
et soit mellez tout ensamble, et soit liiez d’un drapel, et soit aers au leu tant qu’il soit sanez.	 And mix everything together well, bind it with a cloth, and apply heat to the area until it is healed.
li cure de chancre par cautere	The treatment of ulcers through cauterization
Quant chancre vient au comencement, et tu lou vues arrester, si le cauterize au cautere qui semble I cercle, tout entor au tour dou chancre.	 When a cancer begins to develop, if you wish to stop it, cauterize with the cautery in the form of a circle all around the tumor.
Et toutevoie li saige dirent que on faice cautere ausi au mileu dou chancre;	 And yet, wise ones say to make a fire cautery like with gonorrhea.
et toutevoie ceu ne me semble mie boin, car je redous que il ne soit ulcerez et corrumpus, et je l’ai ja veut avenir aucune fois;	 And yet, I do not think it is good either, for I have seen that it can become ulcerated and corrupted, and I have never wanted to use it before.
et plus droituriere chose est qu’il soit cauteriés entor, au cautere qui est apelez «circule», si com nos avons dit en mout de cauteres.	 A more correct thing is that they should be treated with fire inside, the caustic called "circulation", as we have said in many of caustics.
de l’enfleure qui ne puet meurer	For non-healing swellings that cannot be healed
Quant aucuns ait une maladie qui est apelee «adubelati», et elle tarde de meurer ou por la superfluiteit qu’ele fait ou por l’eaige dou malaide quant il est decrepites (c’est a dire trop vielz) et il a poc de sanc, ou por lou tens;	 When some have an illness called "adubaillite", which causes them to die quickly or due to the excess it produces or from the sickly appearance when they are elderly and have little blood, or for their time.
et tu la vues haster de meurer:	 And you will see him hastening to die.
adonques le cauterize entor de mout de petis cauteres en poignant;	 Then, accordingly caulk around with many small cauterizations by pricking;
aprés le laisse ensi.	 After that, leave it so.
Car elle se hastera de meureir.	 It will delay dying.
Et se tu la vues percier a tout le cautere, si chaufe le cautere de coi ci est li forme:	And if you see the entire area with caustics, heat the area where the shape is:
Et met ta main en mileu de cele maladie qui est apellee «adubelati» tant que li cauteres ait perciet lou keur, et soit telz li cauteres que li malaides lou sente defuers en teil maniere que li cours de la porriture soit alegis.	 And insert your hand into the illness called "adubelati" until you feel the heat of the cautery, and make such cauteries that the sick person feels behind in a way that the course of purification is adjusted accordingly.
Aprés le cure tant qu’il soit sanez parfaitement.	 Afterwards treat it until it becomes perfectly healthy.
li cure dou feu par fer	The care of fire with iron
Une autre maniere de maladie i a qui est apelee «corrodens», et n’est autre chose que une mengeson de membre, car ele menjut les membres ausi com li feus les leignes seches.	 Another way of illness there is called "corrodens," and it's nothing but a mixture in the limb, because it eats away at the members as dry wood does with flames.
Se tu vois ceste maladie en leu qui puisse soffrir cautere ensamble feu, adonques eschaufe les cauteres clavile mout petit et grant, selonc ceu qu’il covient au leu ou li maladie est;	 If you see this disease in place that may suffer caulking with fire together, then soak the caulk both small and large as required by where the ailment or location is.
aprés le cauterize de toutes pars tant que tu erraiche toute la corruption, et nen remaigne rien de li, que tout ceu qui est corrumpus ne soit osteit.	 After caulking all parts until you have removed the entire corruption, and nothing remains of it, that all which is corrupted be pulled out as bone.
Et puis le laisse III jors, et met sus les leus cauterizez soffre broiet avec oile tant que les eschaudures dou feu soient ostees, et toute li corruption.	 And then let it rest for three days, and apply poultices with oil until the burns from fire are healed, and all the corruption is gone.
Aprés lou cure d’oignemens engendrans char.	 After applying the ointment causing heat.
Et se tu vois aprés III jors que chars saine ne naisse, c’est boin;	 And if after three days no fresh flesh appears, this is good;
et se ceu non, si rencomence le cautere sus ceu qui est demoreit des leus corrumpus.	 and if not, then resume caulking over what remains of the corrupted veins.
Et ceste mengeson est aucune fois esteit curee de medicine ague en leu de cautere de feu;	 And this mengeison is sometimes treated with cold medicines at the site of fire cautery.
mais toutevoie cautere de feu est de plus grant aide, et j’ai ja dit la cure de la medicine ague en la division:	 However, fire cautery is of greater aid, and I have already discussed the treatment with cold medicines in its application:
pren la quant tu en as mestier.	 Take what you need.
des porrelz qui vienent as piez	Cords or strings that come to the fingers
Mout de fois avient que as piez par defuers naist une maladie qui est apelee «clos» selonc nostre entencion, et est une grosse chose fautree qui blece lou piet.	 Often there occurs that in the feet, from behind, a disease emerges which we call "closed," and it is a large growth that afflicts the foot.
Et li cauteres de ceste maladie si est selonc II manieres.	 And the cautery for this illness is done in two ways.
C’est a savoir cautere de feu, et cautere d’aigue chaude.	 It is known as fire cautery and hot water cautery.
Cautere de feu si est que tu eschaufe I cautere cheveit ausi com est une penne de vouteul, et soit fait de boin fer a la mesure qu’il puisse porpenre le clou de toutes pars, et qu’il i ait subtilz marges;	 Fire cautery is such that you should heat it like an earthen cone and make it of good iron to pierce the nail entirely, and that it has subtle edges.
aprés le met tout chaut sus lou clou, et torne ta main tot entor le clou tant qu’il viegne au font dou clou;	 After heating all around the nail, turn your hand completely around the nail until it feels cool at the tip of the namen.
et lou laisse ensi III jors tant qu’il encomence giter porriture;	 and leave it as such for three days until it begins to develop pus.
puis li fai un emplaustre de malves savaiges broiies avec seil, et laisse l’emplaustre sus toute la nuit, et li clous cherra et sera desracinez de ses racines.	 Then make an emplaster of well-ground barley soaked in water, and leave the poultice on throughout the night, then the thorn will draw out and be uprooted from its roots.
Puis cure le leu d’oignement enjanrant char tant qu’il soit sanez.	 Then treat the joint with an ointment until it is sound again.
Et s’il sont convertit par defuers lou cors, et maintes fois avient et en mains et em piez, si covient que tu i amenistres cautere d’aigue chaude;	 And if they are turned to the back of the body and often occur in hands and feet, it is necessary that you treat with a hot water cautery.
et est en teil maniere:	 and it happens this way:
pren une cainne d’arain ou de fer, ou une penne de vouteul, et met sus lou clou et l’althelul, c’est asavoir porrelz verrues;	 Take a vessel of pitch or iron, or the edge of a spade, and place it on the thorn and its sheath, that is to say for warts:
et met la cainne sus si qu’ele porpreigne tout entor, puis i met un poc d’awe chaude, et retien bien ta main, et presse ta main en tornant si que li marge de la cainne viegne a la racine dou clou, et puisse trover l’aigue chaude voie parfonde jusc’a la racine;	 and place the vessel so that it covers all around, then put a bit of hot water in it, hold your hand steady, and press with your hand while turning so that the edge of the vessel reaches to the root of the thorn, allowing the hot water to reach deep down to the root:
et soffre li malaides un poc la mordication de l’aigue chaude une houre;	 And suffer the patient a little from the biting of hot water for an hour.
puis le laisse ensi, et il se derracinera tous a tout ses racines.	 Then leave it so, and it will peel off completely at all its roots.
Ensi fai un aprés autre, tant que tu esraiches toz ces qui sont au cors, puis les cure des oignemens qui engenrent char.	 Thus do another after another, until you relieve all those that are in the body; then treat with anointments of fat.
li cure dou trembler	of the pen, which to make s le tissaz:
Quant aucuns tremble de froidor de ners, ou de fievre quartaine ou d’autre, si covient que tu li faices IIII cauteres ou IV sus l’espinee dou dos, I cautere entre chescune espinee;	 When anyone shivers from coldness or fever of a quarter day or other, it is fitting that you make four cauldrons on the backbone of their lower back, one between each vertebra.
et I cautere ou pez, et I sus l’estomac au cautere olivaire;	 and one at the chest as an olive cauldron;
si laissera lou trembler, et se hastera li santez de la maladie froide.	 it will leave them shivering, and their health from the cold disease will be restored.
des pustules puans	Of pus-filled pustules
Aucune fois apperent par defuers le cors bathes, ou pustules puans, que vienent de grosses matieres corrumpues.	 At no time is it apparent before the body has bathed or pustules filled with foul matter coming from large corrupted materials.
si covient au premier quant eles apperent que on faice cautere sus chescun chief de la pustule:	 if it is necessary in the first instance that you appear to make cauldrons above each head of the pustule:;
un cautere subtil de fust de mirte, de coi li pointe soit emprise au feu, ou de racine de aristologe longe, ou au cautere lenticulaire.	 A subtle fire cautery made of mister wood, where the tip is taken hold in flame, or from a long aristolochia root, or with a lenticular caustic.
Et aucune fois les cauterize on au comencement quant il aperent, selonc ceste maniere, et il ne puent croistre des enqui en avant, mais est desrompue li superfluitez dont il vienent, et sont sanez;	 And never apply a caustic at the beginning when they see it this way, and nothing can grow from there forward, but excess tissue is removed where it comes.
mais il covient que ceu soit fait aprés l’evacuation de sanc.	 But it must be done after blood evacuation.
quant li artere est copee	When the artery is harmed
Maintes fois avient grans decorremens de sanc de l’artere qui est copee a la plaie que vient au pardefuers, ou a l’incision de l’aposteme, ou au cautere dou membre, et as semblans choses;	 Many times there are great consequences of blood from an artery that is cut at the wound coming to the periphery, or in the incision of an abscess, or with a member caustic, and similar things.
et est mout grief chose d’estenchier.	 And it is a very grave thing to stop flowing.
Et toutevoie quant ceu avient a aucun, si te haste de mettre ton doi indice sus la plaie de la voinne, et l’estrain mout tant que li sans soit apaisiez desoz ton doi, et que goute n’en isse plus;	 Whenever this occurs with anyone, quickly place your index finger over the vein wound, and strain it very much until the blood has calmed under your finger, and no more oozes out.
puis met au feu les cauteres olivaire plusors petis et grans tant qu’il soient tuit rouge;	 Then apply fire to various small and large herbal cauterizations until they are all red;
puis empren I, ou grant ou petit selonc la plaie et lou leu en coi li artere est route, et met le cautere sus cele voine ou tu tiens ton doi, et tien le cautere tant sus que li sans soit restainchiez.	 Then take iron (I), either large or small depending on the wound and its location where the vein is cut, place the caution near the vein while holding your finger, and keep the caution in place until the bleeding stops.
Et s’il saut fuers quant tu lieves ton doi desus la voinne, et li cauteres estint, si pren hastivement .i. autre des cauteres qui sont au feu.	And if it leaps away when you lift your thumb over the vein, and the caustic is extinguished, then quickly take another from those heated near the fire.
Et ne cesser de faire ceu l’un aprés l’autre tant que li sans soit estenchiez;	 And continue doing so one after another until the bleeding has stopped;
et warde que tu n’ardes lou nerf qui est delez, et que autre malice ne viegne sus lou malaide;	 And beware that you do not burn the nerve nearby, and let no other harm come to the patient.
et saiches que quant sans decourt de l’artere, c’on ne lou puet mie bien restenchier meismement quant li artere est grans, se ceu n’est par une des IIII manieres que nos avons dit:	 And you know that when a vessel is cut without severing an artery, it cannot be properly sutured on its own if the artery is large unless by one of the four methods we have mentioned.
ou par cautere, ou par extraction quant ele n’est mie traite, ou par fort liement de fil, ou par medicines mises sus qui ont pooir de restenchier sanc;	 Or through cauterization, or by extraction if it is not treated in another way, or by strongly binding with thread, or by applying remedies that have the power to stop bleeding.
et soit liee et estrainte avennament.	 And thus tied and strained as needed.
Qui i amenistrera restenchement de liier estroitement de drapelz ou de metre choses ardans sus, ou autres semblans choses, se n’i profite se poc non.	Who will provide the tight binding with cloths or burning substances on it, or other similar things, if there is no good result.
Et se ce avient a aucun et il n’ait mie mire ne medicine present, si doit mettre son doi indice sus la plaie de la voinne si com nos avons dit, et bien estrendre tant qu’il soit restenchiez desus la plaie et desus la voinne;	 And if it happens to anyone and they have no remedy or medicine on hand, then they should put their index finger on the wound of the vein as we have said, and stretch it well until it is stopped above the wound and the vein.
et ne remuer lou doit, mais lou moille d’awe froide sovent que soit mout froide tant que li sans soit congelez et engrossiez et restenchiez;	 And it should not move, but apply cold wetness often enough that is very cold until the blood has congealed and thickened and rehardened.
et faice des enqui en avant ceu dont il a mestier de cauteres et de medicines.	 And make incisions as necessary for cauterization and application of medicine.
Ci encomence li secons livre des cures de taille	This begins the second book on wound suturing.
Nos vos avons dit ou premier chapistre toute maladie en coi il covient cautere de feu, ou de medicine ardans, et les oquisons et les causes et les estrumens et les formes des cauteres;	 We have told you in the first chapter about all diseases that require fire cauterization or burning medicines, and applications of ointments, plasters, powders, and forms of cauterizations.
et ai mis celui chapistre des lou chief jusc’a piez, et je irai en cest chapistre par celi meisme voie por ceu c’on trueve plus legierement ceu c’on voura.	 And I have placed that chapter regarding the upper body up to the feet, and I will proceed in this chapter by the same method so that it can be read more easily as desired.
Et ainsois que je encomence ceu, il covient, chier fil, que vos aprenez que en cest chapistre a plus de peril et de paor que ou premier des cauteres, et por ceu il covient plus grant cautele.	And so as I begin this section, it is necessary, dear son, that you learn in this chapter there is more danger and fear than with the first cauterization, and therefore greater care is required.
Car en l’ovraige de cest chapistre avient maintes fois evacuation de sanc a l’ovrir la voinne, et a l’incision sus aposteme, et as cures des plaies, et a l’estraction des saiettes, et a l’incision sus la piere, et les semblans choses;	 For in the work of this chapter, there is often evacuation of blood when opening a vein, and incision for an abscess, treatments for wounds, extraction of arrows, cutting into stones, and similar things.
ou il a doutance et paor, et en vient li mors a plusors.	 When there is doubt and fear, death comes to many.
Et je vos amoneste que vos n’entreprenez folie.	 And I advise you not to undertake foolishness.
Car mout de manieres de gens vienent en cures.	 For many methods of treatment come from people's experiences.
si vienent de telz qui s’aïrent si avec lor maladie qu’il muerent legierement por la forsenerie qu’il trueve de sa maladie, et de la grandour de son malice;	 If it comes from those who are so afflicted by their illness that they easily perish due to the severity and intensity of their sickness.
et de ces doit on avoir paor.	 And one should have fear for these.
Et de ces i a qui te done son sens, et dit:	 And among them are those who give up hope, and they say:
«atendez, je sui garis»;	 "Wait, I am healed;
et li maladie est despitouse.	 And the illness is resistant.
Il ne covient mie que vos vos consentez a ces qui vienent a vos qui ont ceste maniere, mais mettez plus grant cusanson en vostre honor qu’en vostre covoitise, et n’ovrez mie folement mais saigement de ceu dont vos estes certain, et dont vos poez avoir pris et los;	 It is not fitting for you to heed those who come seeking your aid with this manner of affliction, but rather put greater trust in your honor than in self-interest, and do not act rashly, but carefully from what you are certain and can reasonably acquire.
et usez de pronostication et de indication en cures de vos malaides a coi salus soit convertie;	 And employ prognosis and guidance in treating your patients to where health is restored.
et ceu vos aidera a aquester bone renommee, et gloire, et memoire de loenge.	 And this will help you achieve good reputation, glory, and memory among the people.
Tres chier fil, Nostres Sires vos doint boin entendement et droiture, et se vos vuelle espireir de la sainte inspiration de sa main, amen.	Three dear son, Our Lords grant you good understanding and righteousness, and if you wish to aspire from the holy inspiration of His hand, amen.
Or je vos ai ordeneit cest chapistre en devisant par chapistres, selonc ceu qu’il est devant ou chapistre des cauteres, que je vos ai deviseit des le chief jusc’a piez, por ceu que vos trovez plus legierement ceu dont vos avrez mestier.	Or I have ordered this treatise by chapters as I discussed in the previous chapter about cautery, from head to feet, so that you may find more easily what you need.
dou chief plein d’aigue	Full of water, headache
Saiches que ceste maladie vient mout de fois as enfans a l’enfanter, et quant li baille estraint trop fort le chief de l’enfant;	 Say that this illness often arises in children during birth, and when too much force is applied to the child's head.
et aucune fois vient ceu de cause reponue que on ne seit.	 and never comes from a reason unknown to us.
Et je ne vis onques ceste maladie fuers qu’en enfans, et a toz ces que j’ai veus se hastait li mors;	 And I have never seen this disease occur outside of children, and in all those cases death was swiftly upon them.
et por ceu me semble qu’il me vaut mues lassier l’ovraige en teilz cures.	 and therefore it seems to me that I should focus more on early treatments.
Et je vis I enfant de coi li chiés estoit plains d’aigue, et li chief engroissoit chescun jor tant qu’il ne lou pooit sostenir;	 And I saw a child whose head was full of water and the skull grew larger each day until it could no longer be supported.
et crut tant li moistor qu’il fut mors, et ceste moistor si est assemblee desoz l’os sus lou syphac, entre lou keur et l’os;	 And it was so much moisture that they died, and this moisture is gathered from under the bone above the shoulder blade, between the flesh and the bone.
et li ovraiges si est telz se li moistor est entre lou keur et l’os, et li apostemes est petis, que tu fendes emmi lou chief une fendure large;	 And such treatments are this: when the moisture is between the flesh and the bone, and the abscesses are small, then you shall make a wide incision into the head.
et soit ausi longe com II nous, tant que li mostor corre;	 And it should be as long as we tell you, until the moisture recedes.
et vez ci la forme dou spatumile:	 and here is how to shape the splint:
Se li moistor est plus creue, et li aposteme soit plus grans, si fai .ij. fendures en maniere d’une croix, selonc ceste forme:	If there is excessive moisture, and the abscess becomes larger, make two incisions shaped like a cross, following this form:
Et se li moistor est desoz l’os, et li signes que tu vois les commissures dou chief overtes de chescune partie, et li aigue saut fuer quant tu la presses de ta main au dedens, et ceu ne t’est mie reponut:	 And if the moisture is from under the bone, and the signs that you see are openings on each side of the head, and the liquid gushes out when you press it with your hand inside, and this does not restore them:
si covient que tu fendes enmi lou chief III fendures selonc ceste maniere:	 If it is necessary, you must make two cuts within the head as follows:
Et aprés l’incision estrai la moistor toute fuers.	 And after the incision, all moisture is removed completely.
Aprés estraint les fendures de drapelz et de poudres, et i met vin et oile, et laisse ensi jusc’a cinquieme jor;	 After making the gashes for bandages and powders, apply wine and oil, and leave as such until the fifth day.
puis le deslie, et cure la plaie par tentes et par oignemens, et laisse estraindre le chief egaument, et done mengier au malaide viande seche de poc de moistor tant que li membre soit confortez et sanez.	 Then let it heal, and treat the wound with bandages and ointments, allowing the head to be properly aligned and have the patient consume dry meat with a little moisture until the limb is comforted and healthy.
Et une autre maniere d’incision est que tu regardes ou apert li grandor de l’aposteme, et li assemblé de l’aigue;	 And another way of incision involves examining whether there are any signs of an abscess or pus collection.
car aucune fois est elle devant;	 because it should never be present.
aucune fois derrier;	 also, it should never be behind.
aucune fois en destre;	 and not on the right side either.
et aucune fois en senestre.	 And never to the left side.
Taille donques lai ou li aposteme apert, et l’emplissement de l’aigue, et lou fent selonc ce que tu en as le pooir;	 Therefore cut where the abscess opens and fill with water, and follow accordingly as much as you are able.
et warde que tu ne coper l’artere;	 and be careful not to obstruct the artery;
et veigne flun de sanc, si que li malaides muere dou decorrement de sanc et de l’evacuation de moistor.	 and watch for blood flowing out, so that the patient may die from the loss of blood and evacuation of moisture.
de reume	Of restoration
Quant il avient a aucun une maladie qui est apelee «catarre» as eulz ou au pis, et li maladie est anciainne, et li cure de medicine ne profite mie, adonques li derraine cure si est li cauteres avec ceu c’on li copera les .ij. arteres.	When a disease called "catarrh" occurs in the eyes or groin and has been present for some time, and medical treatment proves ineffective, then the subsequent remedy is the fire cautery with which one ties off the two arteries.
Il covient donques, cant tu les vues coper, que li malaides faice rere son chief;	 It is then necessary, when you see it obstructed, that the patient raises his head backward;
aprés li frotte lou leu d’un drapel aspre tant que les arteres aperent, puis estraingne li malaides son col a tout I drapel;	 after rubbing the area with an abrasive cloth until the arteries appear, then pull out all of the patient's collar with it.
puis regarde ou li voine bait, et li leus de l’une et de l’autre sont aprés les oreilles, et poc sont reponues;	 then look where the vein is above, and both sides are behind the ears, and few return to them;
puis signe les leus d’enche, puis cope l’une et l’autre d’un spatumile agut de II pars, tant que li taille veigne jusc’a l’os, et ceu soit par lou large dou chief.	 Then sign the ends of the bone, then wrap one and the other with a strip of linen about two fingers wide, as long as it reaches the bone, and cut across broadly at the head.
Et se tu vues, boute le spatumile desoz l’artere et la cope au desus, en taillant ausi com .ij. dois au traver.	And if you see this, take the gut strip off from above the artery and tie it upwards as two fingers across.
Et quant li voinne est copee, si saut li sans en haut continuelment fuers.	And when the vein is opened, let it bleed continuously upwards.
Et se li artere n’apert au sentir, si covient que tu mesures la quantiteit de l’espaice de III dois, puis seigne d’enche et fent jusc’a l’os;	 And if the arrow does not open upon feeling, it is necessary to measure three fingers' space and then apply a tourniquet up to the bone.
et ceu qu’il covient dou sanc mettre fuers si est VI c/, et par aventure un poc plus ou moins, selonc ce que li malaides puet soffrir, et la repletion de l’artere;	 and that much blood to be poured out if it is six ounces or so, depending on what the patient can endure, and the pressure in the artery.
puis regarde la plaie:	 then examine the wound:
s’il remaint sus l’os point dou syphac, si le cope que apostemes chaus n’i veigne, puis estrain la plaie et lie, et la cure d’oignement tant qu’ele soit sanee.	 if it remains above the bone without an exit channel, and no abscess forms within, then bandage the wound tightly and cleanse with ointment until healed.
de emigrainne	And when infection until is gone: let it up to cease; sirop dressez it syphon, and sew on after aseepistressure; as it untie the wound to treat with the syring.
Quant emigrainne anciaine vient, et catarre agut, por les moistors des larmes et les chalors en temples et sode anciene forsenee et semblans choses, et il est medicinez par manieres de cures de medicine et tout ceu ne li profite mie, si estraions les arteres des temples et lou cauterizons, si com nos avons conteit.	When migraine occurs early and with acute catarrh due to moisture from tears and heat in the temples and old headache, and medicine by methods of medical treatment does not help at all, we extract the arteries from the temples and cauterize them, as we have demonstrated.
Et li maniere de l’estraction d’elles si est que li malaides faice rere les poilz de ses temples, et entende a l’artere qui apert en la temple, car elle apert bien par son batement, et est poc reponue fuers que en aucuns homes qui sont trop froit;	 The method of extracting them is such that the patient braids his hair from the temples and listens to the artery opened in the temple, for it opens well by its pulsation, and heals quickly like some people who are too cold.
et s’elle est reponue, si estraigne son col li malaides d’aucuns drapelz, puis frote le leu d’aucun aspre drap, et arose le leu d’aigue chaude tant que li artere apere manifestement;	 If it heals, the patient should stretch their neck with some cloths, then rub the head with a rough towel, and apply warm water until the artery is clearly visible.
puis pren le spatumile de coi ci est li forme:	 Then take the spatula as follows:
puis escorche le cuir legierement tant que tu veignes a l’artere, puis la trai en haut as pinceures, et la depart bien des toiles que sont desoz li de chescune partie;	 Then lightly scrape the skin until you find the artery, then cut it at the nipples, and separate cleanly into pieces from each part.
et se li artere est subtilz, si la torne a la pointe de l’uncine, puis la cope de celle partie selonc la quantiteit des II chiés.	 And if the arrow is slender, turn it to the point of the hook, then wrap that part with a bandage according to the quantity of two fingers.
Car s’elle n’est copee, si ne saut mie li sans dou tout en tout.	 If it is not coped with, then there will be no relief at all for the wound.
Et trai dou sanc des VI c/, jusc’a III;	 And track down six pints of blood until three;
et se li artere est grans, si covient que tu la lies en II leus d’un fil double fort de soie, que porriture n’i veigne devant le soudement de la plaie, et veigne decorremens de sanc;	 And if the arrow is large, it must be tied with two loops of strong silk thread to prevent rotting at the wound site and bleeding as it heals.
puis cope la superfluiteit qui est entre les II liiens en celle houre meisme, et puis, se tu vues, si lou cauterize dou cautere cutellaire jusc’a l’os tant que li chiés soient copez;	 Then bandage the excess between the two loops with it at that same time, and then, if you see, use a cutting caustic until the bones are exposed.
et c’est li muedre oevre, se li malaides n’a fievre et il est de chaude complexion.	 This is the final work, as long as the patient does not have a fever and is of a warm constitution.
Car li cauteres est aide por finir les moistors:	 The fire cautery is used to finish up dampness:
por ceu est il de plus grant aide as moistors.	 For this reason, it is of greater help with dampness.
Ou il covient por l’estraction des arteres que om emplisse lou leu de viel coton et mette on sus tentes bien faites;	 Or when one must extract the artery, let them fill up that place with old cotton and put it under well-made slits.
et quant on les desliera, si soit curez de medicines seches que font naistre char, et de tentes, tant qu’il soit sanez;	 And when they are to be removed, then use dry medicines that produce heat and slits until it is healthy.
et se sans cort de l’artere tant dis com tu i oevres, si te haste dou coper par cautere, ou tu emple lou leu de vitriole et l’estrain a ta main que li sans soit estainchiez;	 And if from the artery there is much bleeding as you do so, then hasten to cover it with cautery, wherein you employ old urine and strain your hand that the wound be cleansed.
et se tu n’as ceu present, si met sor le leu ton doit tant que li sans soit congelez, et arose le leu d’aigue froide tant que li sans cesse, et soit estraint si com il covient;	 And if you do not have this on hand, then lay it there until the bleeding is clotted, and place cold water over that area until the bleeding stops, and strain as necessary.
et ceu qui est muedre et plus legier en l’estraction de l’artere est que tu cauterizes la voinne de cest cautere trenchant de II pars, mais li trenchant soient bien espés por warder plus longement lor chalor.	 And the one who is skilled and more agile in extracting arteries should use this fire cautery blade sharp on two sides, but the edge must be well honed to maintain heat longer.
Car quant li estrumens est trop tenves, si tient moins sa chalor.	When inflammations are too prolonged, they retain less heat.
Et doit avoir entre les II coutelz I doit de gros d’espaice, et puis quant tu as signiet d’enche les II leus, et tu mes lou fer ardant sus tant qu’il viegne jusc’a l’os, et cope la voinne en II leus;	 And it must have a space between the two blades, and when you are ready to use them, heat both blades until they reach the bone, and cut the vein in two parts.
et soient esloigniet entre les II chiés car il n’est mie soudez de cest cautere dou tout en tout;	 And be sure to separate them between the two sides because this fire cautery is not suitable for all cases.
et c’est li forme dou cautere:	 and here is the form of the fire cautery:
des larmes	Of tears
Quant les larmes des eulz sont dessendans des voinnes que sont sus lou test dou chief de fuer, et il ne profite mie cure de medicine c’on i faice, et tu vois la faice dou malaide enrougir, et sent ou front ambulation si com de fremis;	 When the tears of the eyes descend from veins located on the forehead above the eyebrows, and it does not benefit from any medicinal remedy applied there, you see the face of the sick person turn red, and their forehead tremble like with fear.
et sui oil sont tenve et moiste si que li poil des papieres sont cheut, et sont eschaufees les papieres, et escorchies de l’ardor des larmes, si ait mestier de ceste cure.	 And those wounds that are kept wet and warm so that the papers (skin) dry out, become swollen, and scorched from the heat of tears, if this treatment is needed.
Et l’apelerent li ancien «cure contuse», et est que tu faices a rere au malaide qui a ceste maladie les poilz qu’il ait ou front, puis li fai III fendures ou front igalment selonc la longesce dou front;	 And they called the ancient "contusion treatment", and so you make it over to the patient with this condition who has hair on his forehead, then you make three incisions or evenly according to the length of the forehead.
et soit l’une des fendures ausi com II doi tout emmi lou front en avalant aval jusc’a neif, et les autres II as II costelz par desus les papieres, et te garde de l’incision des arteres que sont as II costez par desus les papieres;	 and one of the incisions shall be like two fingers width into the forehead sloping down to the bridge (of the nose), and the others shall be twice a finger's breadth above the skin, being careful not to incise the arteries that are also twice a finger's breadth above the skin.
et aloigne ta main de la continuation des II mandibules, et soit chescune plaie la quantiteit de III dois au traver joins;	 And remove your hand from the extension of the two jaws, so that each wound is as much as three fingers in width.
et aies apparillie une piece d’esponge et mout de drapelz ses por essuer lou sanc, puis boute le spatumile agut de II pars de coi ci est li forme:	 And have prepared a piece of sponge and many cloths to wipe away the blood, then apply the sterile dressing with two parts of which this shape is.
des l’incision qui est dever la temple jusc’a la seconde incision;	 From the incision that extends from the temple down to the second incision;
et escorche tout le keur qui est entre les II fendures a tot lou syfac qui est sus l’os, puis fai autreteil des la moiene incision jusc’a l’autre seconde, et puis estrai fuer cest spatumile.	 And scrape off all the core that is between the two openings and remove it entirely from the sac which is above the bone, then make another section with the middle incision down to the other second, and then extract this sterile dressing.
si boute en la premiere fendure l’estrument qui est apelez «cultellaire», et est tresbien trenchans d’une part, et d’autre part est souef, ne mie trenchans, et c’est li forme:	If you insert the instrument called "culteral" into the first opening, and it is very sharp on one side but on the other side is smooth, not cutting. And that's its form:
Et met le costeit taillant vers la char aerse au keur, et lou costeit souef vers l’os, et lou boute tant qu’il veigne a la moiene fendure.	 And cut the ribs towards the chest near the curve, and make them smooth toward the bone, and push until it reaches the middle crack.
Et cope toz les vasselz que dessendent dou chief as eulz tant que l’incision soit continue jusc’a ceu qui apert dou keur, et puis autreteil fai en la moiene fendure jusc’a l’autre defuer;	 And remove all vessels that arise from the head until the incision is continuous to where the core opens, and then make another section in the middle opening down to the other end.
et puis estrai dou sanc igalment, et espresse lou leu por le sanc pris;	 Then remove the blood evenly, and express the site for the taken blood.
puis met en chescune fendure une tente de viel coton, et met sus drapelz moilliez en vin et en oile et en aisil, et garde que apostemes chaus n’i veigne;	 Then place in each wound a tent of fine cotton, and cover with cloths soaked in wine and oil and herbs, ensuring that abscesses do not form.
et au tier jor deslie lou liien, et i amenistre grant planteit d’aigue tede, puis lou cure d’oignement basilicon avec oile roset, et d’autres cures dont on cure plaies, tant qu’il soit sanez.	 and after three days leave the wound open, then apply a large amount of clean water, and treat with basil oil balm, and other remedies used for treating wounds, until it is healthy again.
dou reume des eulz	As for the eyes, they are blinded or do not see properly due to this condition.
Quant a aucun vienent catarre agut acostumeement, et tu vois les eulz tenves et petis, et afoiblir la veue, et les papieres brulees;	 When certain come with hardened habits, and you see the eyes swoln and small, and blurred vision, and burnt papers.
et li poil chieent, et ou chief en parfont a dolor ague, et li malaides esternue;	 and the hair falls out, and they have pain all over their head, and the patient sneezes.
adonques saiches par ces accidens que celles matieres et cil catharre ne vient fuer que de maintes voines, et li muedre cure que i est, si est ceste.	 Then you can say from these occurrences that those matters and the catarrh come only from various winds, and the moistener must treat there where it is.
Et est que tu comande au malaide a rere son front, puis fai une grant fendure emmi lou front, et une autre dou large I poc.	 And it is for you to instruct the patient to raise his forehead, then make a large cut near the center of the forehead, and another wide open hole.
Et comence des la fendure de la temple senestre a la temple destre, et soit li incision jusc’a l’os;	 And begin with an incision on the left temple to the right temple, and make the cut until the bone.
et esloigne ta main des ners des temples que muevent au mengier;	 and remove your hand from the nerves of the temples that move during eating.
et quant li os est descovers, si essue tout le sanc a une esponge, et puis desevre entre les II levres de la fendure et i met coton viel, et tentes de lin;	 and when the bone is exposed, let all blood flow into an absorbent sponge, then place thread between both edges of the incision and apply lint.
puis lie desus drapelz moilliez en vin et en oile, et te garde d’aposteme chaut;	 then cover with cloths soaked in wine and oil, and protect from hot abscesses.
quant il est ostez, si covient que tu frottes l’os tant que chars i comence a naistre, puis le cure de choses exiccatives, que font enjanrer char.	 when it is ossified, one must rub the bone until healing begins, then treat with things that expel pus, encouraging new flesh to form.
En teil maniere:	 In this manner:
pren II parties de flor de froment, et de colofoine IIII parties, et en fai emplaustre;	 Take two parts of wheat flour, and four parts of cinnamon, and make an ointment.
et l’aministre en ces plaies por enjanrer char per tout.	 And apply it to these wounds to heal them completely.
de l’estoupement des oreilles	Of ear blockage
Tout ceu que chiet ens oreilles est une des IIII choses:	 All that which flows from the ears is one of four things:
ou grains, ou beste, ou piere de mine ou semblans chose si com fer;	 either grains, or beasts, or stones like iron, or similar substances.
ou semence, si com jaisses, feves, pois;	 or seeds, such as peas, lentils, and beans.
ou chose defluans si com aigue et aisilz et semblans choses.	 or substances that flow like water and easily pass, similar to other things.
Quant il chiet en l’oreille piere ou autre maniere de chose que ne s’ajoste mie a l’oreille, ne ne croist en l’oreille, si met l’oreille au solel.	 When it falls into the ear as a stone or any other matter that does not reside in the ear, and grows not within the ear, then place the ear against the sun.
Se tu vois la piere, si distille aucun poc d’oile violet ou oile de sisament, puis i amenistre extraction;	 If you see a stone, and if it secretes any purple oil or frankincense oil, then perform an extraction.
et lou fai esternuer de condisi, et li estoupe les narines quant li esternuemens vient, et met entor l’oreille pieces de drapelz ou laine;	 and if it is a condition causing sneezing, then clear the nostrils when sneezing occurs, and place cloth or wool between the ears.
et estent l’oreille au desus.	 And they raise the ear above.
Mout de fois vient fuer par ceste cure;	 Often healing comes from this treatment;
et s’elle ne vient fuer, se li amenistre extraction as pinceures subtilz, de coi ci est li forme:	 and if it does not come about, prepare the delicate extraction of splinters, for there is the procedure:
S’elle saut fuer as pinceures, c’est boin;	 If it comes from the splinters, that is good;
se ceu non, si amenistre extraction a l’oncine subtil de petite doubleure;	 if not, prepare the delicate extraction of small wire-thorns;
et s’elle ne saut par ceu, si fai une caine d’arain et boute lou chief de la cainne ou pertuis de l’oreille fort, et estoupe ceu qui est entor la cainne de cire mole si que li vens n’i puisse entrer avec la cainne;	 and if it does not come out from there, make a grain of tar and pour the head of the gadfly or hole of the ear strongly, then stuff with wool around the grain so that he cannot enter with the gadfly.
puis le trai fuer forment, car mout de fois vient fuer si com nos avons dit;	 then treat it firmly, as often as we have said it comes about.
et s’elle ne vient fuer en teil maniere, si prent glut de coi en prent les oisiaus, et met en som aucun estrument qui soit a point por ceu faire, et met un poc de coton entor;	 And if it does not come in any way, take linseed which is used for the eyes, and place on some instrument sharp enough to do so, and put some cotton around.
puis presse le glut sus la piere ou quel chose que ce soit, et trai fuer.	 Then press the lens onto the stone or any other object, and grind it down further.
Et s’elle ne saut fuer de toutes ces choses que nos avons dit, si te haste de fendre l’oreille ainsois que aposteme chalz i veigne, et spasme;	 And if it does not decrease from all the things we have said, hurry to cut an ear where blood may appear and swelling occurs.
et li maniere de la fendure si est que tu faices premier sainier lou malaide de la cephalique, et estrai dou sanc selonc la mesure de sa vertu, puis fai seoir lou malaide entre tes mains et li torne l’oreille au desus, et fent une petite fendure en la racine de l’oreille a la graisse ou leu dependant;	 and the manner of cutting should be that you first treat the patient's headache, and draw out blood according to its power, then make the patient sit between your hands and turn the ear upwards, making a small cut at the root of the ear near the fat or tissue.
et soit li fendure ausi com une lune, tant que tu viegnes a la piere, puis l’oste selonc ton pooir, et la suce hastanment a ta bouche;	 And it is the cut as like a crescent until you reach the bone, then according to your ability, and quickly suck the shard into your mouth.
et la cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	 And apply the treatment until it heals properly.
Et se c’est grains qui est ens et il enfle, si aministre extraction;	 And if there are stones present and they swell, then arrange for their removal;
et si’il ne puet issir, si amenistre I spatumile tenve subtil selonc ceste forme:	 and if it cannot be removed naturally, make a gentle incision following this method:
et amenistre incision de celui grain.	 and make an incision in that grain of sand.
Mais ne faire mie ceu quant tu penses que li grains est moistes por la moistor de l’oreille, tant que tu en aies fait maintes pieces;	 But do not attempt this when you think the stone is wet due to earwax, until you have made many attempts.
puis l’estrai as pinceures subtilz et au succier, si com nos avons dit, si que li estractions soit aligie.	 then extract carefully with tweezebar and a suction device, as we have said before, to ensure the extraction is successful.
En l’aigue donques que chiet en l’oreille covient que li malaides use d’esternuement de condisi premiers, et ample l’oreille de viel coton.	 In this case then when it comes to the ear, the patient should practice initial sneezing of conditions, and fill the ear with old cotton.
Et soit gisans sus celle oreille meisme ou li aigue est.	 And lie down on the same ear where the water is present.
s’elle saut fuer per ceu, c’est boin.	 If it comes out strongly like this, it's good.
se ceu non, si prent maintes pieres selonc li longesce de ton doit tenves et legieres, et les eschaufe un poc au feu;	 if not, then take many pieces according to the length of your instrument and lightness, and warm them slightly over fire.
et em mette li malaides une ou pertus de son oreille, et saille sus i. de ses piez d’autre part, et fiere d’une autre piere sus la piere qui est en l’oreille;	 And place the patient a poultice from his ear, and it rises up in him. From his feet on the other side, and pierces another stone above the one that is in the ear.
et ne cesse de faire ceu de piere em piere tant que li aigue isse toute fuer, et ensi saut elle toute fuer;	 And it continues to move from stone to stone as long as the water has passed all through, and thus it flows completely.
et se tu vues, si prent I jonc, et boute l’un des chiés en l’oreille, et l’autre chief emprent de feu tant que li plus dou jonc soit ars;	 And if you see this, take a reed, and put one of the heads into the ear, and the other head through fire until the thinner reed has burned.
puis refai autreteil d’autres jons tant que li aigue isse toute, si com nos avons dit en la piere.	 Then make others from different reeds as long as water passes through, just as we have said in the stone.
En l’estraction de la beste, s’elle est de petit cors, si com puce et semblans chose, cure la si com nos avons dit en la division;	 In extracting the beast, if it is of small stature like a flea or similar thing, treat it as we have said in the division.
mais s’elle est de grant cors c’on la puisse sentir, si amenistre extraction de pinceures;	 But if it is of a large body so it can be felt, then arrange for drainage with probes.
et c’est li chose plus legiere a oster qui soit en l’oreille.	 and this is the easier thing to remove which is in the ear.
En l’estraction des vers enjanrez as oreilles, quant tu lou cures si com nos avons dit en la division et ou traitier des distillations, et li cure ne profite mie, si covient que tu regardes l’oreille au soleil:	 In the removal of worms from the ears, as we have instructed in the section on treating distillations, and if the remedy does not work, then you must examine the ear in sunlight.
s’il i apert nulz vers, si les trai as pinceures subtilz, et s’il n’aperent, si prent la cainne de coi ci est li forme:	 if there are no worms, use fine probes, and if they don't appear, take the hornlike material that is present.
Et soit estroite desoz et large desus.	 And it should be narrow at the base and wide above.
Et boute lou plus subtil chief en l’oreille selonc la quantiteit de la soffrance dou malaide, puis succe forment a tot la caine;	 And insert the finer part in the ear according to the amount of suffering the patient has, then proceed similarly with all the material.
fai ceu sovent tant que tuit li ver issent.	 Perform this often until all wounds are healed.
Et s’il n’obeissent a issir, si estoupe entor la cainne de coton si com j’ai dit en la piere;	 And if they do not obey in leaving, then stop around the edge of the cloth as I have instructed with stones.
et s’il ne saillent fuer si com nos avons dit, si aministre distillations que li ancien ont esprovees en l’ocision des vers, et tu les troveras ou traitier des distillations;	 and if they do not exit as we have said, then administer dilutions that the ancients have tried with arrow wounds, and you will find or treat with dilutions.
et si distille tes oiles et tes medicines en l’oreille a tout cest estrument, de coi ci est li forme si com tu vois:	 and if you distill your oils and medicines into this instrument in the ear, thus is its shape as you see it here.
Et soit d’argent ou d’arain estrois desoz a I petis pertuis, et desus overs por distiller;	 And made of silver or brass without small holes and above openings for distillation;
et por presser dedens la distillation a I estrument d’arain bien fait por ceu, et se tu vues pren I raseur et envoloupe entor la pointe avenanment coton;	 And to apply pressure on the distillation with an arsenic instrument well-made for this purpose, and if you see rust and wind around the tip immediately wrap in cloth.
puis i giete ton oile ou ton jus, et ceu que tu vues de tes medicines en la cainne, et li caine soit en l’oreille;	 Then pour on your oil or juice, and what you see of your medicines in the jar, and let it be applied to the ear.
puis boute dedens lou raseur a tout lou coton, et presse ta main tempreement tant que li oile soit distilleit ou chevement de l’oreille;	 Then stuff the syringe with all the cotton, and press your hand firmly until the oil is dripping or seeping from the ear.
et lou sente li malaides dedens, et soit li distillations I poc eschaufee au feu ainsois c’on la distille en l’oreille;	 And let it scent the patient inside, and be the distillation of drops heated in fire just as one would distill it into the ear.
et garde qu’elle ne soit trop froide, car li medicine ne seroit mie si bone.	 And keep that it is not too cold, for the medicines would not be so good otherwise.
de l’estoupement des oreilles	Of ear blockage
Aucun enfant naissent qui n’ont nul pertus ens oreilles;	 No child is born without any hairs on their ears.
et ceste meisme chose avient as homes par estoupement de plaie, ou de char nee dedens l’oreille, et cist estoupemens vient aucune fois em parfont en l’oreille, si c’on ne lou puet veoir;	 And this same thing happens in adults by the outpouring of a wound or moisture inside the ear, and these outpourings come from time to time into the ear if it is not visible.
et aucune fois avient I poc defuer lou pertus, et lou voit om bien.	 At no time does one fail to find relief with poultices, and they see very well improvement.
Celle donques que vient em parfont, si c’on ne la puet veoir, est de grief sanation em plusors dispositions, et en cele c’on voit covient que tu mettes l’oreille dou malaide au soleil;	 Therefore if one comes by it and cannot see, it is of serious healing in various conditions, and where it must be that you place the patient's ear to the sun.
et regarde dedens:	 and look inside:
se tu vois l’opilation apparent, si la oevre a tot cest spatumile de coi ci est li forme:	 if you see apparent swelling, then the work is all in this area of which it has form:
Et soit agus et trenchans devant et derrier tout plain, si qu’il ne blece l’oreille;	 And be sharp and cutting before and behind completely flat, such that it does not bend the ear.
se li opilation est de char nee ou cors de l’oreille, si la tien as pinceures subtilz, et la cope legierement, tant que celle chars soit toute ostee.	 if the swelling is of chancre or body of the ear, take it with subtle pinchers and cut lightly until all bone is removed.
Et se li opilations est em parfont en l’oreille, si pren I raseur subtil legier et l’eschaufe un petit au feu, puis li met ou cors de l’oreille.	 And if distillation is partially in the ear, take a light and subtle razor blade and shave it slightly over fire, then place or adjust the part of the ear.
Se tu sens l’opilation dont li malaides sent grieteit a l’oïr, perce legierement, et garde que tu ne grever les ners de l’oreille;	 If you feel the obstruction of which the patient feels pain in hearing, puncture lightly, and be careful not to damage the nerves of the ear.
puis met en l’oreille une tente selonc la largesce dou pertus, et la moille en l’oignement egyptien.	 Then place a dressing in the ear according to the size of the puncture, and apply ointment with Egyptian balm.
Fai ceu aucun jor tant que li plaie soit soudee, ou tu pren une tente et la moille en aigue rose, et poudre sus vitriole broiet;	 Do not do this for any day until the wound is healed, or you take a dressing and apply ointment with rosewater, and powder it with white lead.
et se tu vois enflee l’oreille, si couvient que tu traies la tente et remue une autre tente moillie en cerote qui soit fait d’oile roset et de cire, tant que li enfleure soit ostee;	 And if the ear starts to protrude, it is necessary that you change the dressing and apply another greasy dressing made of rose oil and wax until the swelling subsides.
puis le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	 Then continue treatment until it becomes healthy again.
Et se decorremens de sanc vient, si plonge une esponge et drapelz en aigue froide, et le met sus l’oreille, et use d’autres cures qui oste lou decorrement de sanc qui sont ou traitier des destillations.	When bleeding persists, immerse a sponge and cloth in cold water, place it on the ear, and apply other remed cuing to stop the blood flow which are used for treating dropsy.
de la char des papieres	From removing parchment layers.
Cist althelul que vienent em papieres des eulz quant ils sont moiste et sont sec, si covient que tu les estendes de tenailles et de pinceures, et le cope d’un spatumile de ses racines;	 This paper linen that comes from hairs when they are wet and dry, it must be stretched with tongs and pincers, and the root of a spatulaceous leaf.
puis met sor le leu vitriole broiet.	 Then place them under the lead acetate solution.
Et se sans en decort, si le cauterize dou cautere lenticulaire subtil, et li cauterizeir aprés l’incision vaut mues;	 And if they do not decay, then you may causticate with the fine lentil-shaped caustic and apply the burn after making an incision;
et maintes fois repairent, cant aucune chose demoure de lor racines;	 and many times heal, for nothing remains attached to their roots.
et quant elles sont cauterizees par feu, si sont arses celles racines et ne revienent mie.	 and when they are causticated by fire, those roots burn and do not return.
de la gresle	Of chalk
Maintes fois vienent em papieres des eulz unes choses que semblent gresle en sa forme et en sa duresce, et por ceu est ceste maladie apelee «grandine», et est une assemblee de moistor grosse en la papiere desus et desoz;	 Often paper linen appears with things that seem icy in form and hardness, and so this disease is called "hailstorm," and it is an accumulation of moisture large above and below the paper.
li ovraiges est telz:	 The work consists of these things:
pren warde se li grandine se muet d’une part et d’autre, et c’est legiere chose a savoir;	 Take care that if hail falls from both sides, and it is an easy thing to know;
fent la donques dou large, puis l’escorche de chescune partie legierement, puis la prent as pinceures, et la cope.	 Then make the slits wide apart, then gently scrap each part, then grasp with tweezers, and bandage it.
se tu ne la pues coper sens percier un poc la papiere, si ne grieve rien au malaide;	 If you cannot cover it without slightly piercing the paper, nothing will harm the patient;
et se li fendure est grans, si l’assemble a une costure, et la cure tant qu’ele soit sanee;	 And if the split is large, then stitch it with a thread, and heal until it is cleaned. ;
et s’elle est petite, si n’i faire point de force, car li oignemens la restoure tantost et enjanre char.	 And if it is small, do not exert any pressure, as the ointments will restore it quickly and cause irritation; ;
Et se li grandine est dessendans au dedens de l’oreille vers la partie desus, si enverse la papiere, et estent la grandine a unes pinceures, et la cope et presse d’une part et d’autre;	 And if the hail is descending into the inner ear toward the upper part, reverse the paper and extend the hailstones with tweezebrushings, then bandage it on both sides firmly. ;
et se li papiere est esloignie par l’incision, ce ne grieve rien;	 If the paper is displaced by incision, it causes no harm.
et quant li grandine est copee, si leive l’oil d’aigue salee, et cure le leu de ceu qui enjanre char tant que li malaides soit sanez.	 And when the large abscess is opened, cleanse with salty water and treat the area until the patient recovers fully.
de la graisse des eulz	From the fat of the eyes
Exinach est une graisse qui est enjanree en toiles des papieres desus, et ce avient plus as enfans c’a nules gens, et grieve mout a lor eulz, et li vienent li catharre as matinees, et ne pueent regardeir la lumiere dou soleil por ceu que les larmes se hastent a lor eulz;	 Epiphora is an oily discharge that occurs under the skin of children and rare adults, causing great eye pain, leading to redness in the mornings, and they cannot look at sunlight because tears rush to their eyes.
et por ceu se couchent il sor lor faices adés, et dorment sus, et sont lor papieres desoz lor sorcilz moistes que li enfleure et li apparance ont covert de l’exinach qui apert en l’oil.	 Therefore, they sleep with their faces downwards, lying on their backs, and the swelling covers their moist eyelids, altering the appearance of the epiphora in the oil.
Et quant tu presses lou leu a tes dois et sent l’exirnach entr’ous.	 And when you press the head with your hands and feel pressure between them.
Et li maniere de l’ovraige si est que li malaides mette son chief en ton sain;	 And the manner of treatment is such that the patient rests their head on a support.
et puis pren I drapeil de lin, et appareille une tente em maniere d’un cercle selonc la quantiteit que conteigne exirnach de chescune partie, puis le met sus li;	 and then take a cloth of flax, and tailor it into a tent shape according to the size needed for each part, then place it over him.
et presse a tes dois d’une part et d’autre, si que li exirnach soit assemblez emmi le cercle;	 and press with your hands on both sides so that the parts come together within the circle.
puis fent em mileu de la moistor au spatumile trenchant une fendure dou large, et ne soit mie plus grans que li plaie c’on fait a la sainie de voinne;	 then make a slit in the membrane with a sharp scalpel, and it should not be wider than the wound made on the vein's sheath.
et fent le cuir em parfont tant que tu veignes a l’exirnach;	 and cut through to reach the dislocated bone as needed.
et em plusors dispositions vient exirnach de la fendure, selonc la forme d’une piece de graisse blainche.	 and in various positions, the dislocation comes from the slit, resembling a white fatty tissue fragment.
Estrai la donques a tout une piece de drap charpit entre tes dois au defuer, et torne ta main a destre et a senestre tant qu’il soit espars;	 Remove it now by grabbing a piece of torn cloth between your thumb and index finger at the dislocation, and turn your hand to the right and left until it is spread.
