li chapistres des apostemes	The surgeons of abscesses
Mout de semblances d’aposteme sont, selonc ceu que li remembrance vient ci aprés d’un et d’autre en cest livre, et sont diver en perforation et en taille;	 There are many types of abscesses, as recounted here from one to another in this book, and they vary between puncture and incision.
et c’est en II manieres dont l’une est en sa semblance meisme, et de ceu qu’il tient moistor.	 And it is in two ways that one is similar to the other because of its moisture content.
Et li seconde maniere si est por les leus ou il sont au cors.	 And the second way is for boils that occur within the body.
car li apostemes dou chief est autres que cil dou fondement, et li apostemes dou leu charnut est autres que cil qui vient en jointures, et chescuns ait son jugement en l’uevre.	 Because abscesses in the head are different from those at the base, and abscesses within muscles differ from those that occur in joints, each has its own judgment in practice.
Et si a apostemes c’on ne doit mie percier, tant que li bowe est meure selonc son acomplissement;	 And if there is an abscess where one must not pierce it until the bowel has completed its process.
et si a de telz qu’il covient percier quant il sont crut, et ne meurent mie selonc lor acomplissement, si com aposteme qui sont delez jointures.	 And if there are such that one must pierce when they have matured and do not die according to their completion, like abscesses near joints.
Car quant apostemes vient delez jointures, et on le laisse tant qu’il est porris entor, par aventure si sont corrumput li liien et li nerf de la jointure, par coi ce est cause de contraction en celui membre.	 When abscesses appear near joints, and they are left to rot there, sometimes the ligament and nerve of the joint become corrupted, causing contraction in that limb.
Ou li aposteme est delez lou membre principel, et se tu tardes la perforation tant qu’il soit meurez, si nuira au membre principeil;	 Or if the abscess is near a limb, and you delay the piercing until it has matured, harm will come to the main limb.
ou il est delez lou fondement, si le perce on ainsois qu’il soit meurs;	 or if it is near the foundation, one should pierce only when it is matured.
et ne covient mie que tu perces aposteme crut sens digestion acomplie, fuers que celui qui est delez lou fondement, qu’il ne porrisse em parfont, et soit alongiez dedens, et i viegne fistule;	 and one must only pierce an abscess when matured with digestion completed, avoiding those near the foundation that may burst openly, elongate internally, and form a fistula.
et ne puisse saner en grant termine.	 And cannot heal completely.
Et covient que tu saiches l’oure de la perforation de l’aposteme qui est meur selonc l’acomplissement, et c’est quant li dolor est apaisie, et li departemens de la fievre, et l’amenuisement de la dolor et de la roujor, et dou debatement et de l’aguisement dou chief de l’aposteme, et les autres signes;	 And it is necessary that you assess the time of abscess perforation when fully formed, and this is when the pain subsides, and the departure of fever, and the diminution of redness and heat, and softening and debilitation at the top of the abscess, and other signs.
et covient que tu faices seoir la perforation ou plus dependant leu de l’aposteme, et la ou il apert mues;	 And it is necessary that you let the perforation sit or be placed further down from the abscess, and wherever it opens.
et soit li perforation dou lonc dou cors, et se li apostemes est as mains ou as piez, ou en jointures et au ners et as arteres, et en toz leus igalz ou il n’a point de ploieure.	 And the perforation should be deep in the body, and if the abscess is on the hands or feet, or at joints and veins, and arteries, and everywhere else similar without a protrusion.
En ces que ploient, par selonc celui membre.	 In those cases where they are dislocated, with the concerned limb.
Et quant apostemes est en leu charnut, si vaut mues que tu laisses la perforation tant qu’il soit confermez en digestion acomplie, si com nos avons dit.	 And when an abscess is in its chronic stage, it should be allowed to drain until complete digestion has occurred, as we have said.
Car se tu lou perces devant ceu, si iert alongiez li cors dou venim de lui, et est plains de mout d’ordure;	 If you pierce it forward near his head, then there is poison spread throughout the body, and it is full of much filth.
et par aventure endurcissent les levres et li parfondetez de lui.	 And sometimes harden the lips and the deepest parts within him.
Et si a aucun aposteme que sont perciet selonc le large dou cors, selonc ceu que li membres en ait mestier.	 And if there are abscesses that can be felt over a wide part of his body, according to what the limbs require.
Et covient que tu amenistres em petis apostemes, petis pertus;	 And it is necessary that you treat small abscesses and small wounds.
et en grans apostemes, grans pertus, et maintes fendures selonc la semblance de la grandor de l’aposteme;	 and in large abscesses, large wounds, and many openings according to the size of the abscess.
et si a de tels apostemes ou il covient chever lou keur, et coper;	 and if such abscesses need covering or sealing, do so.
quant il est jai devenus ausi com I drapelz, et est amortis, si covient faire ausi com on fait as bubes:	 When it becomes just like a cloth, and is numb, then one must treat it as with blisters.
et si a de telz que sont fendut en III angles, et si a de telz dont on cope ausi com la fuelle de mirte, si com apostemes des angres;	 And if there are ones that are split into three corners, and those cut as one would the bellows of a mill, like arrowhead abscesses.
et si a de telz ou on fait une reonde taille, et autres tailles et semblant copeure.	 And if there are ones where a round wound is made, and other shapes and appearances.
Cil qui n’ont point de chief, si com aposteme souef superficial, il covient que tu lou perces plainnement;	 Those who have no head, like a surface abscess, one must simply pierce it directly;
et covient quant li apostemes est gros, et il a coillit grant bowe, et tu lou perces, si ne traire mie toute la bowe en celle houre, mais en trai une partie;	 And when the abscess is large and has collected much pus, and you pierce it, do not draw out all the pus at once but drain part of it.
puis estoupe l’aposteme jusc’a l’autre jor, puis en trai aucune chose derechief;	 Then dress the abscess for another day, then completely empty it.
fai ceu par maintes fois de greit en greit, tant que li bowe isse toute;	 Do this many times gradually, until the bow has fully healed.
meismement se li malaides est de foible vertut, ou femme portans, ou petis enfes, ou viez hons decrepites.	 However, if the patient is weak in virtue, or women carrying, or small children, or old and infirm men.
Car li esperis tressaut aucune fois avec l’issue de la bowe, que par aventure muert li malaides, et tu ne t’en persois.	 For the arrows sometimes leap at the time of pus release; it may happen that it kills the patient, and do not be dismayed by this.
Eschuez donques cest chapistre par grant cautele, et quant tu as perciet ton aposteme, si essue la plaie, et regarde se li plaie de l’aposteme est petite;	 Therefore, avoid this treatment with great caution, and when you perceive the abscess, open the wound, and examine if the wound from the abscess is small.
et se c’est une tailleure plainne, si amenistre tentes de lin ou de viez coton;	 and if it's a simple tear, then prepare threads or old cotton for stitching.
et se c’est uns grans apostemes, et il i a mout de pertus, si covient que tu boutes en chescun une tente si qu’ele viegne l’une contre l’autre;	 And if it is a large abscess with much pus, it must be drained in each one so that they come into contact with one another.
et se tu as copeit en l’aposteme une partie dou cuir, et tu l’as cheveit entor, si covient que tu l’emplisses de viel couton ou de rasure de dras de lin sens moistor, et le lie jusc’au tier jor;	 And if you have cut into the abscess and woven around it with thread, then fill it with fine cotton or flax cloth strips without moisture, and bind until the third day.
puis l’oste, et le cure d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez.	 Then bandage, and apply a healing salve until it is healthy.
Et se decorremens de sanc avient a ton ovraige, si amenistre aigue froide et aisil, et moille I drapeil, et met sor le leu decorrant par maintes fois.	 When bleeding occurs at your wound site, treat with cold and soothing water, and apply a damp cloth, placing it over the area multiple times.
Et se li decorremens de sanc persevere, se i amenistre governement et cure, et les poudres que j’ai dit em mains leus en cest livre, et se c’est ou tens d’iver, et li leus ou li apostemes est est mout nervous, si couvient que tu mettes sus tentes et drapelz moilliez en vin et en oile chaut;	 And if the bleeding persists, manage and treat it well, and apply the powders mentioned in this book, and if it is winter or the wound or abscess is very sore, then place warm cloths and bandages soaked in wine and hot oil on top.
et se c’est en esteit, et li leus est charnus, si covient que tu mes sus drapelz moilliez en aigue et en oile, ou en vin et en oile froit, jusc’au tier jor, si com nos avons dit;	 If it is inflamed, and the flesh is raw, then you must wrap it in clean cloths soaked in water and oil, or wine and cooled oil, until the third day, as we have said.
et puis deslie l’aposteme et l’essue et le cure, si com il covient, tant qu’il soit sanez.	 And then drain any abscesses and exudate and heal it, as necessary, until it is healthy again.
Et ceu covient il conoistre universement en cures des apostemes:	 It is important to know generally how to treat abscesses in wound care:
or vos ai dit coment on doit aler avant as cures des apostemes, et vez ci le chapistre.	 As I have told you before about how one should proceed with the treatment of abscesses, and here is the chapter.
des soros	About pus. (The word "des" in Old French can mean both "of" or "from", so it's often a matter of context)

Et li taille sus l’aposteme pierous et le moiste, si est plus legiere, car il sont de poc de sanc.	 And the cut above a bloody abscess and wet area is more lightweight, for there is little blood involved.

et trovai l’aposteme ausi com une piere xourde, aspre et blainche, et ne pooit brisier;	 and found the abscess as hard as a long stone, rough and scaly, that could not be broken.
et s’on en eust ferut aucun, on li eust ausi bien fait plaie com d’une piere.	 If one had struck it with something, they would have also made a wound like that of a stone.

et les cure si com il covient.	 and treat them as necessary.
des scrophules	the f h. Manze de lapeccest c's.
Maintes fois avienent cist aposteme au col, et desoz les asseles, et ens angres, et aucune fois vienent autre part ou cors, et sont mout, et sont enjanrees l’une avec l’autre.	 Many times these abscesses occur on the neck, and under the shoulders, and in the armpits, never appearing elsewhere or on limbs, and they are very large, and closely related to each other.
Et chescune scrophule est proprement dedens sa cote, si com li nout et li aposteme dou chief, si com nos avons dit;	 And each scrofula properly arises within its location, just like the head and the abscess at the top, as we have said.
et les semblances de ces scrophules sont maintes.	 and there are many similarities to these scrofulas.
Il i a de teles que contienent moistor, et si a de malignes qui ne vuellent obeir a santeit.	 There are some that contain moisture, and others which are of an evil nature and do not wish to obey health.
en celle donques que tu vois de bone disposition au tochier, et est semblans a la color dou cors, et muet de chescune part et n’est mie aerse as ners dou col ne a l’artere ne au conduit, et n’est mie parfonde;	 in that one where you see good condition at touching, and it appears to have the color of the body, and is not swollen on any side nor red over the neck or artery or duct, and it is not deep.
si covient que tu la copes par desus, et l’escorche de chescune partie, et estent les II levres dou keur as oncines, se tu en as mestier, si com nos avons dit en apostemes dou chief;	 If it is necessary to handle from above, and scrape each part, extend the inner lips white as bone, if needed, as we have said in head abscesses.

puis quier a ton doit indice s’il i demoure nules petites scrophules, si les cope et les munde.	 Then apply the correct remedy if there are small warts remaining; cleanse and heal them.
Et s’il a en la racine de la scrophule voinne grant, si ne covient mie que tu copes celle scrophule en sa racine, mais la lie d’un fil double fort, et la laisse cheoir par li, sens nuisement;	 And if the vein in the root of the wart is large, do not scrape out that wart at its base; instead, tie it off with a strong double thread and let it hang without harm.

And if you remove the entire scrofula, it is necessary to join the two edges of the wound and sew them up without leaving excess due to the size of the scrofula.
si covient que tu entendes a coper la racine de li, et traire fuer, et la cout si com nos avons dit.	 If necessary, you must expose and remove the root (of the disease), pull out any pus-filled abscesses, and close up as we have previously described.

et la perce ensi com celle devant dite, en dependant, puis i amenistre tentes avec oignement et semblans choses, si qu’elle corrompe ceu qui est demorez de la corruption;	 and do so as previously mentioned, then dress them with ointment and similar substances if they show signs of deterioration.
et quant li plaie est bien mundee, si la cure d’oignement enjanrant char, tant qu’il soit sanez.	 And when the wound is properly cleaned, then apply an ointment fragrant with herbs, until it heals completely.
de squinance	Of quinsance
Li ancien dirent et parlerent de la tailleure de la gorge;	 The ancient ones spoke of throat surgery;
mais je ne vis onques en nostre terre qui la feist, et c’est li escripture de lor parole.	 However, I have never seen it done in our land, and this is the script of their words.
A ces qui ont squinance, il covient que li fendure de la gorge qui est apelee «epiglote» soit eschuee;	 For those with stridor, it is necessary to excise the "epiglottis" from the throat incision;
et c’on ne faice aide par ceu, por ceu que toutes les voines et li pormon dou malaide sont a ces qui ont aposteme chaut en la bouche, ou en la gorge ou en II amandres.	 And this is not done by it, because all the veins and the painful tumor are found in those with abscesses burning in the mouth, or throat, or two arms.
Quant li maladie est en la chenal dou pormon, il covient coper l’epiglote por fuir la perdition qui vient de l’estranglement.	When the disease is in the channel of the main part, it is necessary to cover the epiglottis to avoid the destruction that comes from strangulation.
Il covient donques, quant nos volons fendre l’epiglote, que nos le fendons desoz III cercles ou IIII une petite fendure dou travers, entre les II cercles ou par la quantiteit de la fendure dou syfac, ne mie en la cartillaige;	 Therefore, when we want to sever the epiglottis, it should be cut below three circles or four through a small incision across the second circle, not in the spine nor by the amount of the incision.
et cil leus si est covenaubles a la section de l’epiglote qu’il n’i a point de char, et li vasseil sont lonc d’enqui.	 And those who are subject to it must undergo the cutting of the epiglottis where there is no humor, and the vessels are long and thin.
Et se li maistres est paourous, si covient qu’il estende le cuir de la gorge a tout l’oncine, puis fende lou keur tant qu’il viegne a la cheneil;	 And if the master is fearful, then it must be stretched with a leather strip around the throat to its full extent, and incise until reaching the windpipe.
et eschue les vasselz de sanc, se tu vois aucune chose, et puis cope lou syfac, si com nos avons dit;	 and drain any vessels of blood, if you see nothing else, then clip off the fats as we have said.
et est demostrez par la section dou fleume de la cheneil ki saut fuer par le leu qui est rompus, et par la defaute de la voix;	 and it is demonstrated by the cutting of the windpipe's lumen which has fallen due to rupture at the location that was cut, and resulting in a loss of voice.
et laisse la plaie overte une piece.	 and leave the open wound uncovered for some time.
Et quant li houre est passee de coi on doute l’estranglement, assemble les II levres de la plaie dou keur, et la cout toute soule sens la cartillaige;	 When the time is past that one doubts the stranglehold, bring together the two lips of the wound with skin, and the stitch feels all through the cartilage;
puis aministre medicines qui font naistre char, tant qu’il soit sanez.	 Then administer medicine to generate heat, until it is healthy again.
Albucasim dist c’on ne faice ce jusc’a tant que li gorge est toute estoupee, et li malaides est jugiez a mort, et li defaut li alaine.	Not until the throat is completely blocked will you do this; and if the patient appears to be dying, and lacks breath.
Adonques cope on l’epiglote por ceu que li malaides ne puet alener, et il respire par la plaie, et ensi est gardez de mort;	 Then you should cut the epiglottis so that the patient cannot breathe through it, and they will breathe from the wound, thus preventing death.
et por ce commanderent li anciain a laissier la plaie overte tant que li malice de la maladie soit passee, et elle est passee en III jors ou en IIII Et adonques il comanderent a coudre la plaie et curer, tant qu’elle fut curee;	 and so they instruct the physician to leave the wound open until the malady of the disease has passed, which takes three or four days, and then command it be stitched up and healed.
et je vos dirai ceu que je vis.	 And I shall tell you what I have seen.
Je vis que une damoisele prist I coutel, et le ficha en sa gorge, et copa partie des chenelz dou pormon;	 I saw a maiden take a knife, and thrust it into her throat, cutting off part of the windpipe.
et je fui apelez por li curer, et la trovai ausi com morte.	 and I hurried to treat her, but found her as if dead.
Je descovris la plaie, et trovai le sanc qui en estoit issus, et soi bien qu’elle n’avoit mie copeit voine ne conduit fuer que la gorge, et li vens issoit fuer par la plaie.	I discovered the wound, and found blood issuing from it, but was well that it had not caused swelling or a tight band to choke the throat; however, there was severe bleeding through the injury.
Je me hastai, et cousi la plaie, et la curai tant qu’elle fut sanee;	 I tended to it urgently, stitched the wound, and treated it until she was healed.
et n’avint a la damoisele fuer qu’elle fut roge de voix, et revint aprés a sa disposition;	 and there occurred to the maiden only that her voice turned red, and she returned afterward to my care.
por ceu di je que en la tailleure de l’epiglote n’ait mie paour.	 for this is why I say in treating the epiglottis there should be no fear.
de la grosse gorge	From a swollen throat
Cist apostemes est apelez «hernie de gorge», et est uns grans apostemes en color d’une jaisse, et est molt en femmes;	 These abscesses are called 'throat hernia,' and consist of large abscesses the color of jet, occurring mostly in women.
et est selonc II manieres:	 and they occur in two ways:
naturez, et accidens;	 By nature, and by accident;
ou natureil n’a point d’engien.	 Or natural causes have no remedy.
Et li accidens est selonc II manieres, de coi l’une est semblans a gras nous, et li autre maniere est semblans a aposteme qui vient de nous d’artere;	 And accidents occur in two ways: one is similar to us being overfed, and the other is like an abscess that arises from our arteries.
et il i ait paour, et ne covient mie ovrer de feir fuers que en celi qui est petite, et le prueve et cerche a tout l’intromissoire:	 and there is fear, and it does not need to work with force in large cases, but rather test and seek all possibilities.
se tu le trueves ausi com I nout gras, et ne pent a nulle voine, si le cope, si com on cope les nous, et le trai a tout sa coife, s’il en i a point;	 if you find it as in being overfed and not caused by any vein, then treat it as we do ourselves, and address the root of the matter, if there is anything.
et encerche bien tot, et le cure si com il covient, tant qu’il soit sanez parfaitement.	 and search thoroughly, and heal as necessary until it is perfectly healthy again.
des nous	From us
Maintes manieres de nous sont, dont je dirai toutes les semblances;	 There are many ways to address this issue, of which I will speak all kinds.
et or covient que je die toute la difference qui est entre nout et issue.	 And it is necessary for me to tell you the entire distinction that lies between cause and effect.
Je dis que issue est chalors et fievre tenans, tant que li ebulicions est passee, et est acomplie li porriture;	 I say that issues are heat and fever-ridden until the boiling over is past, and decay is complete.
adonques repose li fievre et li chalor.	 Then rests the fever and heat.
Avec lou nout n’a ne chalor ne fievre ne dolor, et contient I syfac, qui est ses propres sac et est selonc la color dou cors, et encomence ausi com une jaisse, et devient gros;	 With ours there is neither heat nor fever nor pain, and it contains pus, which is its own sack and according to the color of the body, beginning like a lead weight and growing larger.
et sont selonc II semblances, ou grais, ou moiste, et mout de color sont si com j’ai dit en la division.	 And it follows certain appearances or grievous conditions, or dampness, with many colors as I have described in the classification.
Il covient, quant tu viens a la cure dou nout, que tu esprueves et l’enquier premierement a tout l’estrument qui est apelez «entromissoire», selonc ce que sa forme venra ou chapistre qui est aprés.	When attending to this matter, first examine and inquire about the entire instrument called "entromissor," according to its form or chapter that follows.
Et li maniere de l’inquisicion des apostemes des nous est que tu preignes ou plus moiste leu que tu trueves en l’aposteme, et torne tes dois poc et poc, tant que tu saiches que li estrumens ait perciet le keur, puis que ce soit selonc la grandor de l’aposteme;	 And the method of investigating boils is that you insert or find more moisture than exists in the boil, and turn your two fingers little by little until you know that pressure has been felt by the pus, then according to the size of the boil.
puis estrai l’entromissoire, et pren garde en ceu que saut fuer.	 Then remove the entrapment, and take care to ensure it does not move again.
Se moistor corrans cort, queil color elle ait, si le fent si com j’ai dit des autres apostemes;	 If moisture runs through the vein, observe its color as I have described for other abscesses;
et se aprés l’entromissoire nen vient moistor, saiches qu’il est gras, si le fent donques en croix, et le prent as pinceures, et l’escorche legierement de chescune part et warde la cotte ou il gist que tu la traies saine avec le nout;	 And if no moisture flows through the entrapment, you may know it is fatty, so treat it as I have described for other abscesses, and scrape lightly on each side, ensuring to cleanse with a tool.
et se tu ne la pues traire saine, si la trai par pieces si qu’il n’i demoure rien.	 And if you cannot cure it thoroughly, treat it in sections so that nothing remains.
Car s’il i demoure rien, si revient li nous par maintes fois;	 For if anything remains, it returns to us many times;
et s’il en demore un poc, et li sans te grieve, si emple la plaie d’aucunes poudres corrosives agues, et estraint la plaie, et met sus choses apaisans aposteme chaut, et le cure d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez;	 And if it lingers a bit and causes no grief, apply the wound with corrosive powders from certain herbs, irritate the wound, and apply soothing substances until it is healed by other treatments.
et se li nous est grans, si cout les II levres de la plaie, et le cure de ceu qui enjanre char.	 And if it is large on us, cut along the edges of the wound, and treat what has been caused by a charm.
et se li voine batans t’est contraire ou autre si te haste et emple le leu de vitriole broiet, et lou laisse liiet II jors ou III, tant que li plaie porrisse, et repose li ebulicion dou sanc;	 And if the boil appears contrary or otherwise, hurry and apply a lead poultice of antimony, leaving it for two to three days until the wound heals, allowing the blood flow.
puis revien au coper ceu que i est demoreit dou nout.	 Then return to where you left off previously.
Vez ci les formes des estrumens entromissoires, et sont de III manieres:	 See here the forms of entrapped hemorrhoids, and they are in three ways:
grans et moien et petit;	 large and medium and small.
et s’en i a III quarrez qui sont apelez «albaret», et I qui est apelez «breb», et s’en i a de III manieres:	 And there are three areas which are called "albarets", and one which is called "breb," and they are in three ways.
grant, moien, et petit, por encerchier les apostemes de fistule;	 large, medium, and small, to treat the boils of a fistula.
et sont ausi com les aguilles dont on cout les sorceles, et sont d’arain citrin, ou de fer, ou d’argent, et mues valent cil qui sont jaune, et sont plus esprovez de plonc noir por encerchier les corbeures de fistule;	 Like needles used for witches, they are made of citrine crystal, iron, or silver. Those that are yellow-colored hold value, and those of black color are more effective in searching for the toadstools of a carbuncle.
et sont de III manieres:	 They exist in three ways:
grans, moiens, et petis, selonc la quantiteit de la largesce des pertus.	 Large, medium, and small, according to the quantity of the width of the apertures.
Les formes des oncines sont de mout de semblances, si com tu vois ci:	 The shapes of tumors are mostly similar, as you see here:
grans, moiens, et petis;	 Large, medium, and small;
et si a oncines qui ont II corbeures de III manieres ausi;	 and if there are tumors with three types of protrusions as well;
et si a oncines qui ont III corbeures, et sont ausi de III manieres;	 and if there are tumors that have three protrusions and come in the same three ways;
et si a oncines qui ont II corbeures, et oncines d’une corbeure soulement, et sont de III manieres;	 and if there are tumors with two protrusions, and only one-protruded tumors, and come in the same three ways;
et tuit cist sont necessaire en lor leu.	 and all of these must be present at their respective locations.
Li chief de ces a coi on fent sont trenchant, et de telz i a qui ne taillent mie fuer que d’une part, dont on escorche les nous, por ceu c’on ne cope la voine ne le nerf;	 The head of these that cut is sharp, and some are such that they only pierce in one place, which we scrape off the skin because thus one does not sever the vein nor the nerve;
et de ces intromissoires sont les alemeles reponues en mainches, si que li malaide ne s’en persoivent a l’overture des apostemes;	 And among these inserted ones are reset shoulder blades held in clutches so the patient does not wince at the opening of abscesses.
et sont de III manieres:	 and there are three ways:
grant, petit, et moien, si com tu vois;	 large, small, and medium, as you see;
et n’en use on mie fuer que en leu charnut, si com jambes, et bras, et mameles, et as angres, et en semblans leus;	 and they are only used in a place like the shoulder joints, such as legs, arms, elbows, angles, and similar places.
et aucune fois fait on I autre estrument petit, semblant a escorces de fistices, selonc ceste forme, a coi on estainche sanc:	 and never made is another small instrument like lancets for incision, according to this form which stanch blood.
et le met on aucune fois au leu qui saine a copement des voines, et as arteres, et aucune fois reont selonc ceste grant forme:	And you put it back into place at times with blood flow from veins, and arteries, and sometimes they return according to this major form:
Aucune fois enflent les mameles d’aucuns homes quant cil encomencent estre corrumput, tant qu’eles semblent mameles de feme;	 Never inflame the eyelids of any men when they begin to be corrupted, until they resemble women's eyelids.
et demorent laides et enflees, et qui les vuet curer, si le covient soier selonc ceste forme des ceste ligne .b. jusques a .g.:	 and remain ugly and swoln, and whoever wishes to cleanse them should be according to this form of these lines b.j. until g:
puis escorche la graisse, et emple la plaie de medicine enjanrant char, puis assemble les II levres de la plaie a costure, et la cure tant qu’ele soit sanee;	 Then scrape off the fatty tissue, and dress the wound with medicinal pork grease, then sew together the two edges of the wound, and bandage until it is healed.
et se li mamele cline aval, et est amolie por sa grandor si com il avient as femmes, si la fent en II costelz desus, par II semblans fendures;	 And if the patient becomes dizzy and weakened due to its severity, similar to what happens with women, they may faint into two ribs above, by two like splits.
de coi l’une soit tenans a l’autre a la fin de l’une et de l’autre, si que li plus grans ligne conteigne la menor selonc ceste forme, des ceste ligne .b. jusc’a la ligne .g.;	 For one to be held by the other at the end of both, such that the larger line contains the smaller according to this form, from this line b. up to line g.
puis escorche le cuir qui est entre les II levres, et oste la graisse, et i amenistre ceu que nos avons dit de costure et de poudres, et ceu qui est necessaire en la cure, tant qu’il soit sanez;	 Then scrape the skin between the two edges and remove fat, and apply what we have said about stitches and powders, and all that is necessary for healing, until it is healthy.
et s’il n’est sanez, ou li incision n’est mie toute faite, por ceu que li malaides ne vuet reposer, ou por le decorrement de sanc, si covient que tu emplisses la plaie de coton moilliet en oignement corrosif;	 If it is not clean or the incision is not fully made because the patient does not want to rest or due to blood loss, then you must fill the wound with a pile of cotton soaked in corrosive ointment.
et le laisse tant qu’il menjuce le remenant et la graisse, puis le cure tant qu’il soit saneis.	 And leave it to heal and accumulate fat and grease, then cleanse until it is wholesome.
des apostemes des asselles	Of abscesses and elbows
Cist apostemes que vienent desoz les asseles sont manieres de scrophules dures ou il ait cotes, et s’en i a que contienent moistor.	These abscesses that arise from under the elbows are forms of hard goiters or swellings, and if there is any containing pus.
Cil donques qui contienent moistor covient qu’il soient copez selonc ceste forme, des la ligne .b. jusc’a la ligne .g.:	 Those thus containing moisture must be cut according to this form, from line .b. up to line .g.:
Et quant toute li bowe qui est en l’aposteme est vuidie, si emple la plaie de viel coton, et la laisse jusc’a l’autre jor, puis oste tout le coton, et cure d’oignement avenant a ceu tant qu’il soit sanez.	the bat:
Et se li apostemes est de semblances de scrophules, si le fent si com nos avons dit en fendures des scrophules, et se li plaie rent bowe, si amenistre cautere si com nos avons dit devant.	And if the abscesses are of similar nature to hard swellings, make an incision as we have described in cutting open hard swellings, and if the wound is bowed out, treat with fire cautery as we have said before.
de la routure de l’artere	Of rupturing of the artery
Quant li artere est route, et li cuir est soudez qui est sus, si en vient maintes fois apostemes, et tout aussi avient il a la voine enflee et aposteme;	 When the artery is ruptured, and the skin is hard where it's above, so often abscesses occur, and in the same way blood flow and abscesses happen.
et si le conoist on ensi quant c’est por l’artere, si est li apostemes lons em parfont;	 And if you extract with this when it's for the artery, so are the abscesses full.
et quant tu le sens a tes dois, si sens I estraignement;	 And when you feel it in your elbows, and it feels strained strongly;
et quant c’est por la voine, si est reons defuer aparans;	 And when it is for the vein, then a reasonable absence appears.
et c’est folie de coper cest aposteme, et meismement quant il est desoz les asseles et as angres et ou col et em mout d’autres leus, et est mout grans.	 And it is foolish to attempt this abscess, especially when it is above the joints and bones and various other places, and they are very large.
Il covient donques eschuir la cure de fer, et celui qui est a chief covient eschuir ausi, et en celui qui est d’enfleure d’artere fent par desus le cuir dou lonc;	 Therefore it is necessary to avoid the application of iron, and those in chief should also avoid this, and for those who have arterial swelling above the long skin.
puis oevre la taille as oncines, et depart bellement l’artere des toiles, tant qu’ele soit descoverte;	 then work with the knife against thorns, and gently remove the artery from its sheath until it is uncovered.
puis boute desoz li une aguille, et la fai percier jusc’a l’autre costeit, et estraint l’artere d’un fil double en II leus, selonc ceu que je t’ai ensigniet en l’estraction des II arteres qui sont en temples;	 then insert a needle from one side and cut until the other side is reached, and hold the artery with a double thread in two places, as I have shown you for extracting the two arteries that are on the temples.
puis point le leu qui est entre les II liens d’un intromissoire tant que li sans en isse qui i est, et soit deliiez li aposteme;	 Then do not move it which is between the two bones of an interposed joint until the blood flow ceases, and let the abscess be released.
puis amenistre la cure que enjanre bowe, tant que li liien chient;	 Then treat the resulting swelling as long as the ligament sags.
puis cure ceu d’oignement avenant a ceu, tant qu’il soit sanez;	 Then apply suitable ointment to that area until it is healed.
et se li apostemes est por la taille de la voinne, si covient que tu teignes a ta main ceu que tu pues de l’aposteme a tout le cuir, puis boute l’aguille desoz le leu que tu tiens a ta main, et la fai percier, et i ait I fil double, si que tu le trais de l’autre costeit;	 And if the abscess is too large for the vein, then bandage as much of the wound with gauze as you can cover the abscess, and place the needle from underneath the area held in your hand, pierce it fully, and make a double thread, so that you pull it from the other side.
puis lie l’aposteme, si com je t’ai dit, ou liien de l’une de II pars as II chiés dou fil;	 Then close the abscess as I have instructed, or bind one part of the two threads together.
et se tu doutes que li filz n’isse fuer, si i reboute une autre aguille a tout I fil desoz tout l’aposteme a l’incision de la premiere aguille, et estraint les filz en IIII leus;	 If you doubt whether the son is still alive, then replace with another needle through all of its thread at the incision from the first needle, and pull gently in four places.
puis cope l’aposteme tant que li superfluitez en isse, puis cope la superfluiteit dou keur et laisse ceu qui est liiez;	 Then cut away the abscess as much as possible until there is no excess left, then cut off the remaining tissue and leave what is tied.
puis met sus I drapeil moilliet en vin et en oile, puis li amenistre cures de tentes et d’oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez.	 Then place a cloth soaked in wine and oil on it, then apply bandages and salves until it is healed.
des apostemes des ners	On the cords from abscesses
Ausi com aposteme vienent en l’artere et en la voine, vienent aposteme as ners quant il sont ferut, ou par trop grant travail, et semblans choses.	is so they le grand. Et so that: the ondce; if: 1  J. If you to not; don’t. Tort (30. JA Dex.
Et ceu avient plus sovent as adjutoires et as dois et en toz leus ou il ait jointures, et c’est I grief apostemes, et sa color semble la color dou cors, et est em plusors dispositions sens dolor;	 This occurs more often in shoulders and elbangs where there are joints, and it is severe abscesses, and its color resembles the body's color, and causes pain.
et quant on l’estraint forment, si sent li malaides dolor, et n’est mie em parfont dou cors, mais desoz lou keur;	 When it is strongly held back, the patient feels intense pain, and it's not entirely throughout the body, but mainly in the head.
et muet bien de toutes pars, et ne va ne avant ne arrier, ne desoz ne desus, et celui qui est en jointures ne covient mie coper par fer:	 And becomes immobile from all parts, and neither goes forward nor backward, nor up nor down, and those with joint issues should not be treated with iron.
par aventure i vanroit contraction;	 There may be spasms.
et cil qui est ou chief ou ou front, fent le cuir au spatumile.	 And those who are in the head or forehead area make the skin contract at the sphacelation (spasm).
Se li apostemes est petis, si le tien a unes tenailles, et le cope en sa racine;	 If abscesses are small, use pincers and treat it at its root.
et s’il est grans, si le sospent a l’oncine, et l’escorche, puis l’oste et assemble la plaie a la costure, et lou cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	 And if it is large, tie it with an incision, then strip the skin, and expose the bone, then stitch the wound closed, and treat until healthy again.
des grosses boces pendans	to make: lesse a l.
Aucune fois avient en ventres et ne mie autre part thelul, et est une maladie qui est apelee «funge» par la semblance d’aus, et est li racine subtilz, et li chiez gros;	 At no time does it occur in other bodies or places than the womb, and it is a disease called "fungus" due to its appearance, and has fine roots but large heads.
et en i a de petis et de mout grans;	 and among them there are both small ones and very large ones.
et je vis I home qui en avoit II ou ventre qui estoient plus semblans a funges que ai autre chose, et n’i avoit point de difference, et estoient blanc, et avoient menue racine, et estoient jai fendut, et en corroit adés moistor.	 I saw patients who had wounds in the stomach that appeared more like fungi than any other thing, with no difference, and they were white, with fine roots, split open, and filled with moisture.

The nature of incision is such that you must check if the patient is damp, and the color of the artery is white and moist with subtle roots.
si le cope au spatumile large, et soient en ta presence li cautere au feu.	 If the head is displaced far, let it be brought to your presence, with the fire cautery applied.

quant li boude ist fuer	When there is an acute fistula
Se li apparance de la boude vient par cautere de plaie ou de fendure de syfac, et est sus le ventre et en ist aucuns des bouez, si com il avient en autres routures, ou de sanc qui cort de voines ou d’arteres selonc ceu qui est devant, ou de ventositeit;	 If the appearance of gangrene comes from a wound or incision in an ulcer, and is on the belly and there are some swellings as occurs in other parts, or blood flows from veins or arteries according to what precedes, or inflammation.
et se c’est par la routure dou syfac et par l’issue dou bouel, si est li color de l’aposteme semblans a la color dou cors, et est legiere chose sens dolor, et apert de diverse issue.	 and if it is from the ulcer or discharge of pus, then its appearance resembles the body's natural color, and it feels light without pain, but open to various exits.
Et se c’est por l’issue de l’intestine, adonques est il plus divers, et quant on le presse a ses dois si se repont, et puis revient, et par aventure si est sarrez, et agrandist mout a l’entree dou bain et por fort travail.	And if it is due to the release of the intestine, then there are more diversities, and when one presses on its sides, so it pops back out again, and sometimes it becomes hardened, and greatly expands at the opening of the bath and requires strong work.
Et se c’est por moistor, c’est legiere chose, et apert bien quant tu le presses a ta main, ne ne constraint mie;	 And if it is from moisture, it is a light matter and opens well when pressed with your hand, do not bind it.
et se c’est por sanc, si apert par ces signes li apostemes gros et dur, et est fichiez selonc une quantiteit;	 And if it is for blood, then open by these signs of a large and hard abscess, which is fixed according to an amount;
et se c’est por ventositeit, si est souef au tochier, et li ovraiges si est que tu regarde se li apparance est por le sanc de l’artere, ou de la voine, ou ventositeit.	 And if it is for inflammation, then it is sensitive to touching, and the appearance should be examined to see if it is due to blood from an artery or vein, or inflammebility.
Si covient que tu laisses la cure.	 If it is necessary to allow the healing process.
Car il en a doutance et paor, si com je t’ai dit ou chapistre des apostemes, por l’artere et por la voine.	 For there is doubt and fear, as I have told you in the chapter on abscesses, for arteries and veins.
Et se li apparance est por l’intestine ou lou boueil, si covient que tu comandes au malaide qu’il teigne son alaine, et soit estendus tout drois, puis seigne d’enche tout entor la boude;	 And if the appearance is of the intestines or bowels, then instruct the patient to insert a finger into their anus and stretch it out straight, and tie it all around the buttocks.
puis le comande a gesir sovin entre tes mains, puis va entor le leu que tu as signiet a tout le spatumile, puis estent la moitiet de l’aposteme au desus a tout le grant uncine;	 then command the patient to lie supine between your hands, then go around the leg that you have tied at all of the thighs, and extend half of the abscess above the entire great joint.
puis le lie entor d’un fil fort, ou d’une corde de fort soie fermement, et soit li nous dou liien assolz;	 Then wrap it closely with a strong thread or cord made of sturdy silk, ensuring the knot is securely fastened.
puis oevre la moitiet de l’aposteme estendut sus le liien, et i boute ton doit indice, et quier l’intestine;	 Then work on extending the end of the abscess above the joint and insert your finger, followed by gently probing with an instrument.
se tu le trueves pris dou liien, si le deslie, et boute l’intestine au defuer dou ventre;	 If you find that it is stuck to the joint, if necessary dislocate it, and then insert the instrument into the bowel below the abdomen.
et se tu trueves le boueil, si le prent a l’oncine, et en cope la superfluiteit;	 And if you find pus, extract any excess with forceps.
et se li artere te fait contraire, ou li voine, si vai belement entor, puis revien a ton ovraige et pren II aguilles, et i boute II fors filz, et boute les II aguilles entor ceu que tu as fait en crois que tu feis percier;	 If the artery is opposing, or it bleeds, then swiftly return to your work and take two needles. Insert the hollow ends into the wound made in a cross-shaped incision you previously performed for drainage.
puis estrain l’aposteme en IIII leus sus les aguilles, et se tu vues, oste les aguilles, et laisse lou leu tant qu’il porrisse, et chiece li char morte par soi;	 Then strain the abscess in four places above the needles, and if you see them, remove the needles, and let it be open until it heals, and extract the dead tissue by yourself.
ou tu la cope quant elle iert subtiliie et porrie, puis le cure de ceu qu’il covient, et cheve l’aposteme si com nos avons dit;	 Or you may cut when it is slender and required, then treat as necessary, and close the abscess as we have said.

de la piere	Of the stone

et ai dit la difference entre la piere enjanree as rains, et toz les signes, et en queil piere on doit ovrer de taille;	 And I said about the distinction between stones within rainbows, and all signs, and in what stone we must work with cutting.
et en la vessie, et en la verge;	 And concerning the bladder, and the penis;

et est legiere li sanation des enfans jusqu’il ont IIII ans, et est mout grief en viellars, et est as jones moiene, a ces qui sont entre jonesce et viellece;	 And the healing of children up to 4 years is easy, and it is very severe in old men, and moderate for those who are between youth and age.
et est li cure plus legiere de ces qui ont la piere grans, que de ces qui l’ont petite.	 And the treatment is easier for those who have large stones than for those with small ones.

Car il encombre aucune fois a querir la piere.	 Because it always hinders one's ability to urinate.

puis la quier et la touche dedens;	 Then grasp and touch within.
se tu sens la piere en l’espaice, si te haste maintenant de taillier sus la piere.	 If you feel the stone in place, then quickly cut into it near the stone.

de la piere des femmes	Of women's pierced areas.

de hernie carnouse	line:
Ramice aquouse n’est autre chose que assemblee de moistor ou blanc syfac, qui est desoz lou keur des coions, que contient l’uef;	 Rheum is nothing else than a collection of moisture or leprosy, which emerges from under the skin surface where hair follicles are located, containing pus.

des apostemes de la marris	Abscesses of the anus
Maintes manieres d’aposteme vienent en la marris, si com chancre et aposteme pierous et herpes et estiomenes et fistules et emorroides et aposteme chaut, et plusors autres maladies que j’ai dit en la division. Or vos dirai les II propres manieres de cousture:	 Here are the two proper methods of stitching:
pren l’aguille, et la boute des la partie defuers jusc’a celi dedens;	 Take the needle and push it through to the inner part up to there.
quant elle a perciet le keur de droit en droit, si lai le chief dou siphac ou cousteit ou tu as bouteit l’aguille, et la fai percier d’autre part des la partie dedens jusc’a celi defuer;	 When it has pierced the correct width from right to left, then lift up the sinew or edge where you inserted the needle, and make it pass through on the other side from within to there.
et li entendemens de ceste costure si est que tu cous ausi com li peletier font les pelz, et que tu laisses une fois le syfac d’une part, et le reprent d’autre, tant que li costure soit toute acomplie.	 And the understanding of this stitching is that you sew as a furrier does with furs, leaving one edge once and then picking up the other, until the entire stitching is completed.
Li seconde maniere de costure, que Galiens dist proprement, si est si com aucun font, qui assemblent les II parties ensamble naturelment, et apploient l’un des chief dou syfac a l’autre chief, en teil maniere:	 The second manner of suture, as Galen properly says, is like any other method that joins the two parts together naturally and applies one head of the sac to the other end in such a way.
fiche une aguille ou chief dou mirach prochiene, et fai percier celui leu soulement, et laisse les II chiés dou syfac;	 Pierce with a needle or nearby thorn and make an incision just enough, leaving both ends of the sac.

de fistule ou qu’ele soit	of a fistula, or if she may be
Saiches que toute plaie ou aposteme, quant il enveillist, si est apelee universement «fistule», et meismement quant elle est chevee et rent bowe.	 That any wound or abscess, when it festers, is universally called "fistula," especially if it rises and flows outwardly.

et aucune fois en saut clere bowe, et autre fois espesse;	 and at times clear as bowl glass, and at other times thick;
