et quant on l’a sovineit sus son ventre, si saut egestion sens volonteit.	 And when you have successfully reset it on its belly, there is involuntary defecation.
Et quant il est sovinez sus son dos et il vuet asseller, si ne puet.	 And when it is soothed on its back and it wants to rise up, it cannot.
Saiches qu’il est mortelz:	 Say that it can be deadly:
si ne laboreir mie en sa cure.	 If one does not labor in his care:
Et se cist accident ne li vienent, si est li chose plus legiere.	And if this accident does not occur, then it is a less serious matter.
Et li cure si est que tu rewardes s’il i a aposteme chaut, si met sus l’espinee oile roset ou oile de moieuf d’uef, tant qu’il soit apaisiez;	 And the treatment is that you apply something hot to it if there's an abscess, place oil of rosewood or hen's egg yolk on the spine until it's soothed:
puis met sus un des emplaustres confortans et sechans, et le lie d’un liien, et comande au malaide a reposer;	 Then place one of those comforting and dry emollients on it and bind with a bandage, and instruct the patient to rest:
et ne dorme mie sus celle partie ou il sent la dolor, tant k’il soit sanez.	 And do not sleep on that part where he feels pain, until he is healed.
Et se aucuns os se dessevre, si covient coper sus lou keur;	 And if any bone dislocates, one must cover the head:
et oste l’os, puis assemble les II levres de la plaie, s’elle est grans, a une costure, puis le cure d’oignement enjanrant char, tant qu’il soit sanez;	 And break the bone, then bring together the two edges of the wound, if it is large, with stitches, and treat with anointing oil, until healed.
et se li chiés de l’os est brisiez, ki est apelez li «chiés de la kowe», se i boute ton pouchet de ta main senestre, et le met igal a l’autre main a ton pooir, puis met l’emplaustre et l’estele sus, se tu en a mestier;	 And if the head of the bone is broken, known as "head of the corner," place your poultice with your left hand and make it even with the other hand in your grasp, then position the splint and stake above, if necessary.
puis l’estraint, et s’il i a os desevreit, si fent sus, et l’oste, et cure la plaie tant qu’elle soit sanee.	 Then secure it (the poultice), and if there are broken bones to be set, do so accordingly, treat the wound until healed.
de la brisure de l’os de la hainche	For breaking of the thighbone
Poc avient que li os de la hainche soit brisiez, et s’il avient, si n’avient fuer c’un poc d’amenuisement au chief;	 It sometimes happens that the bone of the hip is broken, and if so, there is not much room for adjustment.
et fent dou lonc, et decline au pardedens, et vient au malaide dolor au leu, et pointure, et enfle ceu que brise.	 And they make a long cut, and descend into the pharynx, and come to cause pain at that spot, and swelling, and break as it grows.
Et li restoration si est que tu estendes ta main sus, tant que tu soies sus la briseure;	 And the repair is such that you stretch your hand over it until you are above the breach.
et saiches quelz est li brisure et li figure de li;	 and identify what the breach is and its shape;
et se li brisure est au chief soulement, si met igal cele brisure, tant qu’ele soit a figure natureil.	 and if the breach is solely on the head, then make it equal to that breach until it's naturally shaped.
Et se li brisure est dou lonc, ou elle decline au dedens, si fai gesir le malaide sus son ventre, tant que li restauration de cele brisure te soit aparillie.	And if the break is long or it descends to the pubic bone, then place the patient on his stomach so that the restoration of this fracture can be properly set.
Et quant tu l’avras mise igal, si met sus l’emplaustre, puis met sus une estele de fust ou de keur, et estraint la briseure, si qu’ele ne se mueve;	 And once you have made it equal, place a splint on it, then put an upright stick or wood over it and secure the breach so that it does not move.
et emple le leu desoz les costes, tant que li lieure soit igalz.	 and apply pressure away from the ribs until they are levelled.
Et comande au malaide k’il dorme sus son costeit sain, ou sus son dos.	And instruct the patient to sleep on their healthy side or back.
Et se apostemes chaus i vient, si n’i tochier, tant que li apostemes chaus soit apaisiez, et met sus ceu que nos avons devant dit;	 And if an abscess comes there, do not touch it, until the abscess is calmed down, and follow what we have previously stated.
et puis revien a la restauration, et l’estraint si com il covient, s’il n’i a nul mavais accident;	 And then proceed to restoration, and apply strapping as needed if there has been no further injury.
et c’est li maniere.	 And that is the way.
de la brisure de l’ajutoire	From the breaking of the shoulder
Li adjutoires est ceu qui est entre lou coute et lou chief de l’espaule, et s’il est brisiez, si le doit on restorer selonc l’une des II manieres:	 The shoulder dislocation is that which is between the collarbone and the head of the shoulder, and if it is broken, it must be restored according to one of two methods:
dont l’une est que tu pren I fust plain de moiene groissor, selonc ceste forme:	 One method is that you take a piece of even medium-sized bone as follows:
Et lie as II chiés II liens, et les pent en haut, et siece li malaide sus I siege;	 And cut it into two pieces, and fix the ligaments at both ends, and place the patient on top of it.
puis li giete som bras brisiet sus le fust, tant qu’il viegne a l’aissele, et ait em mi une corbeure de fust, puis pent sus aucune pesant chose ou li ministres l’estende aval;	 Then pour the poultice of bruised branches on the trunk, until it reaches the chest, and take some splints from wood, then attach under any heavy object or extendable staff.
puis mette li mires la briseure igal a ses mains ensamble, tant que li briseure retorne si com il covient.	 Then apply the bandage to the fracture, equally with his hands together, until the fracture heals as it should.
Et li autre maniere si est que on sovine le malaide sus son hatereil, et li lie la main a son col, puis comande a .ij. ministres que li uns teigne ceu qui est sus la briseure a ses mains, et li autres teigne desoz a tout .i. liien, et estende chescuns a sa partie.	And the other manner is that one suspends the patient on his hatterail, and ties the hand to his neck, then commands two ministers so that one washes the part above the wound with their hands, and the other washes below from top to bottom, stretching each towards its part.
Et se tu vues que li estraction soit plus fors, si estraint I liien desoz la briseure, et sus la briseure, et estende chescuns des ministres a sa part.	 And if you see that the extraction is further, restrain the ligaments from under the fracture, and on both sides of the fracture, and extend each member to its place.
Et se li briseure est prochiene au chief de l’espaule, si covient que tu mettes I liien moien desoz l’assele, et I autre vers lou coute, desoz la briseure;	 And if the fracture is near the shoulder blade, it must be that you place a bandage underne.chestbone and another towards him from the break, below the fracture.
et ausi se li briseure est devers lou coute, si i covient mettre I liien legierement, sens labor, tant que li briseure soit igalz sus lou leu, et sus lou coute;	 and likewise if the fracture is towards him from underne.the clavicle, it must be that you place a light bandage gently, without effort, until the fracture heals equally at the site and above the clavicle;
puis met igal la brisure, si com il covient, et l’estraint, se apostemes chaus n’i vient.	 Then properly align the fracture as it requires, and hold if an abscess does not arise.
Et se apostemes chaus i vient, si ne l’estraindre mie jusc’a VII jors, et met sus lainne moillie en aisil et en oile roset, tant que li apostemes chaus soit apaisiez;	 And if an abscess does arise, do not extract it until VII days have passed, and apply linen soaked in oil rosé (rosemary-scented oil) to the area until the abscess is calmed.
puis l’estraint, et li maniere de l’estraindre si est que tu mettes l’emplaustre sus la briseure, puis assemble le bras sus l’ajutoire, et met ta main sus l’espaule ou sus lou sein;	 Then extract it, and the manner of extraction is to place a heated piece (emolument) on the fracture, then bring the arm up over the shoulder, and place your hand either under the armpit or above the chest.
et met le drapeil, et estraint sus l’ajutoire, et sus lou bras, si que li bras soit en leu d’esteles, s’aucune chose ne le te deffent, ou se li os n’est muez.	 and bind it with a bandage, extracting at the shoulder joint and along the arm until the limb is straight again if nothing prevents it or if there is no movement in the bone.
Et se tu doutes que li os ne se mueve, si use d’esteles, et met sus la brisure une estele plus large et plus fort des autres, et ait entre chescune estele I doi d’espaice, et soit chescune estele si grans qu’elle passe la briseure III dois de chescune part;	 If you doubt whether the bone does not move, use splints, and place on the fracture a wider and stronger splint than the others, with an interval of one inch between each splint, and let each splint be large enough to pass over the fracture by three inches from each side.
puis estrain sus les esteles, ensi com j’ai dit au comencement dou chapistre sus la briseure, plus fort et moins en aloignant.	 Then strain them (the splints) firmly as I said at the beginning of this chapter on fractures, stronger and less loosely aligned.
Et se tu vois l’assise des esteles, et l’estrignement, si com nos avons dit, en l’oure que tu restoures le membre brisiet, et tu doutes l’aposteme chaut, si le laisse a liier jusc’a septime jor, si com nos avons dit;	 And if you see the seat of the splints and the tightening, as we have said, at the time when you restore the broken limb, and doubt if the wound is hot, leave it bound until the seventh day, as we have said.
puis regarde chescuns III jors lou lien, que prurite ne enfleure n’i viegne au leu, ou li norrissemens ne puist venir au membre por ceu k’il est trop estrois.	 Then observe each of the three days that neither itching nor swelling comes to this place, or numbness cannot come to the limb because it is too narrow.
Si l’adrece, si com nos avons dit.	 If done as we have said.
Et se nulz telz accidens n’i vient, si ne lou desliier fuer que aprés III jors ou plus, et dorme li malaides sus son dos, et ait ses mains sus son stomac;	 And if such events do not occur, then the dislocation should not be reset until after three days or more, and have the patient lie on his back with hands placed above his abdomen.
et met desoz l’ajutoire I cussin plain de laine igalment, et regarde chescune houre dou jor ou de la nut, que li figure dou membre brisiet ne se mueve, ou ne soit amollis li liiens;	 and place a linen bandage evenly on the shoulder without stretching it, and watch each hour of the day or night to ensure that the shape of the broken limb does not move or that the ligaments are softened.
si l’adrece par la vertu de medicine, et li done la viande que nos avons devant mis, en teil maniere que li viande soit au premier subtilz;	 if advised by the power of medicine, and give it the flesh that we have previously prescribed, in such a way that the flesh is consumed first.
et quant il comance a reprendre, si soit grosse.	 And when it begins to resume, so let it be firmly fixed.
Et est costume que li ajutoire et li jambe doient estre repris en XL jors dou tout;	 And it is customary for the shoulder and limb to be restored in forty days entirely;
et adonques lou doit on desliier et aministrer bain et medicines d’oignemens por le leu adrecier.	 Then one should detach them and administer baths and oil-based remedies to direct the healing properly.
Et se li estricture est laide et emboee, si demore a desliier L jors ou II mois.	 And if the stricture is unpleasant and embedded, wait to reset it for days or months.
de la brisure du bras	of the broken arm
Li bras est compos de II os, qui sont apelez li dui «foscile», de coi li uns est petis, et est cil qui enseut le pouchet;	 The arm is composed of two bones, called "physis," one small and the other that anchors the muscle.
et li autres est grans, et est cil qui est desoz, devers lou petit doi;	 and the other is large, which extends from below towards the smaller joint.
par aventure brise li grans foscile soulement, ou li petis, et par aventure andui ensamble.	 Either it may break solely the larger bone or only the smaller one, or both together.
Quant li petis fosciles est brisiez, li restaurations est legiere, et li sanations;	 When the smaller physis is broken, the restoration and healing are relatively easy;
et quant li grans est brisiez, si est li sanation male, et plus griés que quant il sont brisiez andui ensamble.	 When the great ones are broken, so is their healing poor, more severe than when they were broken together.
Se c’est li petis foscile qui est brisiez soulement, si le covient poc estendre legierement, et mettre igal.	 If it's only small bruises that occur, then slight extension is appropriate, and keeping them level.
Et se c’est li grans foscile, si le covient estraindre plus fort;	 And if it's a large fissure, then it must be strongly drawn out;
et l’estende sus I cussin, et teigne le pouchet de la main plus haut des autres, et li petis dois plus bas des autres dois, et soit li malaides croisiez sus lui meisme, et I cussin devant lui plus haut, que li malaides ne soffre nule labor;	 and stretch it above the suture, and raise the pocket of the hand higher than others, and the small fingers lower than other fingers, and cross them against each other at once, and the suture to be lifted higher in front of it that the patient suffers no pain.
puis estende li ministres som bras a la partie desoz a sa main, ou a I liien, et uns autres ministres a I autre au desus.	 then stretch the ministers of both arms to the area opposite their hand, or at the elbow, and other ministers above it.
Et puis le mette li mires igal, selonc sa millor forme.	 And then place the mirrors evenly, according to their best form.
Et se en la brisure a pieces, si met chescune en son leu, et s’il en i a nule desevree ke poigne lou keur, et tu ne la pues restorer en son leu, si fent sus et l’oste, si com nos avons dit devant.	And if there is a break into pieces, put each piece back in its place; and if any are displaced that they prick the edge, do not attempt to restore them to their place, but instead make an incision by it as we have said before.
Et se avec la briseure a plaie, je en ai parleit au chapistre singuler;	 And if with the fissure there is also an open wound that I have discussed in particular with the surgeon;
si pren la cure.	 If you take this treatment.
Et se en l’encomencement dou restorement sorvient apostemes chaus, si glue I drapeil de cerote fait d’oile roset et de cire blainche, que ne soit mie ne trop durs ne trop molz;	 And at the beginning of restoration, abscesses arise, if a plaster made of rose oil and white wax is applied, it should not be too hard or too soft.
et lie I drapeil par sus subtilment, tant que li apostemes chaus soit apaisiez.	 And apply the plaster gently over it until the abscesses are soothed.
Et puis oste lou cerote, et i met l’emplaustre de la poudre dou molin avec abun d’uef, pues met les esteles, et soit li estele de la briseure adés plus fors, et un poc plus large que les autres;	 Then remove the plaster and place an empolastrone powder with plenty of egg whites, then put in the splints, ensuring that the broken one is stronger and slightly wider than the others.
et saiches que il doit avoir VI esteles ou bras em plusors dispositions:	 and ensure it has six or more splints arranged differently:
soit que li briseure soit en l’un des os, soit en II;	 whether the fracture is in one of the bones, or two. 
et estraint plus sus la briseure que autre part, et toz jors moins en aloignant, si com j’ai dit au comencement dou chapistre;	 And it is strained more towards the fracture than elsewhere, and every day less in alignment, as I have said at the beginning of this chapter.
et soient li drapelz que sont sus la briseure molz et moistes, et ne soient mie dur ne aspres;	 And be cloths that are on the fractured area soft and moist, and should not be hard or sharp.
et soit li filz, dont il est estrains, de lin, ne trop gros ne trop menus, si com nos avons dit.	 The bandage shall be of flax, which is strained, neither too thick nor too thin, as we have said.
Et rewarde lou membre et lou liien aprés aucuns jors.	 And restore the limb and ligament after certain days.
Et se aucuns mavais accidens vient au membre, si com prurite ki vient au membre, si covient que tu aroses lou membre d’aigue chaude, tant que cil prurites soit apaisiez;	 And if any accident comes to the limb, like itching that comes to the limb, you shall wash the limb with warm water until the itch is eased.
et laisse le membre ne mie estroit reposer.	 and let the limb not rest too tightly.
Et puis rencomence l’estrignement, et se li liiens est amolis et li os desevrez, et semblant chose, si l’adresce.	 And then resume the strapping, and if the ligaments are softened and the bones healed, and similar things, so be it.
Et se pren warde se li norrissemens ne puet venir au membre, por ceu qu’il est trop estrois, si covient que tu l’amollisses .i. poc, et laisse ensi aucuns jors, tant que li norrissemens i corre, et puis l’estraint.	And if the numbness cannot come to the limb because it is too tightened, you must soften it a bit and let it be so for some time until sensation returns, then strain again.
Et se nules de ces choses que nos avons dit ne vient au malaide, si ne lou desliier jusc’a XX jors.	 And if none of these things we have said comes to the patient, then do not reset until XX days.
ou enqui entor, puis li pent les mains a son col, et soit ses cols igalz, et se warde de movement et de degitement, et dorme sus son dos;	 or inquire around it, then pinch the hands to its neck and make their sizes even, and watch for movement and turning, and sleep on his back.
et saiches que ceste briseure est restoree en XXX jors ou en XXXV, et par aventure en XX jors, selonc les compositions et les complexions des vertus.	 And understand that this fracture is restored in 30 or 35 days, or perhaps in 20 days, depending on the constitutions and combinations of virtues.
de la brisure de la main	of a hand fracture
Saiches que au dos de la main et as nous des dois avient poc de briseures, et n’i vient mais que ploieure maintes fois.	That at the back of the hand and on the forearm occur few fractures, and there come only frequent bends many times.
Et quant li plante de la main est brisie ou ploie, si covient que li malaides siece croisiet, et siet droitement devant lui igalement;	 And when the plant of the hand is broken or bent, it is necessary for the patient to lie crosswise with arms extended straight.
puis met sa main sus la toie estendue, et estende li ministres les os brisiez, et les mete igalz li mires, tant qu’il soient bien joint;	 then he places his hand over the outstretched limb and extends the fractured bones equally, until they are well joined.
et met l’emplastre et les estoupes, se apostemes n’i vient, puis i met une estele selonc la quantiteit dou leu;	 and he applies a poultice and splints, if there is an abscess, it does not come forth, then he places a staff according to the amount at hand.
et soit envoloupee en I drapeil de lin.	 and it should be wrapped in one linen cloth.
Et se li briseure est au pardedens entor lou ventre de la plante, si fai une spere de drapelz, et comande au malaide qu’il l’estrigne a sa plante brisie;	 And if the fracture is around the heart near the belly of the hand, make a cone from cloth and instruct the patient to hold it against his broken hand.
et puis l’estrain d’un lonc drapeil, et soit li estele de keur souef ausi grans com li plante de la main, et l’estraint, si com il covient.	 Then use a long strap or leather strip as large as the palm of the hand, and strain it as needed.
Et se li brisure est au defuer, si covient que tu mettes une estele sus, et une autre desoz en la plante, si que li mains soit overte et droite, puis le lie tot entor la main, et estanche lou liien entre les dois.	If the fracture is in the foot, it is necessary to place a splint underneath and another one on top of the sole, so that the hands are kept open and straight; then wrap around entirely with bandages, ensuring the ties secure the joints between them.
Et se li briseure vient a aucun des nous des dois, se c’est li pouchés, si le met igal, si com il covient;	 And if fractures come to any of us in the thighs, when they are hernias, set them straight as needed.
et l’estraint avec la plante, et se tu vues si met une estele droite petite por lever la briseure, et ne se mueve;	 and strain with a flat object, and if you see that placing a small stake helps to lift the fracture, do not move.
et se li brisure est as autres dois, si com en l’indice ou l’un des autres, si le met igal, et lou lie avec lou doi sain qui est aprés;	 and if the fracture is in other thighs like in the index or another, set them straight, and bind with healthy bone that follows.
ou tu les lie toz en I tenant, que mues vaut, ou tu met sus une estele, si com ou pouchet;	 or you tie all together tightly so they can move a little, or place under a stake as needed if there is a hernia.
et pren warde en la restauration et en la disposition d’aposteme chaut, et secor ceu qui i vient, si com j’ai dit.	 And take care in the healing and positioning of abscesses, and seek out those who come with them, as I have said.
de la cuixe brisie	Of a broken thigh bone
Li os de la cuixe est maintes fois brisiez, et bien le voit on quant elle torne devant et derrier;	 The bones of the thigh are often broken, and one can see when they turn forward and backward;
et li restauration si est c’on lie I liien desus la briseure, et I autre desoz.	 And its restoration is by binding it above the fracture, and another below.
Et li malaides gise sus sa faice, puis estende chescuns ministres son lien a sa part igalment;	 The patient lies on their face, then each attendant extends their hands equally to its parts.
et c’est quant li brisure est emmi l’os.	 And this is when the fracture is within the bone.
Et se li brisure est prochiene a la racine de la cuixe, si soit li uns des liiens devers lou poignil, et li autres liiens desoz la briseure.	 And if the fracture is close to the base of the thigh, let one ligament be near the wrist, and the other ligament above the fracture.
Et ausi s’elle est prochiene au genoil, et adonques soit li liens delez lou genoil, et soit li extension aval;	 And similarly if it's near to the knee, and then the ligature should be near the knee, and extend downwards.
puis mette li mires l’os igal a ses II mains, tant qu’il soit selonc sa figure natureil, et puis met l’emplaustre, et lou lie, se apostemes chaz n’i vient.	 Then place the mirror to balance the bone with his two hands, as according to its natural shape, and then place the splint, and tie it securely, ensuring no abscesses come forth.
Et s’il i a aposteme chaut, si le laisse apaisier puis revien a ton ovraige et a ta cure;	 And if there is an abscess present, leave it to heal first then return to your work and treatment.
li lieure est faite en teil maniere.	 The dislocation is performed in a particular manner.
Il covient que tu envoloupes sus la briseure I bendeil dur doublé en II ou III, et en demoure li superfluitez, puis torne la jambe tant que li talons veigne a la racine de la naige, et boute I fil lonc entre la cuixe et la jambe, delez lou genoil desoz, et veignent li chief dou fil au desus;	 It is necessary for you to wrap around the break with a doubled or triple bandage, and secure any excess, then turn the leg so that the ankle approaches the root of the thigh, and tie a long thread between the hip and the leg, below the knee joint, and guide the head of the filament above.
puis torne sus la jambe et sus la cuixe le bendeil, puis met sus la briseure esteles, et met une estele sus l’os de la jambe;	 then turn the leg and hip with the bandage, then place an esse on the break, and put another esse on the bone of the leg.
puis emple le leu vuit entre la jambe et la cuixe de drapelz souef por mettre igal l’estrignement, puis comence a liier forment III tors ou IIII sus la briseure;	 then place the remaining wool between the leg and hip with soft cloth to apply equal pressure, then start binding firmly using three or four twists on the break.
et quant plus vas en sus de la briseure, et moins l’estraint;	 And when more you work on the breakage, and less it is held back.
puis enten as II chiés dou fil que tu as bouteit entre la jambe et la cuixe, et en lie III esteles que sont desus, puis revai au desoz au chief dou fil, tant que tu veignes delez le piet;	 Then go to the head of the suture that you have tied between the leg and the thigh, and there three stitches are above, then return below at the top of the thread until you reach near the heel.
et l’estraint, si qu’il ne se mueve de son leu, puis le laisse ensi, puis k’il n’i vient ne aposteme ne enfleure n’autre semblant.	 Hold it back if it cannot move from its place, then let it be so, and ensure that no abscess or swelling appears.
Et s’il i avient, si le deslie, et adresce ceu que i vient, si com nos avons dit maintes fois;	 And if this occurs, reseat whatever comes out, as we have said many times;
et se il i a pieces de l’os que poigne, si le covient ewer, s’om puet;	 And if there are pieces of bone that protrude, it should be removed, if possible.
et s’on ne puet, si covient fendre le leu, et traire fuer;	 If it cannot be done, then splitting the opening and draining is necessary.
et le cure si com nos avons dit, tant k’il soit sanez.	 And for treatment as we have said, until it is set right.
Et aucune fois est brisie li cuixe ensi c’on i met esteles, si com en l’ajutoire et ou bras;	 And at no time should the thigh be broken so that stakes are inserted therein, as in the shoulder and arm.
toutevoie, en la restauration ensi faite ne cloche mie li malaides.	 Likewise, in restoring it this way does not harm the patient.
Et saiches que li cuixe est restoree en .l. jors, ou poc moins ou poc plus, selonc les diversitez des complexions.	Know that the thigh is restored in one or two days, more or less, depending on the different temperaments of individuals.
de la ruelle dou genoil	Of the groove of the knee joint
Saiches que en la ruelle dou genoil avient poc brisure, mais elle ploie maintes fois.	 It is found that in the groove of the knee joint there are few fractures but many times it bends.
Et s’elle brise, si n’est mais c’une fendure, ou I pertus, et avient a tout plaie, et sens plaie, et ce sent om bien.	 And if it breaks, it is not a crack or puncture, but causes all kinds of wounds and feels like everything is well.
Et li restauration si est c’on mette igal ceu qui est rons a ses dois, tant qu’il soit assemblez mues c’on puet;	 And the restoration is such that one places equal parts as are present at its ends, so that they may be joined and moved.
puis met l’emplaustre, et i met une estele reonde, se tu en as mestier, et l’estraint si com il covient, puis rewarde toutes les dispositions que nos avons dit ens autres briseures, si com aposteme chaut et autre semblant;	 Then place the splint, and if needed, a round stake, and bind it as required, then repair all the arrangements that we have said about other breaks, such as abscesses hot and similar.
si met a chescun accident ceu k’il li covient, tant qu’il soit sanez.	 Then apply to each incident what is needed, until it is set right.
de la brisure de la jambe	s
Saiches que en la jambe ait II os, de coi li uns est apelez par droit non «mustelz», et li autres est apelez «foscile»;	 That there are two bones in the leg, one called 'right' and the other called 'left'.
et avient tout auteil briseure com il vient au bras, et por ceu est li restauracion si com celle dou bras igalment, et li ovraiges est tout i. Et se li dui os sont brisiet ensamble, si torne li jambe de toutes pars.	 And there is a fracture as it occurs in the arm, and thus is the restoration just like that of the arm equally, and the workings are all therein. And if both bones are broken together, turn the leg completely around.
Et se li os subtilz est brisiez, si torne devant.	And if the smaller bone is fractured, it twists forward.
Et se li gros os est brisiez, si sent on grant dolor, et le voit on bien;	 And if the large bone is broken, one feels great pain, and it can be seen clearly.
et torne desoz.	 and straighten out.
Adonques amenistre extension, et le met igal, et lie les esteles igalement;	 Then make an extension, put it evenly, and tie the screws equally.
mais toutevoie, il covient se li brisure est laide, et il i a plusors pieces, que li extension soit menor et plus legiere;	 but nonetheless, if the fracture is ugly, and there are more fragments, that the reduction be minor and lighter.
et l’alige selonc ta vertu.	 And align according to your artistry.
Et quant tu as tout acomplit ton ovraige, si pren II faixes de fust chevees que porpreignent la jambe d’une part et d’autre, et soient dou lonc de la jambe des le genoil jusque desoz;	 And when you have completed your work, take two pieces of hardwood that encompass the leg on one side and the other, and are as long from the knee joint to just below.
puis envoloupe en II leus I bendeil desus et desoz, et le lie em mileu ausi, et a ceste lieure ne pora li jambe decliner a destre ne a senestre, et ensi est bien;	 then wrap them with two layers on both above and below, and tie it securely as well, and to this bandage the leg will not bend to the right or left, thus it is good.
et aucun i aministrent I bers dou lonc de la jambe, et s’est de fust, et i met on la jambe por warder de movement, et proprement fait on ceu en la brisure ou il a plaie;	 and none may administer the two layers along the length of the leg, and it is made of wood, and he puts it onto the leg to prevent movement, and properly done in the fracture where there is a wound.
et remue chescun jor la jambe, por veoir s’il i a aposteme chaut n’autre accident;	 and each day moves the leg, to see if there is any bleeding or other accident.
si le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	 If you treat until it becomes healthy again.
de la brisure des os dou piet	On the fracture of the bone in the foot
A la cheville ne vient point de brisure, mais as os dou piet vient aucune fois brisure et as dois poc, et n’i avient fuer que quassure em plusor dispositions.	To the ankle there comes no breakage, but to the bone of the foot there is never any breakage and to the joints little occurs except strain in various positions.
Et s’il avient as os dou piet brisure, et tu vois ces os sormonter l’un l’autre, si mette si malaides som piet sus la terre, ausi com s’il voloit aler, et puis met maintenant ton piet sus lou sien, lai ou li os sont levez, puis le presse tant k’il reveignent en lor leus;	 And if it occurs as a broken bone fracture, and you see the bones protruding from each other, place such poor limb on the ground as if it would walk, then now put your foot under theirs, where the bones are raised, and press until they return to their places.
puis met l’emplaustre et estoupes sus, et met desoz lou ventre dou piet une petite tauble a II chiés plains, puis l’estraint au piet avenanment, puis que tu as envoloupez drapelz entor, et autres choses dont tu as mestier.	 Then place the plaster and padding on it, and apply a small rolled bandage with two finger breadths under the abdomen of the limb, then strain to align immediately, and once you have wrapped in dressings around, and other things which you need.
Et quant .iij. jors ou .iiij. seront passez, si deslie lou liien, car tu troveras les os igalz, soient brisiez, soient desaluez.	And when three or four days have passed, you shall remove the ligature, for you will find the bones equal, whether they are broken or dislocated.
Et s’il i a aucuns des dois brisiez, si les restoure, si com nos avons dit as dois de la main;	 And if there are any broken bones, restore them, as we have said of the hand's bones;
puis met au doi brisiet une estele selonc la longesce dou doi, et soit un poc plus large, puis met desoz le piet celle tauble que j’ai dit, et l’estrain avenanment;	 Then break the bone with an iron rod according to the length of the arm, and make it slightly wider, then insert below the elbow the table I have mentioned, and secure tightly.
et s’il en i a II ou III, ou plus, brisiez, si met sus chescun doi une estele selonc sa quantiteit, envoloupee en I drapeil de lin, et estraint la tauble desoz lou piet;	 and if there are two or three, or more, break each arm with an iron rod according to its quantity, wrapped in a linen cloth, and secure the table under the elbow.
et soit estans sus lou chief de la tauble defuer lou ventre dou piet, si qu’il le teigne bien.	 and when they are above the head of the table beneath the belly of the arm, that you do well.
Et covient que tu n’oblier mie les autres choses que j’ai dit as autres briseures, des que nos avons dit;	 And it is necessary that you not forget the other things I have said about other fractures, just as we have described;
et secor chescun accident si com il covient.	 and treat each accident as needed.
de la brisure de l’os dou poignil	For the fracture of the bone of the wrist
Quant li os de la nature la femme est brisiez, si la fai seoir enlargie, puis l’encline a la partie dou dos, et soit tenue par derrier;	 When the bone of a woman's nature is broken, if she may sit expanded, then tilt to the part of her back, and be held behind.
puis emplisse li baile la nature de la malaide de couton, et en i mette ausi gros com I sto;	 Then fill the wound with the patient's own hair plucked out, and place it there as large as possible.
puis deboute la femme, et lieve lou dos poc et poc, et adonques saut li coton, tant qu’il vient a l’entree de la nature, et revient li os avec lou sto;	 Then have the woman stand up, and gently lift her back little by little, so that the hair then jumps into the wound until it reaches near its opening, reattaching with the flesh.
et quant elle vuet pissier, si oste lou coton, et quant elle a pissiet, se li remette, et ensi faice VII jors ou entor:	 And when she needs to urinate, remove the hair then, and when she has finished, reset it, doing so for seven days or thereabouts:
si sera restoree li brisure, et se tu vues, pren une vessie de berbis, et lie au pertus une cainne, et boute toute la vessie en la nature;	 If this restores the fracture, and if you see it, take a bag of beaver skin, tie thread to its opening, and pour all the contents into the wound:
puis soffle en la cainne forment, tant que li vessie soit enflee dedens:	 Then blow air through the tube until the contents of the bag are expelled inside:
la nature si revenra li brisure;	 The nature will return to heal the fractures.
puis soit emplie de coton, et le laisse ensi aucuns jors, tant qu’il soit sanez.	 Then be filled with cotton and leave it thus for several days until it is sound.
Et quant li os dou poignil de l’ome est brisiez, ou de la femme, si le restoure ensi com nos avons dit en l’os de la hainche;	 And when the bone of the hand or woman's limb is broken, restore it as we have said with the thigh bone.
et ne sont mie occultees ces briseures prochienes a celui qui i met son estude et son us, et entent mon livre.	 and these fractures are not hidden from those who apply their study and skill, and listen to my book.
Car li brisure li signifie em plusors dispositions la droite voie de la restauration:	 For fractures indicate various ways in the right path of restoration:
enten le donques.	 Thus understand.
En la verge, quant elle est brisie, pren une gorge d’oie et i boute la verge;	 In the penis, when it is broken, take a goose's neck and insert the penis;
puis envoloupe drapelz entor, et le laisse III jors ou enqui entor, et il sera sanez hastanment.	 then wrap with cloth around, and leave for three days or more, and it will be sound soon.
de brisure avec plaie	Of break with wound
Il covient a celui qui a brisure avec plaie, meismement s’elle est grans, si com li os de la cuixe ou de l’ajutoire ou semblant, qu’il soit sainiez maintenant, si que les sainies que nos avons dit le tesmoignent.	It is necessary for those who have a break with a wound, especially if it is large like the bone of the hip or shoulder or similar, to be examined now so that the signs we have mentioned confirm them.
Et se li plaie saine, si la restainche de vitriole, se tu n’as autre chose, puis rencomence a restorer la briseure en cele meisme houre, ou celui jor, se apostemes chaus n’i vient.	And if the wound is healed, if there remains lead poisoning, unless you have something else, then continue to restore the break in that same hour or day if no abscesses come.
Et se apostemes chaus i vient, si laisse la restauration jusc’a nuevime jor, tant que li apostemes soit apaisiez, et n’i touchier ne au tier jor ne au quart, car tu i feroies venir malvais accident.	t he:cordon ; c;t, they can be le se leso's the mele tre la anguille as de ust; please; do not d.
Et se li os brisiez est aparans sus lou keur descovert, si covient que tu lou mettes a point legierement a tes mains, a extension petite.	And if the bone is broken and appears at the edge revealed, it must be placed carefully with your hands in slight extension.
Et se li extensions ne t’est apareillie por mettre igal a tes mains, si le ramoine a cest estrument qui est de fer, qui a VII dois ou VIII de lonc, et li largesce est selonc la quantiteit de la plaie;	 If the extension is not properly adjusted to equalize your hands, if you reset with this instrument made of iron, which has seven or eight long tines, and the width depends on the quantity of the wound.
et por ceu est mestier au mire qu’il empreigne III ou IIII, selonc ceu qu’il en ait mestier en chescune cure de briseure;	 And therefore the healer must grasp three or four [tines], depending on what is needed for each fracture treatment.
et soit rons et un poc gros, k’il ne ploie mie a la compression sus lou membre a ton ovraige, et soit agus devant, et gros des le mileu en avant, ensi:	 And it should be round and slightly larger so that it does not bend during the pressure on the limb in your workshop, and thick in front, with a greater diameter there:
Et est apelez «palainche», por coi il covient que li chiés corbes soit mis sus lou chief de l’os apparent;	 And it is called "clavicle," for which the patient's head must be placed under the visible bone.
et le boute a une fois, tant k’il reviegne, et soit igalz l’un encontre l’autre.	 and the bandage should be wrapped once so that it returns to its starting point, and they are even against each other.
Et se li brisure est subtilz, et li estrumens ne puet bien prendre l’os, si covient que tu copes lou chief de l’os, tant que li estrumens en ait possance.	 And if the fracture is subtle and tendons cannot properly grasp the bone, it must be that you cut off the bone's head until the tendons have access to it.
Et se tu ne pues ramener l’os, si com nos avons dit, si lou cope d’un estrument covenable a ceu, ou incisoire ou soieure, a ton pooir;	 And if you cannot bring the bone back as we have said, with the cup of an appropriate instrument, either cutting or drilling, within your power.
puis reis ceu qui est demorez en l’os d’aspreteit et de menues escorces.	 Then remove that which is lodged in the bone due to splintering and small shards.
Et quant li os est ramenez, et li malaides sent grant dolor aprés, saiches qu’il n’est mie en son leu natureil.	 And when the bone is returned, and the patient feels great pain afterward, believe that it is not in its natural place.
Si fai tant qu’il soit en son leu, puis moille I drapeil en vin stiptique noir, et proprement se c’est en esteit;	 If you have managed to put it back in its place, then make a poultice with wine and black sticking ointment, and properly apply as needed.
et ne mettre mie sus la plaie cerote ne autre chose ou il ait oile, qu’il n’i faice venir porriture et corruption;	 and do not place any other substance or oil on the wound unless it has oil, so as to prevent decay and putrefaction.
puis aministre esteles quant tu as restoreit l’os, et laisse la plaie descoverte, et cope la coverture tout entor, selonc la quantiteit de la plaie, et te done bien en garde que li plaie ne soit estrainte avec la brisure;	 then apply linen dressings when you have restored the bamen, and leave the wound uncovered, applying a covering all around it according to the quantity of the wound, ensuring that the wound is not strained with any break.
et maintes fois ont ce fait li fol mire, et ont fait venir sus le malaide ou mort ou corrodent aucune fois;	 And many times have the wise men done this to the foolish, bringing about pain or death at any given time.
et soit li estrignemens plus molz et plus souef des autres brisures.	 Thus it is the gentle handling that differentiates these fractures from others more severely broken.
Et se li plaie est male ou grans, et tu doutes que mavais accidens n’i veigne, si com nos avons dit, et tu trueves dolor au leu, si n’i covient mie mettre sus esteles;	 And if the wound is bad or large and you suspect it may be contaminated by an accident as we have said, and there is pain at the location, then one should not apply splints.
mais envoloupe entor, en leu d’esteles, drapelz durs, et les lie.	 but wrap around it, in place of splints, with stiff cloths, and bind them.
Et quant tu vois aprés I jor ou II enjanrer bowe a la plaie, si oste ceu que tu as mis sus a tout vin, et i met oignement sanant plaies, si com oignement tetrafarmaçon et semblans.	 And when you see after one or two days that pus appears in the wound, take off what you have applied on it all along, and apply healing balm to the wound, like tetrapharmacist's ointment and similar substances.
Et covient que tu deslies lou membre .ij. fois le jor, lou matin et au vespre, tant qu’il soit soudez et sanez.	It is necessary to loosen the limb twice a day, in the morning and evening, until it is relaxed and healed.
Et covient que li membres soit aparilliez en teil maniere que li bowe corre aval legierement.	And it is proper that the limb be bandaged in such a way that the bow is bent slightly.
Et se maint jor trespassent, et il ne puet souder mais rent adés bowe, saiches k’il i a petites pieces d’os, por coi il covient que tu quieres la plaie avec tente, et oste toutes ces pieces desevrees que font venir celle dolor.	And if more than one day passes, and it cannot heal but remains bent, as there are small fragments of bone, so you must clean the wound with lint, and extract all those unnecessary fragments that cause pain.
Et se fistule vient au leu, ou autre maniere de corruption, si covient que tu le cures, selonc ceu qu’il dist en son chapistre ci devant.	 And if a fistula appears at the site, or another type of decay, you should treat it as described in this chapter before.
Et quant li os est brisiez, et apert sus lou membre, si com li os de la cuixe ou de l’ajutoire, et autres semblans des grans membres, si ne le traire mie, car maintes fois en vient li mors, mais le laisse tant qu’il porrisse;	 And when the bone is broken and exposed on the limb, as with the hip or shoulder bones, and similar large limbs, do not attempt to treat them, for often death ensues, but leave it until it heals.
par aventure cherra par lui aprés XX jors ou XXX, puis cure la plaie, se tu pues;	 Perhaps it will attach itself again after twenty or thirty days, then treat the wound if you know how.
et se tu ne pues, si la laisse.	 And if you don't know, let it be.
des brus qui vienent sor la sodure	From bruises coming over the shoulder blade
Nous vienent maintes fois aprés la santeit de la briseure, meismement quant c’est pres de la jointure, et laide chose est a veoir li figure dou membre;	 We often come after the healing of the fracture, especially when it's near the joint, and an ugly thing is to see in the affected limb.
et par aventure ne puet faire li membres ses ovraiges naturelz.	 and sometimes it cannot perform its natural functions.
Pren warde donques se li nous est fres:	 So be careful, if you are fresh (meaning young or inexperieneb).
si li aministre medicines stiptiques, si com aloes, encens, et mirre, et sarcocolle, acaice, et semblans autres, ensi que tu preignes aucune de ces choses, ou toutes ensamble, et les confit avec vin stiptique ou avec abun d’uef ou avec aisil;	 if you administer styptic medicines such as aloes, incense, myrrh, and tragacanth, then whether you use any of these things individually or all together, mix them with tonic wine or abundant honey or rosewater.
et les met sus le nout en estoupes, et l’estraint bien, et ne la desliier en mains jors;	 And when it is placed on a wooden block, keep it firmly strained so that it does not slip for days.
et puis la desloie, et rencomence une autre, tant que li nodations soit ostee;	 Then dislocate again and repeat with another, until the joints are set straight.
ou tu estrain sus une piece de plonc bien faite;	 or strain it using a well-made splint;
car li proprietez dou plonc si est qu’il oste toutes les enfleures desus les membres;	 for the properties of the splint are such that they remove all swelling from over the limbs.
et se li nodation est ja convertie en durteit ausi com piere, et il est besoing de l’oster, si la cope desus, et fent la superfluiteit apparent;	 and if the dislocation is hardened as a stone, it needs to be removed by making an incision there, and removing the excess tissue.
ou tu la reis a aucun raseur, tant qu’ele soit ostee, et la cure tant qu’ele soit sanee.	 or reset with any razor until it is straightened out, and cleanse as long as it remains healed.
dou membre qui est foibles aprés la garison	A limb which becomes weak after healing
Quant li brisure de l’os est restoree, et demoure aprés li membres foibles et subtilz, si avient por mout de causes:	 When the broken bone has been restored, but the limb becomes weak and delicate for various reasons:
de coi l’une est por ceu qu’il fut liiez trop estroit, et ne fut mie liiez si com il covenoit;	 That is why one was too tightly bound, and it was not loosened as it should have been.
ou por ceu qu’il i ot trop de liiens, et ne pooit venir li norrissemens au membre;	 This is because there were too many bindings, preventing the member from moving freely.
ou por multitude d’arosement;	 This is due to excessive bleeding;
ou por trop grans movements, ne mie en son houre;	 When too great movements are made, they do not occur at their proper time; or if from excessive moisture.
ou por ceu qu’il a poc de sanc en son cors, si est foibles.	 Or because it has little blood in its body, so it is weakened.
Et li cure si est que tu faices mengier le malaide, et faire le cors tendre, tant que li sans soit multipliiez en lui;	 And the treatment should be that you feed the patient well, and make their body supple, until blood is multiplied within them.
et li aministre bain, et li done joie et liesce;	 and administer baths, and give them joy and ease;
puis met poix sus le membre, si que li poix atraie a li grant norrissement, et l’arose sovent d’aigue tede, tant que li norrissement corre au membre;	 then place pitch on the limb, so that it draws much nourishment to itself, and often heals with water poultices, until nutrients reach the member.
et reviegne a sa figure natureil.	 and returns to its natural form.
dou membre tort aprés la santeit	After the healing of an injured limb, a member becomes twisted
Quant li membres est tors aprés la restauration, et li os brisiez apert, et li forme dou membre est laide, toutevoie ne pert mie son ovraige natureil:	 When the limb is twisted after restoration, and bones are broken openly, and the form of the limb is unattractive, nonetheless it does not interfere with its natural function:
si ne croire mie les folz qui dient c’on doit brisier lou membre tout de noveil, et maint fol mire ont ce fait en nostre terre;	 If you do not believe those madmen who say that we must break the limb anew in its entirety, and many a fool has done so on our land.
et cist ovraiges est blamez, et en vient grans malz, et par aventure li mors;	 And this work is to be blamed, leading to great harm, and sometimes death occurs as a result.
toutevoie, se li nodations et li torture sont fres, si covient k’il soient arosez d’aigue chaude, ou herbes mollifians soient cuites, si com foilles de vismalve, et racines, et mellilote, et semblans choses;	 Nevertheless, if the swelling and torture are fresh, it is proper to apply hot water, or cooked soft herbs such as violet leaves, roots, honeycomb, and similar things.
et li fai I emplaustre mollificatif, si com dyaquilon bien fait, et tu pren le muscillaige de vismalve, et la confit avec graisse de geline ou oile de sisament, et fai emplaustre sus;	 and the ointment with mollifying properties like an excellent diaper rash cream is to be taken, as well as musk from violets, mixed with lard or sesame oil, and applied externally.
ou tu pren figues graisses, et les broie avec fien de colon, et semblans medicines que amenuisent le soudement.	 Or take fatty figs, and grind them with fine wheat bran, and similar medicines that reduce swelling.
Et aucune fois est ostee li nodacion por froter continuelment et longement a mains moistes.	 And at no time is there an inflammation of the bone by rubbing continuously and extensively with wet hands.
Et soit amenistrez movement au membre chescune houre.	 And thus provide movement to each limb periodically.
Et se li tortuositez est enveillie et endurcie, ausi com piere, et besoins est de l’oster au fer, si la covient coper jusc’a l’os, a l’incisoire subtil legierement;	 And if the curvature is old and hardened, like stone, and it needs to be cut out with iron, then it should be coped until reaching bone, with a finely sharp incision.
et mettre cusenson et estude en la cure.	 and place splints and carefully study the treatment plan.
Ci encomence li livres des dislocations	This is the book of dislocations.
Dislocations est issue d’aucune jointe de son leu, por coi il ne se puet muevre, et est li membres mal figurez, et sent li malaides grant dolor et grant lesion.	Dislocation occurs when a joint moves out of its place, which prevents it from moving, and the limb is misaligned, causing the patient great pain and injury.
Quant dislocation vient a aucun, si le covient maintenant ramener sens targier.	When dislocation occurs, it must now be gently moved back to its place.
Car s’on tarde, si enfle li leus, et par aventure si le remet on a poines au leu;	 For if delayed, and the joint swells, and perhaps when resetting it causes pain at its original location;
por ceu ne covient mie c’on le mueve a l’oure k’il est enflez:	 for then one should not move it until it has subsided.
maintes fois fait venir spame et autres dolors;	 many times causes swelling and other pains;
toutevoie, quant ce avenra, si fai sainier lou malaide, puis le laisse, tant que li apostemes chas soit apaisiez;	 yet, when this occurs, provide the patient with warmth, then leave them to rest until the inflammation has eased.
puis arose le membre d’aigue chaude et d’oile, puis le ramoinne legierement, et cure chescun membre si com li cure venra en son leu.	 Then apply a hot water and oil mixture, then gently relocate the limb, and treat each member as care is applied to its place.
Et j’ai ordenez les chapistres des dislocations des lou chief jusc’a piez.	f Armf: TI; ça;
des mandibules	Of jawbones
Poc avient que les mandibules soient desaluees andous, et li dislocations d’ambedous est selonc II manieres:	 Sometimes jaws become dislocated between them, and the dislocation of both occurs in two ways:
ou elles sont un poc ostees de lor leus, et mollifies un poc;	 or they are slightly out of their place, and somewhat loose;
ou elles sont desaluees entierement, et pendent vers lou pis, et cort li salive de la bouche qu’il ne la puet tenir, ne ne puet clore sa bouche, et envoloupe sa langue avec la parole.	 or they are entirely dislocated and hang towards the worst part, and spill the saliva from the mouth that it cannot hold, nor can it close its mouth, wrapping its tongue with speech.
Quant li dislocations est petite, si revient par li em plusors disposicions.	When dislocation is small, it may return to various positions.
Et s’elle est entiere et acomplie, si covient que tu la ramoinne hastanment, et ne targier mie;	 And if it is complete and severe, one must reset it promptly without hesitation;
et en tel maniere que li ministres teigne le chief dou malaide, et boute li mires som pochet de l’une de ses mains en la racine de la dislocation de la mandibule dedens la bouche, se li dislocations est de II pars;	 and in such a way that the minister douses the patient's head with a small pot of herbs, and inserts the tip into one of his hands at the root of the jaw joint dislocation within the mouth, as the dislocation is of two parts;
et li autre doi des mains soient defuer, por mettre igal;	 And if the other two hands are also defective, to set them equal.
et comande au malaide qu’il les amollisse, ses mandibules, et les mueve de toutes pars.	 and instructs the patient that he soften his jaws, and move them from all sides.
Et li mires la mete igal, tant qu’elle reveigne en son leu.	And places the mirror evenly, until it returns to its place.
Et se li ramener est griés, meismement se ce sont les II mandibules ensamble, si les arose d’aigue chaude et d’oile, tant que les ramoinnes legierement;	 And if the patient returns with difficulty, especially when both jaws are together, then apply warm water and oil until they can be moved gently.
ne ne targier mie dou ramener, si com nos avons dit.	 Do not attempt to reset it, as we have said.
Et quant elles sont ramenees igalment, et li bouche dou malaide clot bien sens mollifiier, si met sus drapelz moilliez en cerote fait d’oile roset et de cire, puis le lie legierement de molz liiens;	 And when they are returned equally and the patient's mouth feels well softened, then put a padded cloth made of oil-soaked linen in cotton, and loosely bind it with soft threads.
et dorme li malaides sus son dos, et ses chiés soit estans entre II cussins, si qu’il ne lou mueve ne a destre ne a senestre, ne ne s’efforce mie de maixier, mais preigne legiere viande, tant que les dolors soient ostees, et soient noees les mandibules;	 and let the patient sleep on his back with his head between two pillows so that he does not move to either side or strain at all but gently chew tender meat until the pains are gone, and the jaws are well moistened.
et puis menjuce ce qu’il vuet legierement, et ne se travaille mie d’ovrir la bouche au mengier et au boivre, tant que li mandibule soit bien noee et sanee.	 And then gently maneuver what it wishes, and do not strain to open the mouth for eating or drinking, until the mandible is well aligned and healed.
Et se les .ij. mandibules ne pueent estre remises a point a une houre, et ne sont mie converties a lor leus, si en vient fievres et sode acostumees, et par aventure solution de ventre, et par aventure vomist cole pure.	When the two jaws cannot be reset to their proper position within an hour and are not returned to their places, fever and usual sweats may occur, and possibly intestinal perforation, and sometimes they may expel their contents entirely.
Et quant tu verras ceu, adonc saiches que c’est perdicions;	 And when you see this, then say that it is a perforation;
et maintes fois muert cil cui il avient, en VIIII jors.	 and many times death befalls those who have it, within nine days.
de la forcelle	Of the forehead or frontal bone.
Li forcele ne puet desaluer dou costeit dedens la continuation de li et dou pis, et est desaluee aucune fois au defuer, et bien le sent on.	The powerful ones cannot dislocate within the ribcage from its continuity to the pelvis, and it is never dislocated once properly aligned; indeed this is felt by him.
Et li restauration si est que li malaides gise sovin sor son dos, et estende ses bras;	 And the restoration is such that the patient lies on their back, and extends their arms.
et puis presse le leu forment a ta palme, et elle revenra;	 and then press firmly with your whole palm, and it will return.
puis met sus l’emplaustre et lou bendeil, et l’estraint;	 then place the splint and bindings on, and secure them.
et li chiez qui est devers lou coute ne puet desaluer;	 and the joint that is towards the knuckle cannot dislocate.
se poc non, et se il desalue aucune fois, si le ramoinne a son leu, si com nos avons dit;	 if not, and if it ever does dislocate once, you must reset it to its place, as we have said.
puis met sus l’emplaustre et le bendeil, et l’estraint, et coumande au malaide qu’il se repose tant qu’il soit sanez;	 Then place upon the plaster and bandage it, and secure it, and command the patient to rest until they are well again.
et ensi meisme est ramenez li chiés de l’espale, quant il est desevrez de son leu.	 And similarly, bring back the head of the shoulder when it is dislocated from its place.
de la dislocation de l’espaule	Li membieres et les os est desavisez par le movement qui avient quoi puisse ains que il ne teste puisque demorer; mais si li est grandement malsain, se doit cauteriser avec saindsont li est ; mais s’est :
Saiches que li espaule n’est desaluee fuer que selonc III manieres:	 Know that the shoulder is dislocated in three ways:
de coi l’une est qu’ele desalue a la partie de l’assele au desoz;	 because one way is when it dislocates from under the acromion;
et li seconde est a la partie dou pis;	 and another is to the part below the greater tubercle;
et par aventure desalue a la partie desus, et ceu avient poc;	 and sometimes it dislocates above, but this happens rarely.
et ne desalue mie derrier por l’espaule, et ne desalue mie dedens por les ners;	 and it does not dislocate behind the shoulder, nor inside for the nerves.
et plusors fois desalue desoz vers l’assele, meismement a ces qui ont poc de char, car a ces saut ele fuer hastanment;	 and often dislocates from under to the scapula, especially in those with little strength, because for these it happens quickly.
a ces qui ont assez char, saut ele a poines, et rentre a poines.	 Those with enough hair fall easily at times and return to their place just as easily.
Et par aventure avient a aucuns homes percussion ou casseure, et enfle li espaule d’un aposteme chaut, et cuide qu’elle est desaluee par ceu.	And sometimes there are individuals who experience a blow or fracture, and the shoulder swells with a hot abscess, thinking it is dislocated because of this.
Il covient donques que tu l’esprueves, tant que tu en soies certains;	 It is therefore necessary that you test it, until you are certain.
et adonques encomence la cure.	 And then begin the treatment.
Et est conue li dislocations quant il est aval vers l’assele, et met difference entre l’espaule malade et la saine, et tu troveras entre lor diversiteit manifeste;	 And it is known when the dislocation slides towards the socket, and there is a noticeable difference between the affected shoulder and the healthy one, and you will find their variety evident.
et troveras au chief de l’espaule une fosse, et desoz l’assele au tochier le chief de l’espaule, ausi com se ce soit uns oes;	 And at the top of the shoulder blade, you will find a hollow, and from the socket to where the head of the shoulder meets the collarbone, as if it were some ears.
et ne puet li malaides ramener sa main a son neis, ne movoir de nulz movemens;	 And the patient cannot return their hand to its rightful place nor make any movements at all.
et ausi, s’elle est desaluee en haut, si n’est mie occultee, car tu le trueves manifestement au tochier;	 And similarly, if it is dislocated upwards, it is not hidden because you can clearly see it at the collarbone.
et ceste maniere de dislocation n’est mie fors a ramener, quant elle est novele, ou se li enfes est malaides.	 And this method of dislocation is not to return it when new, or if the child is ill.
Et li maniere est que li ministres lieve la main dou malaide en haut, puis met tes peuchas desoz l’assele, et lieve la jointure a force en haut au leu;	 And the method is for the minister to lift the sick person's hand upward, then remove splints under the saddle, and gently raise the dislocation back into place.
et li ministres lieve la main, et l’estende en haut, pues le mette desoz;	 And the minister lifts the hand, extends it upwards, then places a support underneath.
si venra hastanment.	 if done quickly.
Et s’elle ne vient si com nos avons dit em mains jors aprés, si covient ke li malaides soit baigniez en aigue chaude;	 And if it does not come as we have said within days afterward, it is necessary for the sick person to be bathed in warm water.
et li amenistre arosement mollifiant et assouajant, si com decoction de altee et de fenugrec et de mellilote en aigue, et soit amenistree;	 and let them soak with something softening and soothing like an infusion of elderberry and fenugreek and honey in water, and be treated.
puis soit sovinez li malaides sus son dos, et mette on desoz l’assele un sto de lainne igal, ne trop mol ne trop dur, puis mette li mires son talon sus le sto, et lieve le chief de l’espaule vertuousement, et traie la main dou malaide;	 Then instruct the patient to lie on their back, and place a band of linen equal in thickness neither too soft nor too hard, then put the footstool under the calf, lift the head from the shoulder gently, and guide the hand away from the injured side.
et uns autres ministres teigne lou chief dou malaide, si qu’il ne se mueve aval;	 And apply other remedies to the top of the affected arm so that it does not move downward;
celle espaule revient tout maintenant, et se tu vues si le ramoinne selonc ceste maniere:	 That shoulder returns now completely, and if you see the joint according to this method:
et est que tu faices estre present I home qui soit plus grans que li malaides;	 And that you bring a person who is taller than the patient.
et soit drois devers lou costeit, et boute s’espaule desoz l’assele dou malaide, et lieve l’assele en haut, si que li malaides pende en l’ar;	 And they should be right-side up facing the patient's feet, and lift the affected shoulder from under the footstool, and raise the stool so that the injured arm hangs freely in the air.
et uns autres ministres traie la main dou malaide aval devers lou ventre.	 And other ministers support the patient with their hand under his belly.
Et se li malaides est trop legiers, si pent avec lui aucune chose pesant, et li dislocation revient maintenant.	 And if the patient is too lightweight, do not burden them with anything heavy; then the dislocation returns now.
Et le ramoinne on ausi en autre maniere:	 And the dislocation is also approached in another manner:
et est c’on fiche I lonc tison en terre, dont li chiés soit ausi reons com I pistal, et ne soit ne trop gros ne trop graile;	 and it is that a long stick is inserted into the ground so that the shoulder can align like on the spit, neither too large nor too small.
puis soit mis desoz lou malaide, mais k’il ait drapelz souef sus, et li malaides soit estans dou lonc dou fust;	 then it is lifted from under the patient, but with cloths placed beneath for support, and the patient should be lying on their long back.
puis soit estendue sa main aval d’autre part forment, et li jointure revenra en son leu hastanment;	 then his hand is extended away to the other side farthest, and the joint will return to its place swiftly.
et s’elle ne vuet revenir por toutes ces choses que nos avons dit, si fai ceste cure:	 If it does not wish to return due to all these things we have said, then perform this treatment:
pren I tison de II bras de grant et IIII dois de large, qui ait le chief reont por mues entrer em parfont desoz l’assele, selonc ceste forme:	 Take a stick of six fingers in width and two hands in length, with the head bent to enter into the joint from the side as follows:
puis lie sus le chief dou fust drapelz souez, que li fust ne blece lou malaide, puis le met desoz l’assele dou malaide;	 Then wrap it around with a soft cloth so that the stick does not prick the patient, then place it under the joint of the afflicted.
et estende som bras sus le fust dou lonc, et lie l’ajutoire sus le fust, et lou bras au chief de la main, puis met le bras sus I eschillon d’une eschiele dou large, et soit estendue li mains aval, et soit laissiez li cors pendans d’autre part:	 And extend the arm over the length of stick, and attach the shoulder to the stick, with the hand at the top of the stick; then place the arm on the edge of an egg-slot wide enough, and let the hands hang downwards, leaving the body hanging on the other side:
li jointure reva ens maintenant.	 The dislocation has been occurring for some time now.
Et quant elle est ens, en quel maniere que ce soit, si covient que tu mettes desoz l’assele une spere de laine igal, puis met l’emplaustre aparilliet de poudre dou molin, avec encens et aubun d’uef, sus toute l’espaule et entor, puis l’estrain desoz l’assele avenanment, et torne le liien sus l’emplaustre, et embraice la main a son col, et soit li mains demorans ensi.	Et quand elle est ainsi, quelle qu'en soit la manière, si il convient de placer sous l’épaule une spere (tison) d'uneine égale ; puis appliquez la plâtrer à poudre fine sur toute l’épaule et autour, avec encens et aubun d'uef; rétablissez immédiatamenr le lien au-dessus de la plâtré et embrassez la main à son cou, les mains reposant ainsi.
Et covient qu’il menjuce poc, tant que li membres soit confortez, car il sanera plus tost;	 And it is necessary that he rests a little while, until the limb is comforted, because then it will recover sooner.
et puis menjuce plus aprés V jors ou VII, et le mueve;	 and then rest more after 5 or 7 days, and move [it].
et s’il est fermeis et il n’est mollifiez, si est sanez.	 and if it is firmly set and not weakened, it will be healed.
Et se li jointure est fuer de leu por moistor que i est venue, ou por autre cause, si covient que tu i aministres cauteres a III pertus, si com il est mis devant ou chapistre des cauteres.	 If the joint is strongly out of place due to moisture or another cause, it must be addressed with three small fire cauldrons as described in the chapter on cauldrons.
Et se tu fais tout ceu, et il deslie aprés VII jors, et li jointure ne se tient, et ne puet lever som bras amont, adonc saiches que li nerf au chief de l’espaule sont copeit ou estendut ou amollis;	 And if you do all this, and it dislocates again after 지7일, and the joint does not stay put, nor can lift either arm upward, then say that the nerves at the top of the shoulder are compressed or stretched or weakened.
et saiches que li jointure n’iert jamais fichie en son leu.	 and state that the dislocation will never be placed back in its original position.
Li dislocation qui est devers lou pis, et les mameles, ou derrier, si est faite par impulsion, et estendement de mains, et i aministre on autre lieure;	 The dislocation that is towards the worse side, and the muscles or back, it is made by impact, lengthening of hands, and administering another remedy.
et cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	 And treat until it is healthy again.
Et se aprés la sanation vient grietez au membre, et tardemens em movement, si use li malaides bain maintes fois, tant que celle grietez soit alegie, et reviegne a sa premiere nature.	And if after healing comes stiffness to the limb and later weakness in movement, many times the patient must use it until the stiffness is relieved, and it returns to its original state.
de la dislocation dou coute	In cases of double dislocation
Saiches que li jointure dou coute est desaluee a poinnes, et a poinnes revient;	 He says that the joint of the elbow has been dislocated by pulling and returns to being pulled out.
et s’est desaluee de toutes pars, et meismement devant et derrier, et li dislocations n’est mie reponue, car on la voit bien et sent bien;	 and it is dislocated from all sides, especially in front and back, and the dislocation is not properly reduced because you can see it clearly and feel it.
et desalue selonc chescune figure.	 and it dislocates according to each position.
Et quant tu joins le coute malaide avec lou sain, si le pues veoir apertement.	 And when you join the sickly limb to its sound counterpart, if it appears clearly deformed.
Car li jointure est chevee, et ne puet ploier lou bras, ne touchier son espaule a tout.	 For the joint is raised, and cannot bend the arm, nor reach its shoulder at all.
Et covient que tu le ramoinnes ainsois que apostemes chaus i viegne, car se apostemes chaus i venoit, si seroit grief li ramener;	 And you must reset it as soon as the swelling appears because if the swelling appears, then repositioning would be difficult.
et par aventure ne puet estre ramenez dou tout en tout, meismement quant ele est au derrier;	 and sometimes it cannot be reset at all, especially when it is behind;
si vaut pis que les autres dislocations, et est de plus grant dolor, et par aventure i vient li mors.	 for it is worse than other dislocations, causes more pain, and possibly leads to death.
Et li restauration si est, quant elle est telz c’on la puet ramener, que tu li estendes sa main a tes II mains;	 And restoration is such, when it can be brought back, that you extend its hand with your two hands.
et ses bras soit espandus, et les mains dou mire selonc le coute entor, desor et desoz, et boute la jointure a ses peuchas ensamble, ou a la racine de sa palme, tant qu’ele reviegne a son leu.	 and its arms are spread out, and the hands in such manner as is taught here, above and below, and place the joint with its pieces together or at the root of its palm until it returns to its place.
Et se li dislocations est au devant, si revient quant il double sa main a sa main, et fier de la racine de la palme lou coute qui est desaluez.	And if the dislocation is in front, when it comes back as he doubles his hand with his hand, and bends at the root of the palm cord that is dislocated.
Et s’il ne vuet revenir au leu, si aministre fort extension;	 And if it does not return to its place, provide strong extension;
et est que dui ministre estendent le bras, et le teignent dui ministre, si qu’il ne se mueve a l’estension;	 and it is that two ministers extend the arm, and you bind with their ropes, so that it does not move during extension;
puis torne le bras de chescune part, puis que tu as envoloupeit un drapeil double lonc et large;	 then turn the arm from each side, then wrap a wide and long cloth around it.
et quant li mires a jointe la jointure a sa main, si l’oigne d’aucun oile por amolir la jointure, puis boute la jointure forment, tant qu’ele reviegne;	 and when the pieces are at the joint with its hand, anoint it with any oil to soften the joint, then set the joint correctly until it returns.
et quant elle est au leu, si met sus emplaustre sec avec aubun d’uef, et l’estrain forment, et pent le bras au col dou malaide, et le laisse aucuns jors, puis le deslie.	 When it is in place, then apply a dry emollient with egg yolk, firmly strain, bend the arm at the patient's elbow, leave for some days, then release.
Et se li jointure est ferme en son leu, si deslie lou liien, et le laisse;	 And if the joint is secure in its place, gently release it and let go.
et se tu vois que li jointure n’estrigne bien, si rencomence l’emplaustre et lou lien, et le laisse ensi aucuns jors, tant qu’il soit fermement mis;	 And if you see that the joint is not tightly secured, repeat the emollient and binding, leaving it for several days until firmly set.
puis le deslie.	 Then release it.
Et se il sent grieteit aprés le ramenement de la jointe, et elle se muet, si le baigne et frote bellement, et presse tant qu’il soit assouagiez;	 And if after resetting the joint, it feels unstable and moves, then bathe it thoroughly and rub well, applying pressure until relieved.
ou tu met sus la jointure une naige de mouton grasse, puis la laisse I jor et une nuit, puis l’oste, et lou fai entrer ou bain;	 or you place a fat sheep wool on the joint, leave it for a day and night, then move it, and let the patient take another bath.
et quant il sue, se li frote la jointure tempreement, puis remet la naige sus, et puis entre ou bain;	 And when it is ready, if you friction the joint timely, then reset it immediately, and then apply a cold bath.
et ensi fai II fois ou III, tant qu’il soit sanez;	 And do this twice or thrice until it heals.
et se tu vues, si met sus fien de vaiche moiste chaufeit avec burre, et l’estrain sus;	 And if you see, place warm wheat flour mixed with butter on it and strain it.
si revenra a sa disposition.	 If it returns to its normal position.
li dislocation de la main	The displacement of the hand
Li jointure de la main desalue, et li revenue est legiere, plus que les autres jointures.	 The joint of the hand dislocates easily, and its return is lighter than other joints.
Toutevoie, il la covient ramener au leu hastanment, en l’oure meisme qu’ele est desaluee, ainsois que li leus soit enflez, ou qu’il i viegne aposteme chaut.	 Nevertheless, it must be returned to its place quickly at the same time as it dislocates, so that the limb is inflated or an abscess forms warmly.
Et li ramenemens si est que tu mettes la main malaide sus une tauble, et estende li ministres la main, et li mires la mette igal, ensi que il mette sa paume sus l’aparance de la jointure, et la boute tant qu’elle reviegne.	 And the realignments are that you place the afflicted hand on a table, spread out the fingers, and align them equally, so that it places its palm over the joint's appearance and hold it until it returns.
Toutevoie, il covient que vos regardez s’il est bien a leu;	 Nevertheless, you must ensure it is properly positioned.
adonc mette li malaides lou dos de sa main sus une tauble a l’estension et au ramenement.	 Then place the patient's hand under a table with extension and flexion exercises.
Et se li dislocations est au dos de la main, si mette li malaides son dos de sa main sus la tauble, et li mires mette sa main sus cele apparance de la jointure.	 And if dislocation is in the back of the hand, put the patient's hand on a table, and let the master place his hand under that appearance of the joint.
S’elle revient maintenant, c’est bien.	 If it returns now, that is well.
Se ce non, si l’estrain d’emplaustres apaisans apostemes chaus, et lou laisse ensi sens rencomencier.	 If not, the strain of soothing balms and herbs may help; he allows it to rest again after a while.
Et s’il ne le puet soffrir, et tu ne la pues mettre au leu aprés aucuns jors, si demore li jointure torte;	 And if he cannot bear it, and you are unable to place it back in position for several days, the dislocated joint may worsen.
et ne nuist niant au malaide fuer que tant que li mains est amoillie, et ne puet estraindre aucune chose a tout:	 then do not let anyone but the patient touch it until his hand is no longer weak and cannot grip anything at all.
adonc saiches que li nerf sont copez, ou li artere;	 thus say that the nerves or vessels are cut.
si n’i a autre engien fuer que d’estraindre par cautere delez le cas, et par aventure n’i vaut autre chose.	 If there is no other means but to restrain by fire near the wound, and sometimes it proves of no further use.
Et quant li mains est au leu, si met sus l’emplaustre que nos avons dit, puis l’estrain et le laisse .v. jors, puis le deslie et laisse ensi.	And when the hands are at rest, place it on the plaster we have mentioned, then stretch and leave for 5 days, then release and let be like this.
Et s’il ne la puet bien movoir, et il i a aucune grieteit, si la moille d’aigue chaude, et le frote tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if it cannot move well, and there is no weakness, then apply hot water poultice, and rub until clean.
de la dislocation des dois de la main	Of the dislocation of the hands' joints
Aucune fois sont desaluez li doi de la main a chescune part, aucune fois au dos de la palme ou au ventre;	 They are never dislocated either side of the hand, neither to the back of the palm nor the belly.
adonques estent le doi, et boute la dislocation a tes pouchés tant qu’il reviegne, puis sostien lou chief dou doi, et le pent vers la partie ou il est desjoins;	 Then they are bent, and the dislocation is pushed back into place until it returns, then support the head of the hand, and bend towards the part where it was dislocated.
et le laisse II jors, et puis le met igal celui jor;	 And leave it for two days, then set it level on the third day.
et de nut le lie, si com nos avons dit, et lou deslie de jor, et lou fai movoir, et le relie la nut;	 And from that time bind it as we have said, leave it unbound for a day, then make it move, and re-bind the nuts.
et fai ce sovent, tant qu’il soit estroit, et tout ausi fai, se il est desaluez au ventre de la main, et fai si com tu as fait ci devant, tant qu’il soit sanez;	 And do this often until it is tightened, and do the same if dislocated in the belly of the hand, and do as you did before, until it becomes healthy.
et tout ausi fai, quant il est desaluez d’autre part.	 And do the same when it is dislocated from another part as well.
dou desaluement de l’eschinee dou dos	Pain relief of the lumbar region of the back.
Quant l’eschinee dou dos ou dou col est desaluee, ou il en i a plusors desaluees, si n’i a point de cure, car li mors haste le malaide.	When the spine of the back or neck is dislocated, if there are many dislocations, there is no remedy, as it hastens death for the patient.
Et li signes si est que li egestions saut fuer sens volunteit, ne ne la puet tenir, et maintes fois sont mollifiez aucun membre, ou les II cuixes ou li dui bras ou I.	 And the signs are that the discharges jump out involuntarily, cannot be contained, and many times a limb is softened or either both thighs or one arm or one leg.
Et maintes fois se muet li eschinee a IIII pars;	 And often the spine moves in four parts;
celle qui se muet au derrier si est apelee «gilbositez»:	 That which moves at the rear is called "gilbosis":
li cure si est que tu rewarde se li gilbositez est venue d’enfance:	 The treatment is that you should check if the 'gilbosis' came from childhood:
si n’i ait point de cure ne de sanation dou tot.	 If there is no cure or healing at all.
Et celle que vient de cheoir ou de percussions ou de semblans choses, dirent li ancien manieres de cures par grans paroles, ou il n’a mie en toutes grant profit;	 And that which comes from falling or blows or similar things, say the old methods of treatment with grand words, where there is no great benefit in all.
mais je l’ai abregiet selonc mon entention, et ai formez estrumens en diverses manieres.	 However, I have shortened it according to my intention, and formed extracts in various ways.
Je dis que en la gilbositeit que vient au pis devant, nen a engien ne santeit;	 I say that in the swelling that comes on the pubis, there is neither remedy nor health.
